# hep-th [[Back]](#toc)

### [1] [Coarse graining from within: Wilson-Fisher universality on $S^3$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04085)
*Alfio M. Bonanno,Renata Ferrero,Giovanni Oglialoro*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种在弯曲时空背景上不依赖动量壳（momentum shells）的协变重整化群（renormalization group, RG）方法，通过引入内禀谱截断（intrinsic spectral cutoff）并用协变拉普拉斯算子（covariant Laplacian）对模式排序，在S³标量场上实现了无动量（momentum-free）的RG流，验证了Wilson-Fisher普适性（Wilson-Fisher universality）在紧致光谱下的成立。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准的Wilson重整化群（Wilsonian renormalization）通常在动量空间（momentum space）中表述，但在弯曲时空背景（curved backgrounds）上，动量壳（momentum shells）缺乏不变意义，因此需要一种不依赖于动量框架的协变重整化方案。

Method: 用内禀谱截断（intrinsic spectral cutoff）替代动量壳，通过协变拉普拉斯算子（covariant Laplacian）对模式排序，并以系统大小（以RG单位表示）设定截断分辨率。在S³上的标量场中实现了无动量的协变RG流，其迹为球谐函数（spherical harmonics）的精确求和。

Result: 当球面相对于粗粒化尺度（coarse-graining scale）足够大时，标准平空间RG流被恢复。紧致谱RG流在不依赖动量壳的情况下实现了Wilson-Fisher普适性：相互作用的固定点（interacting fixed point）在有限分辨率下存在，具有一个相关方向（relevant direction），且平滑趋近平空间对应物，临界指数（critical exponents）仅受紧致光谱微弱影响。

Conclusion: 所提出的协变谱截断方法为弯曲时空上的重整化群提供了一种自然且内在的框架，在保持Wilson-Fisher普适性的同时，避免了动量壳概念在弯曲背景下的不变性问题。

Abstract: Wilsonian renormalization is usually formulated in momentum space, but on curved backgrounds momentum shells have no invariant meaning. We replace them by an intrinsic spectral cutoff, ordering modes by the covariant Laplacian and setting the cutoff resolution by the system size in renormalization group (RG) units. For a scalar field on $S^3$, this yields a covariant, momentum-free RG flow whose trace is an exact sum over spherical harmonics. The standard flat-space flow is recovered when the sphere is large compared with the coarse-graining scale. As a nontrivial test, the compact spectral flow realizes Wilson-Fisher universality without momentum shells: the interacting fixed point survives at finite resolution, has one relevant direction, and approaches its flat-space counterpart smoothly, with critical exponents only weakly affected by the compact spectrum.

</details>


### [2] [The Awada-Gibbons-Shaw Algebra in de Sitter Space and SUSY Breaking](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04318)
*T. Banks*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文从Awada-Gibbons-Shaw局部超对称代数（local supersymmetry algebra）的形变出发，重新推导了宇宙学超对称破缺关系（Cosmological Supersymmetry Breaking Relation）$m_{3/2} = \frac{C}{\sqrt{R_{dS} L_P}}$。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有宇宙学超对称破缺关系的推导可能依赖于特定的假设或框架，本文旨在通过另一种途径——即通过形变（deformation）Awada-Gibbons-Shaw局部超对称代数——来重新推导该关系，从而提供更坚实的理论依据或新视角。

Method: 通过对Awada-Gibbons-Shaw局部超对称代数（local supersymmetry algebra）进行形变（deformation），在形变后的代数框架下重新推导超对称破缺关系。

Result: 成功从形变后的Awada-Gibbons-Shaw代数重新导出了宇宙学超对称破缺关系 $m_{3/2} = \frac{C}{\sqrt{R_{dS} L_P}}$，其中 $m_{3/2}$ 是引力微子质量（gravitino mass），$R_{dS}$ 是de Sitter时空的曲率半径，$L_P$ 是普朗克长度（Planck length），$C$ 是常数。

Conclusion: 该工作通过代数形变的方法为宇宙学超对称破缺关系提供了新的推导路径，有助于加深对de Sitter时空（de Sitter spacetime）中超对称破缺机制的理解。

Abstract: We rederive the Cosmological Supersymmetry Breaking Relation $m_{3/2} = \frac{C}{\sqrt{R_{dS} L_P}}$ from a deformation of the Awada-Gibbons-Shaw local supersymmetry algebra.

</details>


### [3] [Multi-entropy in random tensor networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04470)
*Miao Hu,Simon Lin,Ion Nechita*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了随机张量网络（Random Tensor Network, RTN）态中Rényi多体熵（Rényi multi-entropies）在大键维极限下的评估问题。证明了对于Rényi指数n=2且任意子体数q，多体熵由网络中的最小多路切割（minimal multiway cuts）决定；对于n>2的整数情形，则通过反例表明最小多路切割猜想一般不成立，并讨论了在RTN与全息对偶（holography）中的应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随机张量网络态是理解全息对偶中多体纠缠结构（multipartite entanglement structures）的重要工具，但此前关于多体Rényi熵的精确刻画尚不完整，尤其是其与网络几何中最小多路切割的关系尚未被严格证明或反驳。

Method: 采用解析方法，在大键维极限下对Rényi多体熵进行严格分析，分别处理Rényi指数n=2和整数n>2的情形。对于n=2，利用最小多路切割理论证明多体熵由最小切割决定，并在退化情形下通过相容切割族（compatible families of minimal cuts）刻画全体最小化子集；对于n>2，构造具体反例（包括单个随机张量和等距铺砌网络）否定最小多路切割猜想的普遍性。

Result: 对于n=2，Rényi多体熵精确由网络中的最小多路切割决定，这自然将双体纠缠（bipartite entanglement）的最小切割描述推广到任意多子体系。对于整数n>2，通过显式反例证明最小多路切割猜想一般不成立。

Conclusion: 该结果为随机张量网络与全息对偶中的多体纠缠结构提供了新的理解：n=2情形下多体熵与网络几何切割的对应关系得以严格建立，而n>2情形则揭示了更高阶Rényi熵的复杂性，表明其不能简单由最小多路切割描述。

Abstract: We study the evaluation of Rényi multi-entropies $S^{(q)}_n$ in Random Tensor Network (RTN) states in the large bond-dimension limit. For the case of Rényi index $n=2$ and arbitrary number of parties $q$, we prove that that multi-entropies are determined by minimal multiway cuts through the network. When the minimal multiway cut is degenerate, we characterize the full minimizer set via compatible families of minimal cuts and give a criterion for all minimizers to come from ordinary cut partitions. For $n=2$, this gives a natural generalization of the minimal cut description of bipartite entanglement to multipartite systems with arbitrarily many parties. For the case of integer $n>2$, we show that the minimal multiway cut conjecture is in general \emph{not true} by providing explicit counter examples for both the single random tensor and for the network built from isometric tilings. We discuss the implication for our results on the multipartite entanglement structures in RTN and holography.

</details>


### [4] [On Cosmologies and Vacua Driven by Tension and Curvatures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04542)
*J. Mourad,A. Sagnotti*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了非超对称弦理论（non-supersymmetric strings）中指数势（exponential potentials）在具有最大对称空间（maximally symmetric spaces）的宇宙学模型中的动力学效应，空间与内部空间的曲率由整数对 $k$ 和 $k'$（$=\pm 1$）标记。通过精确解、特殊解、标度渐近分析与数值检验，对平坦空间切片情形下的通用动力学进行了半定量刻画。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非超对称弦理论中自然出现的指数势对宇宙学演化有重要影响，但其在具有弯曲空间切片（curved spatial slices）和内部空间的一般情形下的动力学行为尚缺乏系统性分类与定量理解。本文旨在填补这一空白。

Method: 采用解析与数值相结合的方法：首先求解单一效应主导时的精确解（exact solutions），再分析两种或多种效应可比拟时的特殊解（special solutions），并辅以标度渐近（scaling asymptotics）分析与数值检验，从而对平坦空间切片这一物理最相关情形下的通用动力学给出半定量图像。

Result: 对所有宇宙学解按其奇点结构（singularity structure）与渐近行为（asymptotic behavior）进行了分类，并在平坦空间切片情形下给出了通用动力学的半定量描述。

Conclusion: 本文为理解非超对称弦论宇宙学中指数势与空间/内部曲率耦合的动力学提供了一个系统的分类框架与半定量分析基础。

Abstract: We investigate the effects of the exponential potentials typical of non-supersymmetric strings in cosmologies whose spatial and internal slices are maximally symmetric spaces with curvatures labeled by a pair of integers $k$ and $k'$ ($=\pm 1$). We classify the solutions according to their singularity structure and asymptotic behavior and present a semi-quantitative picture of the generic dynamics in the physically most relevant cases with flat spatial slices. The analysis relies on exact solutions emerging when one of the effects dominates, special solutions arising when two or more effects are comparable, scaling asymptotics, and some numerical tests.

</details>


### [5] [Resonance transformations for the $(2,2p+1)$ minimal string via $x-y$ swap: a proof of Artemev's conjecture](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04854)
*Kornelis Dekinga,Sergey Shadrin,Erik Verlinde*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文证明了一个关于$(2,2p+1)$极小弦理论（minimal string）中共振变换（resonance transformations）与拓扑递归理论（topological recursion）中$x-y$交换之间关联的近期猜想（Artemev猜想）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 验证并证明Artemev提出的猜想，该猜想将$(2,2p+1)$极小弦理论中的共振变换与拓扑递归理论中的$x-y$交换联系起来，从而揭示两个理论框架之间的深层结构关联。

Method: 采用严格的数学证明方法，针对Artemev猜想中涉及的共振变换与拓扑递归中的$x-y$交换关系进行形式化推导与证明。

Result: 成功证明了Artemev猜想，确认了$(2,2p+1)$极小弦理论的共振变换与拓扑递归理论的$x-y$交换之间的等价性。

Conclusion: 该证明为极小弦理论与拓扑递归理论之间的数学联系提供了严格基础，进一步深化了对这两个领域内在结构的理解。

Abstract: This paper contains a proof of a recent conjecture of Artemev that connected the resonance transformations for the $(2,2p+1)$ minimal string to the $x-y$ swap in the theory of topological recursion.

</details>


### [6] [$\text{AdS}_D\times I$ solutions in axio-dilaton gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04933)
*Giuseppe Dibitetto,Nicolò Petri*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了在非超对称 AdS_D × I 背景下的引力-轴子-胀子理论，通过将运动方程重整为自治动力系统，分析了不动点、稳定性以及解析解，并推广至 IIB 和 massive IIA 超引力情形。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索非超对称 AdS_D × I 解在引力-轴子-胀子（axio-dilaton）框架下的存在性与稳定性，填补超对称情形之外的理论空白，并为高维超引力（如 IIB 和 massive IIA）中的新背景提供统一描述。

Method: 将运动方程重写为一阶自治动力系统（first order autonomous dynamical system），通过不动点分析（fixed point analysis）研究解的稳定性条件，并针对任意维度 D 寻找特殊解析解类别。

Result: 发现了几类适用于任意维度 D 的解析解，包括类型 IIB 超引力中的 AdS_9 × I 背景；同时通过数值流（numerical flows）分析了 massive IIA 超引力情形下的解行为。

Conclusion: 非超对称 AdS_D × I 解在 runaway 势和指数耦合条件下存在丰富的物理结构，动力系统方法为统一理解高维超引力中的这类背景提供了有效工具。

Abstract: We study non-supersymmetric $\mathrm{AdS}_D\times I$ solutions in the context of $(D+1)$ dimensional gravity coupled to an axio-dilaton with arbitrary runaway potential for the dilaton and arbitrary exponential coupling of the dilaton to the axion kinetic energy. We analyze the equations of motion, reformulate them in terms of a first order autonomous dynamical system, and discuss the set of fixed points, their physical interpretation and their stability conditions. We find a few special classes of analytic solutions for arbitrary $D$, including $\mathrm{AdS}_9\times I$ backgrounds in type IIB supergravity. We conclude by discussing the properties of numerical flows including the massive IIA supergravity case.

</details>


### [7] [Off-shell Thermodynamics and Kinetics of Holographic CFTs Dual to Charged AdS Black Holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04949)
*Debabrata Sahu,Chandrasekhar Bhamidipati*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文利用离壳自由能（off-shell free energy）研究全息共形场论（holographic CFT）的热力学与相结构，分析了三种系综下的相图，并通过随机的福克-普朗克方程（Fokker-Planck equation）计算了相变动力学，包括首次通过时间分布及其随电荷与中心电荷的变化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在全息对偶（holographic duality）框架下，带电反德西特黑洞（charged AdS black holes）对应的边界共形场论具有丰富的热力学与相结构，现有研究对相变动力学的定量描述尚不充分。本文旨在通过离壳自由能方法，系统分析不同系综下的相图及其随机动力学行为。

Method: 采用离壳自由能来描述全息共形场论的三个系综：固定 (Q̃, V, C)、(Φ̃, V, C) 和 (Q̃, V, μ)。利用基于离壳自由能的随机描述研究相变，导出依赖于系综的福克-普朗克方程，并计算首次通过时间分布（first-passage-time distribution），包括平均首次通过时间及其涨落。

Result: 给出了三个系综对应的相图。在固定 (Q̃, V, C) 和 (Φ̃, V, C) 系综中，揭示了竞争态之间的相变动力学。计算了随温度变化的平均首次通过时间及其涨落，并分析了相结构与动力学如何依赖电荷 Q̃ 和中心电荷 C。

Conclusion: 离壳自由能方法有效刻画了全息CFT在不同系综下的相结构与相变动力学，且该动力学显著依赖于系综参数（如电荷与中心电荷），为理解全息对偶中的非平衡过程提供了定量框架。

Abstract: We study the thermodynamics and phase structure of holographic conformal field theories dual to spherically symmetric charged AdS black holes using an off-shell free energy. We consider three ensembles of the dual CFT with fixed: $(\tilde Q,{\cal V},C)$, $(\tilde Φ,{\cal V},C)$, and $(\tilde Q,{\cal V},μ)$ and present their corresponding phase diagrams. For the fixed $(\tilde Q,{\cal V},C)$ and $(\tilde Φ,{\cal V},C)$ ensembles, we study the transitions between competing states using a stochastic description on the various phases given by off-shell free energy. This is described by an ensemble dependent Fokker-Planck equation, allowing us to compute the first-passage-time distribution, including the mean first passage time and its fluctuations over a range of temperatures. We also examine how the phase structure and the associated kinetics depend on the electric charge $\tilde Q$ and the central charge $C$.

</details>


### [8] [Thermal effective action for the $O(N)$ vector model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05059)
*Lorenzo Mauro,Alessandro Vichi*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文在三维大N极限下，计算了带有非零角向扭曲（angular twist）的临界O(N)矢量模型（critical O(N) vector model）热有效作用量（thermal effective action）的前导系数，并通过球面扭曲配分函数和一般弱弯曲背景上的路径积分两种独立方法验证了结果的一致性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了从热有效作用量中提取共形场论（conformal field theory, CFT）的通用数据，如卡西米尔能（Casimir energy）和对于卡鲁扎-克莱因规范场（Kaluza-Klein gauge field）的响应，需要精确计算热有效作用量的前导系数。

Method: 采用两种独立计算方法：一是在高温极限下计算二维球面（two-sphere）上的扭曲配分函数（twisted partition function）；二是直接在一般弱弯曲背景（generic weakly curved background）上进行路径积分（path-integral）计算。

Result: 两种方法给出的热有效作用量前导系数结果一致，这为热有效作用量框架提供了非平凡的自洽性验证。

Conclusion: 本文确认了在三维大N极限下，带有角向扭曲的临界O(N)矢量模型的热有效作用量框架是自洽的，其前导系数可以通过高温和弯曲背景两种途径统一确定。

Abstract: We compute the leading coefficients of the thermal effective action for the critical O(N) vector model in three dimensions, in the large-N limit in presence of non vanishing angular twist. At high temperature, the partition function on a product of a two-dimensional spatial manifold and a thermal circle admits a Kaluza-Klein reduction to a local effective action on the spatial slice, whose coefficients encode universal CFT data such as the Casimir energy and the response to a Kaluza-Klein gauge field. We determine these coefficients through two independent computations: an evaluation of the twisted partition function on the two-sphere in the high-temperature limit, and a direct path-integral computation on a generic weakly curved background. The two methods yield consistent results, providing a non-trivial check of the thermal effective action framework.

</details>


### [9] [Fermionic Kaluza-Klein mode mixing in braneworlds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05086)
*Chun-E Fu,Wen-Xuan Ma*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究厚膜世界模型中费米子Kaluza-Klein（KK）模式在一般背景扰动下的混合现象。通过精确奇异值分解（SVD）处理非对角化的Dirac质量矩阵，揭示了微扰导致的KK模式间耦合、宇称依赖的混合类型以及概率密度极化效应，使得原本“暗”的KK模式变得可见。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统厚膜世界模型假定静态孤立背景，其KK本征态构成正交基，但一般背景扰动沿额外维度具有非平凡空间分布，导致不同KK能级之间产生非零重叠积分（overlap integrals），从而在4D有效质量矩阵中引入非对角耦合，使得原有本征态不再精确成立。因此，需要严格处理这种模式混合并揭示其对物理本征态的影响。

Method: 在原始KK本征态基下展开完整的相互作用Dirac算符，将空间变化导致的非对角耦合纳入4D有效质量矩阵。采用精确的奇异值分解（Singular Value Decomposition, SVD）处理全非对角化的Dirac质量矩阵，以严格保持5D手征结构（chiral structure）并解析出真实的物理本征态。

Result: 模式混合引入小而结构化的质量本征值修正；奇宇称（parity-odd）扰动算子仅引发同宇称混合，保持宏观Z2空间对称性；偶宇称（parity-even）算子则引发跨宇称混合，破坏Z2对称性，导致KK概率密度严重空间极化。极化效应将波函数向膜（brane）方向推移，使概率零点变为非零值，从而照亮了原本“暗”的KK模式。

Conclusion: 背景扰动会破坏KK模式的正交性，必须通过SVD而非简单的微扰展开才能正确刻画5D手征结构。不同的宇称扰动算子对Z2对称性产生不同影响：奇宇称算子保持对称性，偶宇称算子破坏对称性并引发显著的物理后果。该工作为理解额外维度中模式混合与宇称破缺现象提供了精确分析框架。

Abstract: We investigate fermionic Kaluza-Klein (KK) mode mixing in thick braneworld models subjected to generic background perturbations. Conventionally, isolated static backgrounds are completely described by a Schroedinger-like formulation, which yields an unperturbed orthogonal basis of KK eigenstates. However, generic perturbations possess a non-trivial spatial profile along the extra dimension. When the full interacting Dirac operator is expanded in this original basis, the spatial variation inevitably yields non-vanishing overlap integrals between distinct KK levels, thereby inducing off-diagonal couplings in the 4D effective mass matrix. Consequently, the original eigenstates are no longer exact physical eigenmodes of the perturbed system. To rigorously preserve the underlying 5D chiral structure and resolve the true physical states, we employ an exact Singular Value Decomposition (SVD) of the full, off-diagonal Dirac mass matrix. Our exact analysis reveals that this mode mixing introduces small but highly structured corrections to the mass eigenvalues. Specifically, parity-odd perturbation operators strictly induce same-parity mixing that preserves the macroscopic Z2 spatial symmetry, whereas parity-even operators trigger cross-parity mixing that shatters the Z2 symmetry, resulting in severe spatial polarization of the KK probability densities. Phenomenologically, such polarization shifts the wave functions toward the brane, turning probability zeros into non-zero values, which directly illuminates previously "dark" KK modes.

</details>


### [10] [Thermal Positivity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05136)
*Clifford Cheung,Rachel A. Rosen*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文证明，在弱耦合相对论无质量玻色子的微扰理论中，洛伦兹不变性（Lorentz invariance）和幺正性（unitarity）对热力学量施加严格的符号约束：所有形如T^{2D-4+4k}（k>0）的低温相互作用修正项（如压强、熵密度和比热）都严格为正。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 作者希望从微观量子场论的基本原理——洛伦兹不变性和幺正性——出发，推导出热力学量在低温下必须满足的普适符号条件，从而为有效场论（effective field theory）的热力学行为提供严格的理论约束。

Method: 将热真空图（thermal vacuum diagram）与前向散射振幅（forward scattering amplitude）建立联系，从而在微扰相对论无质量玻色子理论中导出一系列关于有限温度（finite-temperature）可观测量符号条件的不等式族。

Result: 证明了在D维时空（spacetime dimension）中，所有形如T^{2D-4+4k}（k>0）的低温相互作用修正项（来自压强，等价于负自由能密度）都严格为正；这些正性条件（positivity conditions）同样适用于熵密度和比热中的对应项。

Conclusion: 研究结果适用于任何无长程力（long-range force）且源于弱耦合紫外完备（ultraviolet completion）的有效场论；在此类理论中，更高阶圈图（higher-loop）和更高重数热图（higher-multiplicity thermal diagram）在参数上被压制，因此符号条件具有广泛的适用性。

Abstract: We argue that Lorentz invariance and unitarity impose sharp constraints on thermodynamic quantities. By relating thermal vacuum diagrams to forward scattering amplitudes, we derive an infinite family of sign conditions on finite-temperature observables in perturbative theories of relativistic massless bosons. In particular, we prove that all low-temperature corrections from interactions to the pressure, or equivalently the negative free energy density, of the form T^{2D-4+4k} with k>0 in D spacetime dimensions, are strictly positive. These positivity conditions are inherited by analogous terms in the entropy density and specific heat. Our results apply to any effective field theory that is free of long-range forces and descends from a weakly coupled ultraviolet completion, in which case higher-loop and higher-multiplicity thermal diagrams are parametrically subleading.

</details>


### [11] [Emergent Closed Universes in Symmetric Orbifold CFTs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04575)
*Akihiro Miyata,Keigo Horikoshi,Hiromasa Tajima,Tomonori Ugajin*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文在大N对称轨道CFT（symmetric orbifold CFT）中识别出与全息对偶对应的闭宇宙扇区（closed universe sectors），表明在大N极限下未加规范约束时Hilbert空间存在指数大的超选择扇区（superselection sectors），其中最大熵扇区表现出闭宇宙Hilbert空间的特征，包括不可区分性和超有限type II₁ von Neumann代数；施加S_N规范约束后，物理Hilbert空间维度仅呈多项式增长，重现了虫洞引力路径积分（gravitational path integral）的定性行为，并解释了Hartle-Hawking半经典近似失效的原因以及外部观测者耦合后如何恢复主导鞍点近似。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究大N对称轨道CFT中是否存在与全息对偶（holographic dual）对应的闭宇宙扇区，并理解其Hilbert空间结构、超选择扇区（superselection sectors）及代数性质，以建立CFT与引力路径积分计算（gravitational path integral）之间的对应关系。

Method: 从种子理论（seed theory）的有限维低能子空间出发构造张量积态（tensor product states），分析大N极限下Hilbert空间的分解结构；施加S_N轨道规范约束（orbifold gauge constraint），比较规范约束前后的状态空间维度变化，并利用von Neumann代数分类工具表征扇区性质。

Result: 未加规范约束时，超选择扇区具有指数大的维度，最大熵扇区（maximally entropic sector）主导未规范Hilbert空间，该扇区中纯态在简单关联函数层面与混合态不可区分，关联算子代数为超有限type II₁ von Neumann代数（hyperfinite type II₁ von Neumann algebra）；施加S_N规范约束后，大N极限下物理Hilbert空间维度仅多项式增长，每个超选择扇区退化为单维。

Conclusion: 所得结果重现了虫洞引力路径积分（gravitational path integral）的定性行为；Hartle-Hawking半经典近似（Hartle-Hawking semiclassical approximation）在未耦合外部观测者时无法复现CFT结果，但将CFT自由度与外部观测者自由度耦合后，引力路径积分的主导鞍点近似可被重建。

Abstract: We identify closed universe sectors in large $N$ symmetric orbifold CFTs with holographic duals. Starting from tensor product states built out of a finite dimensional low energy subspace of the seed theory, we show that the large $N$ Hilbert space decomposes into superselection sectors labeled by occupation number distributions. Before imposing the orbifold gauge constraint, these sectors have exponentially large dimensions, and the maximally entropic sector dominates the ungauged Hilbert space. We argue that this sector exhibits several characteristic features expected of a closed universe Hilbert space: pure states become indistinguishable from a mixed state at the level of simple correlation functions, and the associated operator algebra is naturally a hyperfinite type II$_1$ von Neumann algebra. We then impose the $S_N$ gauge constraint. The large gauge redundancy drastically reduces the number of independent states. In particular, in the large $N$ limit, the dimension of the physical Hilbert space grows only polynomially with $N$. Consequently, each superselection sector after imposing the constraint is one dimensional in this limit. This reproduces the qualitative behavior suggested by gravitational path integral calculations with wormholes. We then show why, in this setup, the Hartle-Hawking type semiclassical approximation for the dominant closed universe fails to reproduce the CFT results. Nevertheless, the dominant saddle point approximation for gravitational path integral calculation is reconstructed once the CFT degrees of freedom are coupled to external observer degrees of freedom.

</details>


### [12] [Chiral Transport in Metric-Affine Geometries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04841)
*Miguel A. Vazquez-Mozo*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了平衡态手征费米子流体在背景Weyl型非度量性（nonmetricity）下的反常输运现象，通过形式降维分析（descent analysis）和递推技巧（transgression techniques）推导了轴矢流（axial-vector current）的本构关系，发现了由流体涡度（vorticity）和Weyl磁场（Weyl magnetic field）驱动的非度量性介导的手征分离效应（chiral separation effect）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索平衡态费米子流体在手征耦合（chiral coupling）背景非度量性下的反常输运行为，特别是非度量性如何影响手征分离效应等输运现象。

Method: 采用形式降维分析（descent analysis）将非度量性张量（nonmetricity tensor）对反常多项式（anomaly polynomial）的依赖编码为Weyl不变的四形式（Weyl invariant four-form）；利用递推技巧（transgression techniques）从平衡态配分函数（equilibrium partition function）中导出轴矢流的本构关系（constitutive relation）。

Result: 发现存在由流体涡度和Weyl磁场驱动的非度量性介导的手征分离效应；还讨论了文献中提出的费米子物质与度规-仿射几何（metric-affine geometries）的第二种非最小耦合（nonminimal coupling）。

Conclusion: 非度量性可以在平衡态手征费米子流体中诱导新的反常输运现象，为理解广义引力理论框架下的量子反常输运提供了理论依据。

Abstract: Anomalous transport in equilibrium fermionic fluids chirally coupled to background Weyl-type nonmetricity is studied. A formal descent analysis is carried out in which the dependence of the anomaly polynomial on the nonmetricity tensor is encoded in a Weyl invariant four-form. The constitutive relation of the axial-vector current is evaluated from the equilibrium partition function obtained using transgression techniques, showing the existence of nonmetricity-mediated chiral separation effects driven by the fluid's vorticity and the Weyl magnetic field. A second nonminimal coupling of fermionic matter to metric-affine geometries proposed in the literature is also discussed.

</details>

### [13] [Controlled Chemical Signaling between Enzymatic Nanomotors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04138)
*Shuqin Chen,Giorgio Lovato,Oriol Jutglar Soler,Daniel Sánchez-deAlcázar,Ramin Golestanian,Samuel Sánchez*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过一种酶促纳米马达（enzymatic nanomotor）系统，实验验证了两群纳米马达之间基于非互易性泳动响应（non-reciprocal phoretic response）的化学通信，其中主群产生H2O2作为扩散信号吸引次群，并通过实验与理论结合揭示了多种集体响应行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实现纳米马达之间的化学通信是构建类生物集体功能系统的关键目标，但长期受限于化学信号传播及接收响应的实验验证困难，本研究旨在突破这一瓶颈。

Method: 构建了一种由葡萄糖响应型纳米马达（主群）和过氧化氢酶驱动纳米马达（次群）组成的双群体系统；主群沿葡萄糖梯度迁移并释放H2O2作为扩散性通信信号，次群则响应此自生化学梯度（chemoattractant）。通过可视化H2O2梯度传播并定量接收纳米马达的时空响应，结合实验与理论分析机制。

Result: 成功可视化并量化了通信信号H2O2梯度的传播过程以及接收纳米马达对化学前沿的时空响应。实验与理论联合分析表明，不同组合的化学吸引/排斥迁移率（chemo-attractive/repulsive mobility）以及底物与产物的消耗/生成催化速率之间的协同作用，导致了系统中多种集体响应行为。

Conclusion: 该工作向可编程合成集体系统迈出一步，拓宽了化学纳米马达的功能，并为未来混合型生物-合成系统开辟了机会。

Abstract: The coordinated interactions between organisms enhance collective functionality, a feature that artificial systems such as enzymatic nanomotors seek to replicate. A key objective, yet still a major challenge, is to achieve chemical communication among nanomotors. Progress has been limited by the difficulties in verifying effective signaling processes, including chemical signal propagation and the response of receiving nanomotors. Here, we address this challenge using an enzymatic nanomotor system that demonstrates communication between two populations through generically non-reciprocal phoretic response. A primary swarm of glucose-responsive nanomotors migrates toward a glucose gradient while producing H2O2 as a diffusible communication signal. This self-generated chemical gradient then acts as a chemoattractant for a secondary swarm of catalase-powered nanomotors. Through carefully designed experiments, we visualize the propagating H2O2 gradient and quantify the spatiotemporal response of the receiver nanomotors to the chemical front. Combined experimental and theoretical analysis has revealed that the synergy between different combinations of chemo-attractive and chemo-repulsive mobilities and catalytic rates of consumption and production of substrates and products gives rise to a wealth of different collective responses in the system. This work represents a step toward programmable synthetic systems at the collective level, broadening the functionality of chemical nanomotors and opening opportunities for future hybrid living-synthetic systems.

</details>


### [14] [Morphogenesis driven by nematic defects in active biological networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04256)
*Silvia Paparini,Giulio G. Giusteri,L. Angela Mihai*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个连续介质框架，将生物组织建模为具有向列序（nematic order）的活性聚合物网络，通过拓扑缺陷（topological defects）驱动应力集中与形态发生（morphogenesis），有限元模拟表明+1缺陷诱导突起形成，-1/2缺陷则稳定结构，可复现水螅再生与发育过程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 细胞形态发生（cellular morphogenesis）——生物组织获得形状与结构的过程——仍是理解模式形成（pattern formation）与细胞组装协调重塑的根本挑战。现有模型难以统一描述向列序、弹性、应力驱动生长与适应性松弛之间的耦合。

Method: 构建连续介质框架，将活体组织建模为活性生物网络（active biological networks），即具有异质性生长与重塑能力的向列聚合物网络（nematic polymer networks）。通过纤维序参量（fiber order parameter）的空间变化捕捉宏观非平衡效应，将形态发生描述为准静态平衡序列，耦合向列序、弹性、应力驱动生长与适应性松弛，并采用有限元模拟（finite element simulations）实现数值求解。

Result: 拓扑缺陷类型控制应力定位与形状演化：+1缺陷驱动突起（protrusion）形成，而-1/2缺陷充当结构稳定剂、生长最小。通过改变初始缺陷配置，可模拟单向再生、触手形成与双向发育等多种形态发生结果。

Conclusion: 该框架成功再现了水螅（Hydra）的再生与发育过程，表明缺陷拓扑（defect topology）是组织形态演化的关键控制因素。

Abstract: Cellular morphogenesis, the process by which biological tissues acquire shape and structure, remains a fundamental challenge in understanding pattern formation and the coordinated remodeling of cellular assemblies. Under appropriate conditions, cytoskeletal filaments can organize into a nematic phase exhibiting partial orientational order. Topological defects within this nematic organization generate localized mechanical stresses that destabilize the tissue and promote deformation and structural rearrangements to relieve internal stresses. We develop a continuum framework that models living tissues as active biological networks represented as nematic polymer networks capable of heterogeneous growth and remodeling. The model captures macroscopic effects through spatial variations in the fiber order parameter which drives the system away from equilibrium. Morphogenesis is described as a sequence of quasi-static equilibrium states governed by the coupling between nematic order, elasticity, stress-driven growth, and adaptive relaxation. Finite element simulations illustrate Hydra regeneration and development when topological defects are prescribed according to the mature organism's expected morphology. The results show that defect topology controls stress localization and shape evolution: $+1$ defects drive protrusion formation, while $-1/2$ defects act as structural stabilizers with minimal growth. By varying the initial defect configuration, we model diverse morphogenetic outcomes, including uniaxial regeneration, tentacle formation, and biaxial development.

</details>


### [15] [Effect of cations on van der Waals interactions between particles in aqueous alkali nitrate electrolytes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04331)
*Micah P. Prange,Jaehun Chun,Gregory K. Schenter,Elias Nakouzi,Yihui Wei,Aurora E. Clark,Kevin M. Rosso,Carolyn I. Pearce*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本研究通过建立基于电子结构计算的介电响应模型，将纯水中范德华相互作用的Lifshitz理论推广至任意浓度的碱金属硝酸盐溶液，并计算了金红石、勃姆石和氧化铝纳米颗粒在不同盐浓度下的哈梅克常数。结果表明，钠、钾、铷硝酸盐浓度的增加会使哈梅克常数显著升高，而硝酸铯几乎无影响，揭示了中高电解质浓度下范德华相互作用对胶体稳定性的不可忽略作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 电解质对范德华相互作用的影响，尤其是中高浓度下的作用机制尚不完全清楚（incompletely understood），现有研究多针对纯水体系，缺乏对盐溶液体系的系统理论描述。

Method: 基于分子组成的电子结构计算（electronic structure calculations），发展碱金属硝酸盐溶液的介电响应模型（dielectric response model），将纯水中的Lifshitz理论推广至任意浓度碱金属硝酸盐溶液，进而计算Hamaker常数（Hamaker constant）随盐浓度的变化。

Result: 钠、钾、铷硝酸盐溶液浓度的增加会使Hamaker常数相比纯水显著增大，而硝酸铯对Hamaker常数几乎无影响；这一结果与普遍假设（prevailing assumptions）相反。

Conclusion: 中高电解质浓度下，范德华相互作用（van der Waals interaction）对胶体稳定性（colloidal stability）具有不可忽略的作用，这为理解与纳米颗粒相关的涌现现象（emergent phenomena）提供了物理见解。

Abstract: The van der Waals interaction has been extensively studied for colloidal forces and resultant emergent phenomena such as colloidal stability, aggregation, and suspension rheology, but the effect of electrolytes on this interaction, especially at intermediate and high electrolyte concentrations, remains incompletely understood. We have extended the Lifshitz theory for van der Waals interactions in pure water to alkali nitrate solutions at arbitrary concentrations by developing a dielectric response model for alkali nitrate solutions that is based on electronic structure calculations of the molecular constituents. Due to their importance in catalysis, ceramics, and coating technologies, the Hamaker constants for rutile, boehmite, and alumina nanoparticles suspended in alkali nitrate solutions are calculated as a function of salt concentration. Contrary to prevailing assumptions, increasing the concentration of sodium (Na), potassium (K), and rubidium (Rb) nitrate solutions causes appreciable increases of the Hamaker constants relative to pure water instead of decreases, whereas cesium nitrate (CsNO3) has almost no effect on the Hamaker constant. We discussed the influence of the solution molar volume, the polarizability of the dissolved ions, and optical properties of the interacting particles in the context of previously published work. Our study indicates a non-vanishing role of van der Waals interactions on colloidal stability at intermediate and high electrolyte concentrations, leading to physical insights on emergent phenomena associated with nanoparticles.

</details>


### [16] [Vibrational model of entropy in dense two-dimensional fluids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04533)
*Sergey Khrapak*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文将三维稠密流体中原子动力学的振动范式推广到二维（2D）流体，用于描述其过剩熵（excess entropy），并通过多种二维系统（如单组分等离子体、偶极粒子流体和Yukawa流体）验证了该模型的准确性和实用性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 三维稠密流体中基于原子振动的范式已成功用于理解流体的输运和热力学性质，但二维（2D）流体中过剩熵（excess entropy）的描述尚缺乏类似的振动模型推广，因此本文旨在弥补这一空白。

Method: 将三维稠密流体的原子振动范式（vibrational paradigm）进行推广，构建适用于二维流体的振动模型，并通过简单实用（simple practical implementation）的实现方式计算过剩熵。模型在多个二维系统中进行验证，包括具有库仑（Coulomb）和对数（logarithmic）相互作用的单组分等离子体、偶极粒子（dipole particles）二维流体以及二维Yukawa流体。

Result: 该振动模型在多个二维流体系统中均能提供准确（accurate）的过剩熵计算结果，涵盖单组分等离子体（含库仑和对数相互作用）、偶极粒子流体和Yukawa流体等不同相互作用类型的体系。

Conclusion: 二维流体的振动模型能够有效描述过剩熵，论文还简要讨论了该模型的适用性限制（applicability limits）、与三维流体的关联、与其他二维现象的关系以及潜在的实际应用前景。

Abstract: A vibrational paradigm of atomic dynamic in dense fluids is known to provide useful insight on the transport and thermodynamic properties of fluids in three dimensions. In this paper, a vibrational model is generalized to describe the excess entropy of two-dimensional (2D) fluids. A simple practical implementation of this model is demonstrated to deliver accurate results for various systems, such as one-component plasmas with Coulomb and logarithmic interactions, a 2D fluid of dipole particles, and a 2D Yukawa fluid. The applicability limits, relevance to three-dimensional fluids, relations to other 2D phenomena, and potential practical applications are briefly discussed.

</details>


### [17] [Contact-network organization and motion statistics in shear-thickening suspensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04605)
*Michel Orsi,Rahul Pandare,Brolin Adu-Poku,Bulbul Chakraborty,Jeffrey F. Morris*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 通过润滑流离散元方法（LF-DEM）模拟，研究致密剪切增稠悬浮液中接触网络组织如何影响颗粒运动。二维和三维模拟均表明，摩擦接触数、渗流（percolation）与刚性团簇涨落增强的区域与平移速度关联增长区域一致，刚性团簇平动而周围非刚性颗粒承担更多局部速度梯度，旋转运动则提供互补视角，揭示了连接性、刚性与速度关联是剪切增稠及接近剪切堵塞（shear jamming）过程中约束性集体运动的相关但不同的标志。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究剪切增稠悬浮液中接触网络组织如何影响颗粒运动，揭示连接性、刚性与速度关联之间的关系，以及它们作为剪切增稠和剪切堵塞过程中集体运动约束的不同标志。

Method: 使用润滑流离散元方法（LF-DEM，lubricated-flow discrete-element-method）进行模拟；在二维双分散单层系统中通过$(3,3)$卵石游戏算法辨识刚性团簇，并辅以三维模拟验证旋转速度统计的定性相似性。

Result: 在应力-固相分数状态图中，摩擦接触数$k \ge 3$渗流（percolation）与刚性团簇涨落均在平移速度关联增长区域增强；刚性团簇平移相干，非刚性颗粒则承担不成比例的速度梯度；旋转运动方面，非仿射角速度分布展宽，近接触旋转反关联增强，刚性与非刚性颗粒呈现不同的统计特征。

Conclusion: 连接性（connectivity）、刚性（rigidity）与速度关联（velocity correlations）是剪切增稠及接近剪切堵塞（shear jamming）过程中约束性集体运动的不同但相关的标志。

Abstract: We use lubricated-flow discrete-element-method (LF-DEM) simulations to examine how contact-network organization shapes particle motion in dense shear-thickening suspensions. The primary system studied is a two-dimensional bidisperse monolayer where rigid clusters are identified by the $(3,3)$ pebble game; three-dimensional simulations are shown to have qualitatively similar rotational velocity statistics. Across the stress--solid-fraction state diagram, frictional contact number, $k\ge 3$ percolation, and rigid-cluster fluctuations all strengthen in the same region where translational velocity correlations grow, consistent with rigid clusters translating coherently while the surrounding non-rigid particles accommodate a disproportionate share of the local velocity gradient. Rotational motion provides a complementary view: non-affine angular-velocity distributions broaden, near-contact rotations become increasingly anti-correlated, and rigid and non-rigid particles carry distinct statistics. Connectivity, rigidity, and velocity correlations are related but distinct signatures of the constrained collective motion that accompanies shear-thickening and the approach to shear jamming.

</details>


### [18] [Functional trends and rheological evaluation of polyurethane microcapsules in dermato-cosmetic applications](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04622)
*Sharadwata Pan,Andreas Wierschem,Natalie Germann,Thomas Becker*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文是一篇综述，系统梳理了聚氨酯基微胶囊（polyurethane-based microcapsules）在皮肤美容应用（dermato-cosmetic applications）中的最新进展（2017年至今），重点探讨了其作为活性成分靶向递送（targeted delivery）载体的潜力，并强调了流变学（rheology）研究严重不足的问题，最后提出了以绿色原料、领域优化和流变表征为核心的可持续发展路径。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 作者采用综述方法，聚焦2017年至今的最新趋势与进展，对聚氨酯基微胶囊在皮肤美容应用中的文献进行检索、筛选和整合；并基于当前前沿进展，对流变学研究的必要性进行批判性分析，识别亟需关注的目标领域。

Result: 发现近年来聚氨酯作为微胶囊壁材（capsule wall/shell component）的研究虽有增长，但记录不连续；聚氨酯基微胶囊的流变学研究严重缺乏，机械行为理解不足；绿色原材料（green raw materials）的引入和面向客户的应用优化尚未充分实现。

Conclusion: 应通过引入绿色原材料、推进领域优化与客户导向的应用、以及采用新型流变表征程序（novel rheological characterization procedures）深入理解微胶囊的力学行为，从而为聚氨酯基微胶囊在皮肤美容领域开辟一条稳健且可持续的发展道路。

Abstract: To date, natural and synthetic polymer-based microcapsules have been used extensively in various dermato-cosmetic applications, with an emphasis on the targeted delivery of active ingredients, including therapeutic and aesthetic interventions. Although numerous polymer candidates have been comprehensively investigated, polyurethane based microcapsules have received comparatively minor attention, despite possessing a multitude of intrinsic benefits. However, in recent years, although there has been an upsurge of studies involving polyurethane, predominantly as a capsule wall or shell component, towards tangible dermato-cosmetic applications, these are only intermittently documented. In the current review, we target this lacuna, explore, and collate only the most contemporary trends and advances (2017-to date) in the field. In addition, despite the significance, and pertaining to the acute deficiency of rheological studies targeting polyurethane-based microcapsules in dermato-cosmetic applications, we critically examine and lay a comprehensive interpretation, based on the current state-of-the-art, inevitability for systematic inquiries, and identification of several target domains that need urgent attention. Finally, we deliberate on the challenges and the impending projections from a diverse outlook. We focus on a steady and more sustainable path forward via incorporation of green raw materials, cumulative domain-optimized and customer-focused applications, and a significantly improved understanding of the microcapsule mechanical behavior via implementation of novel rheological characterization procedures.

### [19] [Tunable supramolecular polymerization from protein charge heterogeneity and architecture](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04766)
*Nynke Marije Hettema,Meng Shen,Frank van Opstal,Emmett Lim,Liedewij Laan*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本研究以酵母蛋白Bem1为模型，结合实验与粗粒化模拟，揭示了电荷极性、蛋白质结构域架构（protein architecture）以及构象柔性（conformational flexibility）如何协同调节多结构域蛋白的超分子聚合（supramolecular polymerization），实现从长纤维到自限制小聚体的尺寸调控。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多结构域蛋白（multidomain proteins）含有柔性非结构化区域，在细胞信号传导中广泛存在，但结构化的相互作用结构域与整体蛋白质架构如何共同调控组装体的尺寸、结构和动力学，这一问题尚不清楚。

Method: 以芽殖酵母蛋白Bem1为模型系统，实验上比较了分离的PB1结构域与全长Bem1的组装行为；理论上发展了最小粗粒化模型（coarse-grained models），将PB1近似为极性5珠结构域（polar 5-bead domain），全长Bem1则增加一颗珠子代表其余区域形成6珠模型。

Result: 分离的PB1结构域形成延伸纤维，而全长Bem1形成显著更短的组装体；5珠模型的纤维长度分布定量遵循可逆Flory类聚合（reversible Flory-like polymerization）理论，且仅在较窄的电荷极性区间内可调；6珠模型在保留相同驱动结构域的条件下使链长分布向更短聚合物偏移，该偏差源于附加非结构化区域带来的空间位阻与几何约束。

Conclusion: 电荷极性、蛋白质架构和构象柔性是可编程的调控旋钮，用于控制超分子聚合；该工作为理解多结构域蛋白如何组装成可调的生物分子结构提供了通用框架。

Abstract: Multidomain proteins with flexible unstructured sequence regions are abundant in cellular signaling. This protein architecture enables self-assembly into supramolecular structures, but how structured interaction domains and overall protein architecture jointly regulate the assembly size, structure and kinetics remains unclear. Here we use the budding yeast protein Bem1 as a model multidomain system to show that supramolecular polymerization can be tuned by charge heterogeneity and protein architecture. We experimentally demonstrate that Bem1's isolated PB1 domain forms extended filaments, whereas full-length Bem1 forms substantially shorter assemblies, indicating that the PB1 domain drives assembly while the remaining protein architecture tunes filament length. To understand these observations, we develop minimal coarse-grained models approximating the PB1 as a polar 5-bead domain and the full-length Bem1 as a 6-bead model with an additional bead representing the remainder of Bem1. The weight distribution of supramolecular filaments assembled by the 5-bead model quantitatively follows reversible Flory-like polymerization theory, which is tunable within a narrow charge polarity regime. In contrast, the 6-bead model shifts chain-length distributions towards shorter polymers despite retaining the same driving domain. We show that this deviation arises from steric and geometric constraints imposed by the appended unstructured regions, where the rotational flexibility between the charge-polar structured domain and the unstructured region emerges as key physical parameter governing self-limited self-assembly. Together, our results establish charge polarity, protein architecture, and conformational flexibility as programmable control knobs for supramolecular polymerization and suggest a general framework for understanding how multidomain proteins assemble into tunable biomolecular structures.

### [20] [Surface Charge Doping for Ion-Pairing Criticality in Confined Electrolytes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04791)
*Na Shen,Yabei Wu,Wenqing Zhang*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该论文通过广义德拜-休克尔-比耶鲁姆（Debye-Hückel-Bjerrum）理论及布朗动力学模拟，揭示了弱表面电荷如何通过掺杂可移动反离子来调控准二维电解质中离子配对、临界温度和扩散机制，从而将表面电荷识别为纳米流体约束中的热力学掺杂场。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 介电约束（dielectric confinement）在准二维电解质中会增强库仑关联并促进电荷中性狭缝中的比耶鲁姆配对（Bjerrum pairing），但此前研究未考虑弱表面电荷对此类系统的影响。

Method: 采用广义德拜-休克尔-比耶鲁姆理论（generalized Debye-Hückel-Bjerrum theory）进行热力学分析，并结合布朗动力学模拟（Brownian-dynamics simulations）验证扩散行为。

Result: 弱表面电荷通过可移动反离子维持有限屏蔽下限，使微观配对与宏观离子性解耦，并将配对驱动的临界温度（critical temperature）移至更低值；临界温度抑制可坍塌为一个标度扰动变量；低本征盐密度下壁电荷减慢面内扩散，高密度下扩散惩罚减弱。

Conclusion: 表面电荷充当热力学掺杂场，能够同时调控纳米流体约束中关联离子稳定性与扩散机制。

Abstract: Dielectric confinement strengthens Coulomb correlations in quasi-two-dimensional electrolytes and can promote Bjerrum pairing in charge-neutral slits. Here we use a generalized Debye-Huckel-Bjerrum theory to show that weak surface charge changes this picture by stoichiometrically doping the slit with mobile counterions. These counterions maintain a finite screening floor, decouple microscopic pairing from macroscopic ionicity, and shift association-driven criticality to lower temperatures. The critical-temperature suppression collapses onto a single scaled perturbation variable, revealing how surface charge and dielectric confinement jointly control charged nanofluidic slits. Brownian-dynamics tests further show that the same counterions are not always fully bulk-like diffusive: at low intrinsic salt density, explicit wall charge slows in-plane diffusion, whereas at higher intrinsic density the wall-induced diffusion penalty decreases and the mobile-counterion description becomes dynamically accurate. These results identify surface charge as a thermodynamic doping field that tunes both correlated ionic stability and the diffusion mechanism in nanofluidic confinement.

</details>

### [21] [Delta-pulse solution in Zener viscoelastic model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04024)
*Andrea Mentrelli,Juan Luis Gonzalez-Santander,Francesco Mainardi*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文基于Zener模型推导了半无限均匀线性粘弹性介质中δ-脉冲（冲击波）传播的积分表示解，并通过最陡下降路径（SDP）方法进行独立计算验证，证明了两种方法在数值上的一致性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在粘弹性（viscoelastic）介质中，脉冲波传播问题的解析解具有重要意义，但Zener模型下的闭合形式积分表示尚未被充分推导。本文旨在填补这一空白，并探索无需显式拉普拉斯逆变换（inverse Laplace transform）的替代计算方法。

Method: 从Bromwich积分表示出发，通过解析反演Laplace变换获得闭合形式积分表示，结果以第一类修正Bessel函数（modified Bessel function of the first kind）和半整数阶Macdonald函数（Macdonald function）表达；同时推导了与Bromwich积分相位函数相关的最陡下降路径（steepest descent path, SDP），将SDP表示为复变量虚部的六次多项式的零点轨迹。

Result: 积分表示解在适当极限下可退化到已知的Maxwell模型解。两种方法（闭合积分表示与SDP方法）在多个模型参数数值比较下吻合良好。

Conclusion: 积分表示为解的结构提供了分析性洞察；最陡下降路径法无需显式Laplace变换反演，在无法获得闭合积分表示的更一般粘弹性问题中可能具有重要应用价值。

Abstract: We derive the integral representation of the solution for the propagation of a delta-pulse (impulsive wave) in a semi-infinite, homogeneous, linear viscoelastic medium governed by the Zener model. Starting from the Bromwich integral representation of the response function, we obtain a closed-form integral representation by analytically inverting the relevant Laplace transforms. The result is expressed in terms of modified Bessel functions of the first kind and Macdonald functions of half-integer order, and is shown to reduce to the known Maxwell model solution in the appropriate limit. As an independent computational approach, we derive the steepest descent path (SDP) associated with the phase function of the Bromwich integral, characterizing its saddle points and showing that the SDP can be expressed explicitly as the zero locus of a sixth-degree polynomial in the imaginary part of the complex variable. The two methods are compared numerically for several values of the model parameters, confirming their agreement. While the integral representation provides analytical insight into the structure of the solution, the steepest descent method requires no explicit inversion of the Laplace transform and may therefore prove especially valuable in more general viscoelastic settings where a closed-form integral representation is not available.

</details>


### [22] [An Elementary Perspective on the Dirac Equation and its Closest Relatives](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04162)
*Rainer Picard,Sascha Trostorff,Marcus Waurick*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文探讨实设定下的狄拉克方程（Dirac equation）与麦克斯韦方程（Maxwell's equation）之间的密切联系。除分析经典狄拉克质量项（Dirac mass term）外，还考察了替代性的马约拉纳质量项（Majorana mass term），并讨论了它们的四元数结构（quaternionic structure）及其推论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 揭示狄拉克方程与麦克斯韦方程在实设定下的深层联系，并澄清不同质量项（狄拉克质量项与马约拉纳质量项）背后的四元数结构，以深化对基本费米子场（fermion field）数学形式的理解。

Method: 在实数域（real setting）中考虑狄拉克方程，通过与麦克斯韦方程对比建立关联。分别对经典狄拉克质量项和马约拉纳质量项进行结构分析，并采用四元数（quaternion）框架统一讨论其代数性质。

Result: 发现狄拉克方程在实数设定下与麦克斯韦方程具有紧密关系；狄拉克质量项与马约拉纳质量项均展现出特定的四元数结构，该结构对场的自由度与对称性有重要影响。

Conclusion: 实数设定下的狄拉克方程与麦克斯韦方程存在内在联系；四元数结构为理解不同质量项（狄拉克质量项与马约拉纳质量项）的代数与物理后果提供了统一视角。

Abstract: We consider the Dirac equation in a real setting to show its close relationship to Maxwell's equation. In addition to analysing the classical Dirac mass term, we also inspect the alternative Majorana mass term and discuss their quaternionic structure and its consequences.

### [23] [Discussion on the Physics Problem of a Boat Crossing a River](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04515)
*Kyle Kou Yuchang,Simon Meng Zimin,Paul Zhang Yixing*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本研究针对非均匀流速下的船舶过河问题，构建了恒定流、线性分布和幂函数分布三种模型，利用向量加法、微积分和拉格朗日乘子法，推导了固定航向角下的船舶空间轨迹解析表达式，并求解了满足对岸边界条件的最优航向角解析解，为内河智能导航系统的路径规划提供了理论支持。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决非均匀流速（non-uniform flow velocity）条件下船舶过河问题，填补现有模型在复杂流速分布场景下缺乏解析解的不足，为内河智能导航系统提供理论支撑。

Method: 构建三种流速分布模型：恒定流（Model 1）、线性分布（Model 2）和偶次幂函数分布（Model 3，通过参数 n 可调）。采用向量加法（vector addition）结合微积分（calculus）和微分方程（differential equation）推导船舶空间轨迹的解析表达式；针对最短时间控制问题，引入拉格朗日乘子法（Lagrange multiplier method）构建约束优化模型，求解满足正对岸边界条件的最优航向角解析解。

Result: 推导了固定航向角下船舶空间轨迹的解析表达式，并得到了最短时间控制问题中满足对岸边界条件的最优航向角（optimal heading angle）解析解。

Conclusion: 研究成果为内河船舶智能导航系统（intelligent navigation system）的路径规划提供了理论支持；所提出的多模型分析框架（multi-model analysis framework）能够有效模拟真实河流中的复杂流速分布场景。

Abstract: This study addresses the boat river-crossing problem under non-uniform flow velocities by constructing three models: constant flow (Model 1), linear distribution (Model 2), and even-power function distribution (Model 3, adjustable via parameter n ). By using the vector addition, combined with the solutions of calculus and differential equations, the analytical expression of the ship's spatial trajectory under a fixed heading angle relative to the water flow is derived. For the shortest-time control problem, the Lagrange multiplier method is introduced to construct a constrained optimization model, and the analytical solution of the optimal heading angle that satisfies the boundary condition of reaching the direct opposite bank is solved. The research results provide theoretical support for the path planning of inland ship intelligent navigation systems, and the proposed multi-model analysis framework can effectively simulate the complex flow velocity distribution scenarios of real rivers.

### [24] [On the Conicality of Causally Simple, Future Cohesive Spacetimes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04643)
*Claudio F. Paganini*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明，对于维数 1+N（N≥2）的时空，因果简单（causally simple）且未来凝聚（future cohesive）的时空满足锥性（conicality）条件；该条件无法仅由与闵可夫斯基空间同伦（homotopy）或全局双曲性（global hyperbolicity）保证，但 TIP 时空（即观察者的类时过去）作为该类时空的特例如期满足该性质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 锥性（conicality）概念由 [2403.00916] 提出，用以刻画时空中有穷集合的联合未来能否通过其光锥结构唯一确定生成子集（generating subset）。已有工作证明闵可夫斯基时空（Minkowski spacetime）在维数 1+N, N≥2 时满足锥性，并猜想该性质在更一般情形下成立。本文旨在检验该猜想，并确定锥性成立所需的更精确的时空条件。

Method: 作者采用反例论证与结构判定相结合的方法。首先构造反例，表明与闵可夫斯基空间同伦（homotopy）或全局双曲性（global hyperbolicity）各自均不足以保障锥性。随后通过引入因果简单性（causal simplicity）与未来凝聚性（future cohesiveness）等更强的因果结构条件，证明在维数 1+N（N≥2）下这类时空满足锥性。

Result: 得到两个核心结果：第一，与闵可夫斯基空间同伦和全局双曲性各自都不是锥性的充分条件；第二，因果简单且未来凝聚的时空（暗含强因果性）在维数 1+N（N≥2）时满足锥性。TIP 时空（即观察者的类时过去）是这类时空的一个特例。

Conclusion: 锥性在比闵可夫斯基时空更广的时空类中成立，但其成立需要比全局双曲性更强的因果条件（因果简单性加未来凝聚性）。该结果与因果建模（causal modeling）的原始动机一致——观察者的过去（past of an observer）是描述实验的自然时空域。

Abstract: The notion of conicality, recently introduced in [2403.00916], captures the extent to which the joint future of a finite set in spacetime uniquely determines the generating subset via its light cone structure. In the same paper it was mentioned that conicality holds for Minkowski spacetime of dimension $1+N$ with $N\geq 2$ and it has been conjectured that this property holds more generally. In this work, we show that neither homotopy with Minkowski space nor global hyperbolicity alone are sufficient for the spacetime to satisfy conicality. We then establish that causally simple, future cohesive spacetimes of dimension $1+N$ with $N\geq 2$ satisfy the condition. This class of spacetimes in particular includes TIP spacetimes, which can be understood as the timelike past of an observer. This is in line with the origin of causal modeling since the past of an observer is the natural domain for the description of experiments.

</details>


### [25] [Maximal Minimal Spacing for Random Points](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04837)
*Fabio Deelan Cunden,Noemi Cuppone,Giovanni Gramegna,Pierpaolo Vivo*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了从直线上N+1个随机点中选取M+1个点以最大化最小间距的问题，等价于将连续间隙最优分组为M个块并最大化最小块和。作者推导了最优间距的精确分布恒等式及其渐近行为，并揭示了该问题与阈值重置随机游走（threshold-resetting random walk）之间的等价关系，后者为数值方案提供了基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 从随机点中选取子集以最大化最小间距是一类典型的极大极小（max-min）优化问题，具有广泛的潜在应用背景，但此前缺乏针对一般间隙分布（gap distributions）的精确分布结果。

Method: 将原问题等价转化为将连续间隙最优分组为M个块并最大化最小块和。进一步将其重构为阈值重置随机游走模型：游走以随机增量前进，在超过固定阈值时重置回原点。最优间距超过某值的概率等价于该游走在N步内完成至少M次重置循环的概率，从而以首次通过泛函（first-passage functionals）给出精确表示。

Result: 对于一般间隙分布及所有M ≤ N，推导出最优间距的精确分布恒等式及其渐近行为。基于随机游走映射提出了适用于大N和M情形的数值方案，并通过精确结果验证了其准确性。

Conclusion: 揭示了最大最小间距问题与阈值重置随机游走之间的深层联系，为问题提供了精确的概率论表示和实用的数值求解途径。

Abstract: From $N+1$ random points on a line we wish to select $M+1$ points so as to maximize the minimal spacing between them. We consider an initial configuration with independent and identically distributed spacings. The problem is equivalent to optimally grouping consecutive gaps into $M$ blocks and maximizing the smallest block sum. For general gap distributions, and for all $M\leq N$, we derive exact distributional identities for the optimal spacing and obtain its asymptotic behavior. The problem admits a reformulation in terms of a threshold-resetting random walk. The walk advances by successive random increments and is reset to the origin upon exceeding a fixed threshold. The probability that the optimal spacing exceeds a given value coincides with the probability that the walk completes at least $M$ reset cycles within $N$ steps. This yields an exact representation in terms of first-passage functionals of the walk. The same mapping suggests a numerical scheme for the max-min spacing problem in the regime of large $N$ and $M$, whose accuracy is tested against the exact results obtained here.

</details>

# gr-qc [[Back]](#toc)

### [26] [Lagrangian Extensions of Newtonian Gravity constrained by Solar System tests](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04077)
*Pedro H. Dalprá,Júlio C. Fabris,Hermano Velten,Júnior D. Toniato*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过引入第二动力学标量场（second dynamical scalar field）扩展牛顿引力，基于变引力耦合（variable gravitational coupling）研究推导了完整场方程及弱场近似下的有效后牛顿引力势，并利用诺特维特效应（Nordtvedt effect）和水星近日点进动（perihelion shift）数据对模型自由参数进行了观测约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索牛顿引力的扩展形式，通过广义拉格朗日函数（generalised Lagrangian function）引入第二动力学标量场，以构建超越标准牛顿理论、同时包含相对论效应的引力模型。

Method: 基于变引力耦合的前期研究，推导完整场方程；采用弱场近似（weak-field approximation）得到有效后牛顿引力势（post-Newtonian gravitational potential）；利用密切轨道法（method of osculating orbits）计算双体系统的轨道近心点长期变化（secular variation of the orbital pericenter）。

Result: 得到了包含相对论关键特征的有效后牛顿引力势；导出了N体运动方程，揭示了惯性质量与引力质量之间的差异；利用诺特维特效应数据约束了模型的自由参数；通过水星近日点进动的最新数据获得了另一观测约束。

Conclusion: 所提出的标量场扩展引力模型可通过诺特维特效应和水星近日点进动两类天文观测数据对自由参数施加有效约束，为检验该理论提供了可行的观测途径。文中还讨论了一些理论示例。

Abstract: We explore an extension to Newtonian gravity through a generalised Lagrangian function with the introduction of a second dynamical scalar field. Building on previous research into gravity with variable gravitational coupling, the work derives the complete field equations and applies a weak-field approximation. This leads to an effective post-Newtonian gravitational potential that includes key aspects of relativistic theories. The resulting N-body equations of motion highlight differences among inertial and gravitational masses, which can constrain the theory's free parameter through data from the Nordtvedt effect. By employing the method of osculating orbits for a two-body system, the study calculates the secular variation of the orbital pericenter and aligns this with the latest data on Mercury's perihelion shift, for another observational constraint on the model. Furthermore, a few examples of theories are discussed.

</details>


### [27] [Gravitationally Induced Quantum Decoherence of Macroscopic Objects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04099)
*Hiroki Takeda,Shogo Tomizuka,Takahiro Tanaka*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文从线性引力（linearized gravity）出发，推导了大质量物体在空间叠加态中由引力诱导的量子退相干（gravitationally induced quantum decoherence）的闭时路径影响泛函（closed-time-path influence functional），并在牛顿长程引力下得到退相干函数的解析表达式，发现主导贡献在宽距离范围内呈对数累积，但在现实条件下弱于传统碰撞退相干。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究大质量物体在空间叠加（spatial superposition）下由引力诱导的量子退相干机制，填补对引力退相干过程定量理解的空白。

Method: 从线性引力与系统粒子及环境标量场（environmental scalar field）的耦合出发，推导闭时路径影响泛函；在非相对论准静态（nonrelativistic and quasi-static）近似下，将退相干指数（decoherence exponent）表示为系统应力-能量张量差与环境应力-能量张量关联子经引力子传播子（graviton propagator）修饰后的有效噪声核（effective noise kernel）的双线性泛函。将该框架应用于牛顿长程引力相互作用，并用有限波包（finite wave packets）并经过时空粗粒化（coarse-grained in time and space）的稀薄非相对论气体（dilute nonrelativistic gas）模型计算退相干函数。

Result: 通过受控近似（controlled approximations）得到累积退相干函数（cumulative decoherence function）的解析表达式，发现主导贡献在宽距离范围内呈对数累积（logarithmically accumulated），但在现实条件下弱于传统碰撞退相干（conventional collisional decoherence）。

Conclusion: 引力诱导的量子退相干效应在牛顿长程引力下表现为对数形式累积，但其强度低于常规碰撞退相干，表明在典型实验条件下该效应不易被直接观测到。

Abstract: We formulate the gravitationally induced quantum decoherence of a massive object prepared in a spatial superposition. Starting from linearized gravity coupled to a massive system particle and an environmental scalar field, we derive a closed-time-path influence functional governing the reduced system dynamics. In the nonrelativistic and quasi-static regime, the decoherence exponent can be written as a bilinear functional of the difference of the system stress-energy tensors and an effective noise kernel obtained by dressing the environmental stress-energy tensor correlator with graviton propagators. We then apply this framework to the Newtonian long-range gravitational interaction and evaluate the resulting decoherence function for a dilute nonrelativistic gas modeled by finite wave packets and coarse-grained in time and space. By performing controlled approximations, we obtain analytic expressions for the cumulative decoherence function and show that the dominant contribution is accumulated logarithmically over a broad range of distances, while remaining subdominant to conventional collisional decoherence under realistic conditions.

</details>


### [28] [Remarks on causal decrease, omniscient foliations and null lines in spacetimes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04148)
*Alfredo Bautista*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过构造反例，反驳了此前关于强因果时空（strongly causal spacetime）中不存在未来零线（future null line）的断言，并引入“因果递减”（causally decreasing）的新假设，放宽了因果性要求，同时在广义 Robertson-Walker（GRW）时空中给出了确保该假设成立的充分条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 此前文献曾断言，在具有紧叶空间（compact leaf space）的过去全知类时叶状结构（past-omniscient timelike foliation）的强因果时空中，不存在未来零线。本文旨在对该断言提出反例，并探讨在何种条件下该结论仍然成立。

Method: 首先构造一个反例，证明在强因果时空中若仅由过去全知类时叶状结构且叶空间紧致，未来零线仍可能存在。随后引入“因果递减”这一关于定义叶状结构的类时向量场的新假设，证明在该假设下时空的因果性条件可放宽至区分性（distinguishing）水平。若缺少该假设，则需更严格的全局双曲性（global hyperbolicity）等条件。最后，针对广义 Robertson-Walker（GRW）时空，推导其尺度函数（scale function）的充分条件，使得自然类时向量场满足因果递减性。

Result: （1）存在反例表明，在紧叶空间的过去全知类时叶状结构强因果时空中，未来零线仍可能出现；（2）在因果递减假设下，仅需区分性（distinguishing）即可排除未来零线；（3）若无因果递减假设，需全局双曲性等更强条件；（4）对GRW时空，给出了尺度函数的充分条件以确保因果递减性，从而保证无未来零线。

Conclusion: 本文修正了此前关于未来零线不存在的断言，通过引入因果递减假设，在更弱的因果性条件下恢复了该结论，并为GRW时空提供了可检验的充分条件。这些结果有助于深化对类时叶状结构与因果性之间关系的理解。

Abstract: This work provides a counterexample to the previously asserted non--existence of future null lines in strongly causal spacetimes $(M, \mathbf{g})$ foliated by a past--omniscient timelike foliation $\mathcal{F}$ with a compact leaf space $Q$. We introduce a new hypothesis requiring the timelike vector field that defines $\mathcal{F}$ to be causally decreasing. Under this condition, the causality requirement on $M$ can be relaxed to the distinguishing level. In the absence of this hypothesis, we demonstrate that more restrictive conditions, such as global hyperbolicity, are necessary to ensure the absence of future null lines. Finally, we derive sufficient conditions on the scale function of Generalized Robertson--Walker (GRW) spacetimes to ensure that the natural timelike vector field is causally decreasing, thereby guaranteeing the non--existence of future null lines.

</details>


### [29] [Shape of U: Measuring the Curvature of the Universe with Gravitational Waves](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04216)
*Arindam Sharma,Ish Gupta,Anuradha Gupta*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过Fisher矩阵方法，预测未来引力波观测站（如Cosmic Explorer和Einstein Telescope）利用中等质量双黑洞并合作为“亮警笛”（bright sirens）测量非平坦ΛCDM宇宙学中的空间曲率参数Ωₖ，发现可将1σ不确定性约束至0.029，而多波段观测（LISA、月球引力波天线）及双中子星源约束效果较差，表明该方法可提供独立于传统宇宙学观测的空间曲率探测手段。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的空间曲率测量依赖宇宙微波背景辐射（cosmic microwave background）或超新星（supernovae）等观测，存在系统性偏差，因此需要独立的探测手段。引力波标准警笛（standard sirens）无需外部校准即可测量距离，结合电磁对应体（electromagnetic counterpart）提供的红移测量，有望为空间曲率提供全新约束。

Method: 选取类似GW231123的中等质量双黑洞并合（intermediate-mass binary black hole mergers）作为亮警笛源，假设其在活动星系核（active galactic nucleus）盘中可产生电磁对应体从而获得红移信息。采用Fisher矩阵预测（Fisher matrix forecasts），评估由两个Cosmic Explorer探测器与Einstein Telescope组成的探测网络对Ωₖ的约束能力，并进一步分析加入LISA或月球引力波天线（Lunar Gravitational Wave Antenna）进行多波段观测的改进效果。

Result: Cosmic Explorer与Einstein Telescope组成的网络可将Ωₖ的1σ不确定性约束至0.029；多波段加入LISA或月球引力波天线对约束提高不显著；双中子星（binary neutron stars）作为亮警笛源只能将Ωₖ约束至0.055，精度较差。

Conclusion: 未来下一代引力波探测器观测亮警笛源（中等质量双黑洞与双中子星并合）能够为空间曲率提供独立且信息丰富的约束，且其系统误差来源有别于其他宇宙学观测，具有重要的互补价值。

Abstract: Gravitational waves (GWs) from compact binary mergers are standard sirens that can measure distances across the Universe without external calibrators. When an electromagnetic counterpart enables an independent redshift measurement, such "bright sirens" can be used to probe the expansion history of the Universe and constrain cosmological models. In this work, we investigate the ability of future GW observatories to measure the spatial curvature parameter, $Ω_{\rm k}$, in a non-flat $Λ$CDM cosmology. We focus on intermediate-mass binary black hole mergers (with masses similar to GW231123) as bright siren sources, motivated by their detectability to high redshifts with next-generation ground-based detectors and by the possibility that mergers in active galactic nucleus disks may produce electromagnetic counterparts. Using Fisher matrix forecasts, we find that a network consisting of two Cosmic Explorer detectors and Einstein Telescope can constrain $Ω_{\rm k}$ to a $1σ$ uncertainty of $0.029$ with these bright sirens. We further show that multiband observations with LISA or the Lunar Gravitational Wave Antenna do not significantly improve these cosmological constraints, because the additional signal-to-noise ratios accumulated in their bands are modest. Further, a population of binary neutron stars as bright sirens provides substantially broader constraints on $Ω_{\rm k}$, with $1σ$ error of $0.055$. Our results show that bright intermediate-mass binary black hole and binary neutron star mergers observed with next-generation GW detectors together can provide an independent and informative probe of spatial curvature, with systematics distinct from those of other cosmological observations.

</details>


### [30] [Real Part Emergence in Purely Imaginary Quasinormal Modes in Perturbed de Sitter Braneworlds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04424)
*Hai-Long Jia,Wen-Di Guo,Yun-Tao Gu,Yu-Xiao Liu*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了厚德西特膜（thick de Sitter brane）上引力扰动谱的稳定性，发现原本为纯虚拟准正规频率（quasinormal frequencies）的模态在引入扰动后变为复频率模式，并产生可观测的瞬时振荡信号，可能影响从引力信号中提取膜上宇宙学常数（cosmological constant）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 对于具有无限额外维的膜世界（braneworlds），其特征谱的稳定性分析是理解其动力学性质的关键。本文旨在探究厚德西特膜中引力扰动谱的稳定性。

Method: 通过在厚德西特膜上引入扰动，分析引力扰动谱的模态变化，并采用时域信号拟合方法，比较中间阶段瞬时振荡信号与首个新诱导准正规模式的频率一致性。

Result: 原本纯虚的准正规频率在引入扰动后产生非零实部，变为复频率模式；时域信号中间阶段出现瞬时振荡特征，其拟合频率与首个新诱导准正规模式一致，而晚期波形仍由零模（zero mode）主导。

Conclusion: 扰动诱导的振荡在早期信号中更易观测，可能影响从引力信号中提取膜上宇宙学常数的过程。

Abstract: For braneworlds with infinite extra dimensions, an analysis of the stability of the characteristic spectrum is essential for understanding their dynamical properties. In this study, we investigate the stability of the gravitational perturbation spectrum in a thick de Sitter brane. Unlike the flat brane case, the de Sitter brane features purely imaginary quasinormal frequencies, corresponding to time-domain signals that decay without oscillation. Our results demonstrate that, upon introducing perturbations on the brane, the originally purely imaginary modes develop a nonvanishing real part that depends on the perturbation parameters, thereby becoming complex-frequency modes with both real and imaginary components. In the time domain, this behavior manifests as transient oscillatory signatures in the intermediate stage of the signal, whose fitted frequencies are consistent with those of the first newly induced quasinormal mode, while the late-time waveform remains dominated by the zero mode. As early-time signals are more readily observable, such perturbation-induced oscillations are more likely to be detectable and may have an impact on the extraction of the cosmological constant on the brane from gravitational signals.

</details>


### [31] [Fast gravitational waveform models for quasi-circular coalescences of neutron star--black hole binaries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04810)
*Felip A. Ramis Vidal,Adrian Abac,Marta Colleoni,Tim Dietrich,Pierre Mourier,Alejandra Gonzalez,Ivan Markin,Anna Puecher*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出了前两个包含高阶模态（higher-order modes）的频域引力波模型——IMRPhenomXHM_NSBH 和 SEOBNRv5HM_ROM_NRTidalv3_NSBH，用于描述准圆形、自旋对齐的中子星—黑洞（NSBH）双星系统；同时还给出了考虑自旋进动（spin precession）的扩展模型 IMRPhenomXPHM_NSBH。模型基于 NRTidalv3 的高阶模态扩展和数值相对论（NR）校准的振幅模型，在参数估计和模拟信号分析中优于前代模型，并与 GWTC-3 和 GWTC-4 目录中的真实事件结果一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有频域引力波模型对中子星—黑洞（NSBH）双星系统的描述多局限于主导四极矩（dominant quadrupole）模态，缺乏对高阶模态（higher-order modes）和潮汐效应（tidal effects）的精确建模，限制了引力波参数估计的精度。

Method: 基于 NRTidalv3 模型的高阶模态扩展，构建了包含潮汐效应的相位和振幅模型；并利用数值相对论（NR）模拟结果对振幅模型进行专门校准。在自旋进动（spin-precessing）情形下，进一步扩展得到 IMRPhenomXPHM_NSBH。

Result: 新模型与数值相对论（NR）模拟及其他现有模型相比，在性能与有效性上表现更优。对模拟信号的参数估计显示出明显改进；对 GWTC-3 和 GWTC-4 目录中的真实事件进行分析，结果与文献一致。

Conclusion: 提出的 IM RPhenomXHM_NSBH、SEOBNRv5HM_ROM_NRTidalv3_NSBH 及 IMRPhenomXPHM_NSBH 模型，首次实现了包含高阶模态（higher-order modes）和潮汐效应（tidal effects）的 NSBH 频域建模，显著提升了参数估计性能。

Abstract: We present IMRPhenomXHM_NSBH and SEOBNRv5HM_ROM_NRTidalv3_NSBH, the first two frequency-domain models for gravitational-wave signals from quasi-circular, aligned-spin neutron star--black hole (NSBH) binaries including higher-order modes beyond the dominant quadrupole. We also present IMRPhenomXPHM_NSBH, an extension of the former model to the spin-precessing case. These models incorporate tidal effects in the gravitational-wave phasing and amplitude using a higher-mode extension of the NRTidalv3 model as well as dedicated amplitude models calibrated to numerical relativity (NR) simulations of NSBH mergers. We test the performance and validity of the new models by comparing them to NR simulations and other existing models for these systems. Finally, we perform parameter estimation studies. The new models show clear improvements over their predecessors in analyses of simulated signals, while yielding results consistent with the literature when applied to real events from the GWTC-3 and GWTC-4 catalogs.

</details>


### [32] [Constraining Cosmological Parameters From Statistical Superluminal Effects Without a Distance Ladder](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04873)
*Hichem Guergouri,Omar Nemoul,Jamal Mimouni*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文采用统计方法研究膨胀平坦FLRW宇宙中光源的表观超光速运动（apparent superluminal motion），通过将发射时刻的共动距离（comoving distance）显式纳入宇宙学效应，推导出表观角速度的概率密度函数（PDF），并证明该分布对宇宙学参数 Ω_{Λ,0} 和 H_0 敏感，进而构建参数约束并提供一种新的宇宙学模型运动学一致性检验（kinematic consistency test）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索表观超光速运动能否作为独立的宇宙学探针，定量评估其统计可观测量对宇宙学参数的敏感性，并解决单一红移观测中参数简并（degeneracy）的问题。

Method: 采用统计方法，在膨胀平坦FLRW宇宙中显式引入发射时刻共动距离以纳入宇宙学效应；基于对光源取向和本征本动速度（intrinsic peculiar velocity）分布的最小假设，推导表观角速度的概率密度函数。

Result: 表观角速度分布及其统计可观测量对宇宙学参数 Ω_{Λ,0} 和 H_0 敏感；通过定义合适的可观测量，可以在 (Ω_{Λ,0}, H_0) 参数空间中构建关联约束，且联合不同红移的测量可有效打破参数简并。

Conclusion: 表观超光速运动可为宇宙学模型提供一种互补的运动学一致性检验（kinematic consistency test）。

Abstract: We employ a statistical approach to study apparent superluminal motion of luminous sources in an expanding flat Friedmann--Lemaître--Robertson--Walker universe, explicitly incorporating cosmological effects through the comoving distance at the emission time. Probability Density Functions (PDFs) of the apparent angular velocity are derived under minimal assumptions regarding source orientations and intrinsic peculiar velocity distributions. We show that the apparent angular velocity distributions and their associated statistical observables are sensitive to cosmological parameters $Ω_{Λ,0}$ and the Hubble parameter $H_0$. Using suitably defined observables, we construct correlated constraints in the $(Ω_{Λ,0}, H_0)$ parameter space and demonstrate that combining measurements at different redshifts effectively breaks the resulting degeneracy. Apparent superluminal motion thus provides a complementary kinematic consistency test for cosmological models.

</details>


### [33] [The geometry of lunar gravitational wave detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04918)
*Jacopo Tissino,Filippo Santoliquido,Francesco Iacovelli,Ulyana Dupletsa,Tito Dal Canton,Matteo Ballelli,Ansh Chopra,Luis Enrique Espinosa Castro,Laura Pezzella,Matteo Schulz,Izumi Takimoto Schmiegelow,Jan Harms*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文针对月球引力波天线（LGWA）计划，证明通过采用随太阳系质心（SSB）共动但原点优化后的参考系，可将采样时间减少一个数量级；并以恒星级质量双黑洞GW250114为例，展示了该几何方法在参数约束精度上的显著提升，验证了探测器轨道运动与信源参数推断之间的解析近似关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LGWA作为月球上的引力波探测器，主要工作于deci-Hertz频段，面临长时信号处理中参考系选择与计算效率之间的矛盾。现有研究尚未系统评估原点位置优化对参数推断与采样时间的联合影响。

Method: 采用与太阳系质心（Solar System barycenter, SSB）共动的参考系，但将其原点选在能最小化定时不确定性的位置；系统性地提出后处理流程以确定太阳系内的最优原点；并探索了除并合时间外的替代时间参数化方案。

Result: 优化后的参考系将采样时间降低一个数量级；替代时间参数化对参数不确定度影响甚微。以GW250114为例，LGWA在其并合前2分钟即可将啁啾质量（chirp mass）测量精度提升至0.0002太阳质量（90%置信度），并约束其天区位置至65平方度（90% HPD区域），约束优于LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA（LVK）探测器，尽管信噪比更低。

Conclusion: 长时引力波信号的推断必须被视为一个几何问题，其中探测器运动、参考系选择和信号演化共同决定参数约束精度与计算效率。Wen和Chen的解析近似在定性上有效，但在某些注入条件下其假设会失效。

Abstract: The Lunar Gravitational Wave Antenna (LGWA) is a planned gravitational wave detector on the Moon, targeting the deci-Hertz band and expected to deliver breakthrough discoveries across several science cases, including the Moon's interior structure and astrophysics. In this work, we show that adopting a frame comoving with the Solar System barycenter (SSB), but with its origin at a location that minimizes timing uncertainty, reduces the sampling time by an order of magnitude. We present a systematic post-processing procedure to identify the optimal origin within the Solar System for any given signal. We explore alternative timing parametrizations beyond the merger time, and find that they have only a minor impact on parameter uncertainties. Using the stellar-mass black hole binary GW250114 as a case study, we illustrate how these geometrical considerations translate into improved parameter constraints. Two minutes before its merger, the LGWA would have measured its chirp mass to a precision of 0.0002 solar masses (90% symmetric) and constrained its sky position to within 65 square degrees (90% HPD area); these constraints are tighter than those obtained by the LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA (LVK) detectors, despite a lower signal-to-noise ratio. We connect our results to an analytical approximation proposed by Wen and Chen, which relates the area spanned by the orbital motion of a detector to its efficacy in constraining the sky position of a source. We verify its qualitative validity for compact binary sources with a series of injections, identifying the regimes in which its underlying assumptions break down. Our results demonstrate that inference for long-duration GW signals with the LGWA must be treated as a geometrical problem, in which detector motion, reference-frame choice, and signal evolution jointly determine both parameter constraints and computational efficiency.

</details>


### [34] [Interior marginally outer trapped surfaces in Hayward black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04988)
*Abbas M. Sherif,Yen-Kheng Lim*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 论文在正则Haward度规（regular Haward metric）中定位了内部类光捕获闭曲面（MOTS）与开曲面（MOTOS），发现了自相交的MOTS对，并揭示了参数b接近临界值时MOTS/MOTOS的分布行为；通过将问题约化至奇异Sturm–Liouville问题，证明了MOTS位置由超几何函数给出，且算子的特征空间是完备、非离散且不连续的。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在正则Haward度规中，参数b存在一个临界（极值）值b_c，该值决定了时空是否拥有视界（horizon）以及拥有内/外视界的结构。为深入理解该度规下内部类光捕获曲面的存在性与分布特征，需系统研究MOTS/MOTOS的几何与谱性质。

Method: 采用正则Haward度规（regular Haward metric），以参数b为控制变量；通过约化问题至奇异Sturm–Liouville问题（singular Sturm–Liouville problem），利用超几何函数（hypergeometric function）求解MOTS的位置；分析算子的特征空间（eigenspace）性质。

Result: 发现了自相交（self-intersecting）的MOTS，它们成对出现；当b接近临界值b_c时，不存在自相交的MOTS/MOTOS，且可通过精细调节b使得内部仅包含近球面（near-spherical）MOTS；在内视界（inner horizon）附近，MOTS位置由超几何函数表达，算子的特征空间是完备（complete）、非离散（not discrete）且不连续（discontinuous）的。

Conclusion: 正则Haward度规中MOTS/MOTOS的分布受参数b的临界值调控，并展现出非平凡的谱结构：特征空间虽完备但非离散且不连续，表明系统的内部几何结构具有复杂的特征值分布与奇异边界行为。

Abstract: We locate interior marginally outer trapped and marginally outer trapped open surfaces (MOTS/MOTOS) in the regular Haward metric with parameter $b$ for which a critical (extremal) value $b=b_c$ demarcates when the spacetime admits no horizon and when it admits inner and outer horizons. We identify self-intersecting MOTS which occur in pairs. For $b$ close to the critical value, there are no self-intersecting MOTS/MOTOS, and one can fine-tune $b$ so that the interior contains only near-spherical MOTS. We also show that in a neighborhood of the inner horizon for certain values of $b$, upon reduction of the problem to a singular Sturm-Liouville problem, the locations of the MOTS are given by hypergeometric functions, the eigenspace of the operator for which is complete, not discrete, and discontinuous.

</details>


### [35] [Self-force calculations with numerical relativity methods](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04998)
*Nils L. Vu,Nami Nishimura,Thomas Osburn,Jonathan E. Thompson,Lawrence E. Kidder,Samuel D. Upton,Barry Wardell*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新的计算方法，用于在 Kerr 时空中进行二阶自引力（self-force）计算，以满足 LISA 任务对极端质量比旋近（EMRI）引力波建模的需求。该方法结合变量分离、零切片、高阶间断伽辽金离散化、自适应网格细化与迭代 Krylov 型线性求解器，在 Kerr 时空中对标量点电荷的自引力实现了指数收敛，计算效率高且代码开源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为即将到来的 LISA 空间任务建模极端质量比旋近（extreme mass-ratio inspirals, EMRI）的引力波波形，需要将引力自引力（gravitational self-force）计算推进到微扰理论的二阶。然而，目前这类计算仅针对 Schwarzschild 时空中的圆轨道这一最简单情形，Kerr 时空中的通用计算尚未实现，这构成了方法上的空白。

Method: 方法融合了数值相对论（numerical relativity）领域的技术：对变量进行 $m$ 模分离（$m$-mode separation）；在视界穿透坐标（horizon-penetrating coordinates）中引入零切片（null "$vtu$" slicing）；使用高阶间断伽辽金离散化（discontinuous Galerkin discretization）和自适应网格细化（adaptive mesh-refinement）求解椭圆型偏微分方程；采用并行化多重网格-施瓦茨预条件（multigrid-Schwarz preconditioning）的迭代 Krylov 型线性求解器。

Result: 该方法在 Kerr 时空中对标量点电荷（scalar point charge）的自引力实现了指数收敛（exponential convergence），适用范围涵盖自旋参数高达 $a=0.998$（索恩极限, Thorne limit）的圆赤道轨道（circular equatorial orbits），以及最内稳定圆轨道（ISCO）附近的正行与逆行轨道。20 个 $m$ 模可在数秒内并行求解。

Conclusion: 该方法可扩展至引力自引力（gravitational self-force）计算和更一般的轨道情形，其代码已在开源数值相对论代码 SpECTRE 中公开，为未来 LISA 任务所需的 EMRI 波形建模提供了可行的计算框架。

Abstract: To model gravitational waveforms from extreme mass-ratio inspirals (EMRIs) for the upcoming LISA space mission, gravitational self-force calculations are needed to second order in perturbation theory. However, to date these calculations have only been attempted for the simplest case of circular orbits in Schwarzschild spacetime. In this work, we present a new computational method aimed at performing generic second-order self-force calculations in Kerr spacetime using methods from the adjacent field of numerical relativity. We perform an $m$-mode separation of variables, add null ("$vtu$") slicing in horizon-penetrating coordinates, and solve the resulting elliptic PDEs using high-order discontinuous Galerkin discretization, adaptive mesh-refinement, and an iterative Krylov-type linear solver with parallelizable multigrid-Schwarz preconditioning. We find that our method achieves exponential convergence for the self-force on a scalar point charge in Kerr spacetime up to spins of $a=0.998$ (Thorne limit) on circular equatorial orbits as close as the ISCO (prograde and retrograde), despite the non-smooth puncture on the grid. We solve for 20 $m$-modes in parallel in a few seconds and retain the flexibility to extend the method to gravitational self-force and more generic orbits in the future. The code to perform these calculations is publicly available in the open-source numerical relativity code SpECTRE.

</details>

Method: 在空间平坦的FLRW（Friedmann-Lemaître-Robertson-Walker）度规下求解含辐射的R²引力宇宙学模型；利用共形度规变换（conformal metric transformation）将模型转化为可积的双场手征宇宙学模型（two-field chiral cosmological model）进行求解。

Conclusion: 含辐射的R²引力模型可解析求解，且辐射可由特定标量场实现，该系统的可积性为研究早期宇宙的动力学行为提供了理论工具。

Abstract: We consider the $R^2$ gravity cosmological model with radiation and find the general solution in the spatially flat FLRW metric. We analyze the possible evolutions of the Hubble parameters in dependence of sign of the radiation energy density. A scalar field with the induced gravity term and the fourth-order monomial potential can play a role of radiation. In this case, the corresponding two-field chiral cosmological model is integrable and its general solution can be found by the conformal metric transformation.We consider the $R^2$ gravity cosmological model with radiation and find the general solution in the spatially flat FLRW metric. We analyze the possible evolutions of the Hubble parameters in dependence of sign of the radiation energy density. A scalar field with the induced gravity term and the fourth-order monomial potential can play a role of radiation. In this case, the corresponding two-field chiral cosmological model is integrable and its general solution can be found by the conformal metric transformation.

### [37] [Hawking Temperatures and Radiation Estimates for Dilaton--de Sitter Black Holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05135)
*Can Ertugay*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文针对Gao–Zhang解中超导dilaton–de Sitter黑洞，系统比较了三种温度定义（标准表面引力温度、Bousso–Hawking归一化温度、两种有效温度）对热力学量的影响，发现温度定义选择可使辐射功率估计相差一到两个数量级。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 荷电标量黑洞（charged dilaton black hole）在正宇宙学常数背景下存在两个Killing视界（Killing horizon），但已有的Gao–Zhang解尚未像Schwarzschild–de Sitter黑洞那样系统比较多种温度定义（temperature prescription）对热力学性质的影响，而缺乏全局热平衡（global thermal equilibrium）使得不同温度定义本身不等价，因此需要填补这一空白。

Method: 选取Gao–Zhang解家族中四维、弦耦合（string-coupling）成员，计算并比较四种温度方案：标准表面引力温度（surface-gravity temperature）、Bousso–Hawking归一化温度（Bousso–Hawking-normalized temperature）、以及基于黑洞视界与宇宙学视界（cosmological horizon）构建的两种有效温度（effective temperature）。

Result: 标量场（dilaton）改变了面积半径（areal radius）、熵（entropy）、光子球条件（photon-sphere condition）和灰体因子（greybody problem），而de Sitter归一化歧义（normalization ambiguity）通过红移因子（redshift factor）的幂次修正辐射估计。在代表性参数下，Bousso–Hawking方案可使Stefan–Boltzmann估计的黑洞辐射功率比未归一化的表面引力方案高出一到两个数量级，而基于熵和（entropy-sum）的有效温度则会压低该估计。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了dilaton–de Sitter黑洞热力学中一个具体的空白区域，并为完整的灰体因子计算（greybody-factor calculation）提供了路线图。

Abstract: Charged dilaton black holes with a positive cosmological constant provide a useful arena in which to test how scalar hair modifies semiclassical physics in a spacetime with two Killing horizons. The Gao--Zhang solution realizes such a geometry in Einstein--Maxwell--dilaton theory by replacing a single Liouville potential, which is insufficient for asymptotically de Sitter boundary conditions, by a three-Liouville dilaton potential. Although the solution and several of its perturbative and optical properties have been studied, its temperature and heat capacity have not been examined through the same range of temperature prescriptions commonly considered for Schwarzschild--de Sitter black holes, where the absence of global thermal equilibrium motivates several inequivalent temperature definitions. We present this temperature-prescription comparison for the four-dimensional, string-coupling member of the Gao--Zhang family. We compare the standard surface-gravity temperature, the Bousso--Hawking-normalized temperature, and two effective temperatures built from the black-hole and cosmological horizons. The dilaton changes the areal radius, entropy, photon-sphere condition, and greybody problem, while the de Sitter normalization ambiguity changes radiation estimates by powers of the redshift factor. For representative parameters, the Bousso--Hawking prescription can enhance a Stefan--Boltzmann estimate of the black-hole power by one to two orders of magnitude relative to the unnormalized surface-gravity prescription, whereas the entropy-sum effective temperature can suppress the same estimate. These results identify a concrete gap in the thermodynamics of dilaton--de Sitter black holes and provide a roadmap for a full greybody-factor calculation.

</details>


### [38] [Mapping the star formation peak with LIGO A# and Next-Generation detectors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05151)
*Divyajyoti,Stephen Fairhurst,Mark Hannam,Mukesh Kumar Singh*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文利用引力波（gravitational waves）观测独立约束恒星形成率密度（SFR density）的红移演化，通过双黑洞并合事件的红移分布反推恒星形成率峰值，并评估了LIGO-A#及下一代探测器（Cosmic Explorer与Einstein Telescope）的测量精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的电磁波段方法测量恒星形成率密度（star formation rate density）依赖于光度转换，受初始质量函数（initial mass function）、尘埃消光等因素影响。引力波可提供一种独立的高红移约束手段。

Method: 采用三种恒星形成种群模型（population model）并结合反时间延迟模型（inverse time-delay model），通过模拟双黑洞并合事件的并合率红移分布，反推恒星形成率峰值。使用升级版LIGO探测器网络（LIGO-A#）及下一代探测器网络（Cosmic Explorer与Einstein Telescope）进行信号模拟和参数约束评估。

Result: 对于一年的观测数据，在并合率峰值红移$z_\text{peak}=1.5$的假设下，LIGO-A#网络可将峰值约束精度控制在$\pm 0.1$；下一代探测器网络（Cosmic Explorer和Einstein Telescope）的精度可达到$\pm 0.02$。

Conclusion: 引力波观测能够有效约束恒星形成率的红移演化，未来探测器网络将极大提升对红移分布峰值的测量精度。

Abstract: Measuring the redshift evolution of star formation rate density is crucial in understanding the origin and evolution of galaxies and large scale structure in the universe. It is currently measured with electromagnetic probes, however, these probes often track luminosity, which is then converted to star formation rate (SFR) depending on various factors such as initial mass function, dust extinction, etc. Gravitational waves provide an independent method to constrain SFR at high redshifts by tracking the redshift evolution obtained from analysis of binary black hole mergers. In this study we explore three population models for star-formation combined with an \textit{inverse} time-delay model and demonstrate that it is possible to obtain bounds on the peak of redshift distribution with a network of upgraded LIGO detectors (such as LIGO-A#). For a year of observation, using simulated signals with a merger rate peak at $z_\text{peak}=1.5$, a network of LIGO detectors at A# sensitivity is able to constrain the peak of merger rate with a precision of $\pm 0.1$. Further, we obtain the results with a next-generation network (of Cosmic Explorer and Einstein Telescope) and conclude that the redshift distribution will be extremely well measured, with a precision of $\pm 0.02$, with future detectors.
