### [39] [High-Order Summation-By-Parts Schemes for First-Order Hyperbolic Systems in Curvilinear Coordinates with Singularities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05155)
*Stamatis Vretinaris,Erik Schnetter*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文针对带有奇异性的曲线坐标系（如球坐标系）中的双曲型系统，提出了一种基于求和-分部积分（SBP）性质的高阶精度、能量稳定的有限差分算子构造方法，并显式构造了最高六阶的算子，通过标量波动方程的算例验证了其优势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在带有坐标奇异性的曲线坐标系（如球坐标系）中求解双曲型系统（hyperbolic systems）时，数值方法的稳定性构建因奇异点的存在而变得复杂，现有方法难以兼顾高阶精度与能量稳定性。

Method: 基于Gundlach等人提出的思路进行扩展，定义了满足求和-分部积分（Summation-by-Parts, SBP）性质的离散梯度（gradient）与散度（divergence）算子；即使在原点存在 $1/r^p$ 坐标奇异性的情况下，算子仍然镜像连续积分-分部（integration-by-parts）原理。算子将网格点直接放置在原点，并给出了最高六阶的显式构造，同时回顾了跨越原点的稳定SBP算子构造方式。

Result: 对所构造的算子进行了精度与谱半径（spectral radii）分析，并通过标量波动方程（scalar wave equation）的演化算例展示了这类算子的优势。

Conclusion: 提出的方法能够在球对称域上构造高阶精度且能量稳定的有限差分算子，有效处理原点处的坐标奇异性，数值算例验证了其可行性与有效性。

Abstract: Formulating stable numerical methods for hyperbolic systems in curvilinear coordinate with singularities, e.g. spherical coordinates, is complicated by the presence of these singularities. We present a method for constructing high-order accurate, energy-stable finite difference operators satisfying the Summation-by-Parts (SBP) property on spherical domains, extending ideas presented by [C. Gundlach, J. M. Martín-García, and D. Garfinkle, CQG 30, 145003 (2013)]. We define discrete gradient and divergence operators that mirror the continuous integration-by-parts principle, even though there is a $1/r^p$ coordinate singularity present at the origin. We explicitly construct such operators up to order six. Our operators place a grid point directly on the origin. We also review how to construct stable SBP operators that straddle the origin. We analyze the accuracy and spectral radii of these operators, and we show example evolutions of the scalar wave equation to demonstrate the advantages of such operators.

</details>

### [40] [Many body localization in Disordered One-Dimensional Fermi-Hubbard Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04948)
*Harmanjeet Kaur,Vinod Ashokan*

Main category: cond-mat.other

TL;DR: 本文通过研究一维费米-哈伯德模型（Fermi-Hubbard model）在无序条件下的非平衡动力学，重点关注多体局域化（many-body localization, MBL）现象。系统初始化为电荷密度波态（charge-density-wave state），通过子晶格不平衡度（sublattice imbalance）和二分纠缠熵（bipartite entanglement entropy）分析时间演化。弱无序下系统表现出快速热化（thermalization），强无序下则出现持久不平衡与慢动力学，表明遍历性（ergodicity）破缺。自旋与电荷通道存在部分解耦，纠缠熵呈现对数增长，揭示了无序与相互作用在动力学中的关键作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究无序一维费米-哈伯德模型中的非平衡动力学，重点关注多体局域化（many-body localization）现象，以理解无序和相互作用对系统遍历性（ergodicity）破缺的协同影响。

Method: 系统初始化为电荷密度波态（charge-density-wave state），通过子晶格不平衡度（sublattice imbalance，分别针对自旋和电荷）以及二分纠缠熵（bipartite entanglement entropy）分析时间演化过程。

Result: 弱无序区间观察到不平衡度快速衰减与纠缠熵快速增长，系统实现有效热化；强无序区间则呈现持久不平衡与慢动力学，标志遍历性（ergodicity）破缺。自旋与电荷通道展现不同的弛豫行为，表明两者存在部分解耦；在相互作用存在时，纠缠熵呈现缓慢的对数增长（logarithmic growth），反映出退相位驱动（dephasing-driven）的多体局域化（many-body localized, MBL）相动力学特征。

Conclusion: 无序与相互作用之间的竞争共同决定了系统的动力学性质，上述结果建立了费米-哈伯德模型中多体局域化（many-body localization）的可靠标志。

Abstract: We investigate the non-equilibrium dynamics of the disordered one-dimensional Fermi-Hubbard model with a focus on many-body localization. The system is initialized in a charge-density-wave-state, and its time evolution is analyzed through sublattice imbalance (spin and charge), and bipartite entanglement entropy. A clear crossover from ergodic to non-ergodic behavior is observed with increasing disorder strength. In the weak disorder regime, rapid decay of imbalance and the fast growth of entanglement indicate efficient thermalization. In contrast, a strong disorder leads to persistent imbalance and slow dynamics, signaling the breakdown of ergodicity. The charge and spin sectors exhibit distinct relaxation behavior, providing evidence for partial decoupling between these degrees of freedom. Furthermore, in the interacting regime, the entanglement entropy shows slow logarithmic growth, reflecting the dephasing-driven dynamics characteristic of the many-body localized phase. These results highlight the interplay between disorder and interactions in determining the dynamical properties of the system and establish robust signatures of many-body localization in the Fermi-Hubbard model.

</details>


### [41] [Effective and Floquet Hamiltonians for High Frequency Driving and Floquet-induced Heating in Quantum Spin Chains](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04976)
*Mayukh Bandyopadhyay,Vinod Ashokan*

Main category: cond-mat.other

TL;DR: 本文通过研究无序周期性驱动量子自旋链的非平衡动力学，分析了相互作用、无序和弗洛凯驱动（Floquet driving）之间的竞争，发现了从热化到弗洛凯多体局域化（Floquet-MBL）的不同动力学区域，并揭示了强无序抑制输运、强驱动频率阻止能量吸收等关键行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索无序周期性驱动量子自旋链中相互作用、无序和弗洛凯驱动之间的竞争机制，以理解系统在弗洛凯多体局域化（Floquet-MBL）区域与热化区域之间的动力学行为。

Method: 以计算基（computational basis）下的乘积态（product state）为初始态，通过约化密度矩阵（reduced density matrix）计算纠缠熵密度（entanglement entropy density），并监测能量吸收，系统性地扫描相互作用强度、横向场、平行场、无序强度W和驱动频率等参数。

Result: 发现了快速退定域化（fast delocalization）与对数纠缠增长（logarithmic entanglement growth）两种截然不同的行为，以及初始态的长久记忆效应，分别对应局域化或预热弗洛凯（prethermal Floquet）区域。强无序抑制输运并导致缓慢纠缠动力学，强驱动频率阻止能量吸收并产生长寿命非平衡态；反之，弱无序或低频驱动则导致退定域化。

Conclusion: 研究结果支持驱动多体系统中存在非平衡相（non-equilibrium phases），为弗洛凯多体局域化与热化之间的转变提供了有力证据。

Abstract: We study the non-equilibrium dynamics of a disordered periodically driven quantum spin chain, with the competition between the interaction, disorder, and Floquet driving being of particular interest. We study dynamics of entanglement entropy, energy absorption to characterize dynamical regimes of the system whether it stays in the Floquet-MBL(many-body localization) region or thermalized region. Starting with a product state in the computational basis, followed by reduced density matrix which in turn gives rise to the entanglement entropy density. With the strength of the interaction, the transverse field, the parallel field, the disorder strength W and the driving frequency, we discover the distinct behaviors of fast delocalization and logarithmic entanglement growth and long-lasting memory of the initial state, indicative of localized or prethermal Floquet regimes. We observe that strong disorder arrests transport and enables slow entanglement dynamics, whereas strong driving frequency arrests energy absorption and creates a long-lived non-equilibrium state. Conversely, weak disorder or low driving frequency leads to delocalization. The outcomes show strong support for non-equilibrium phases in driven many-body systems.

### [42] [The Free Lunch Theorem of Homogenisation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04498)
*Andreas Buchinger,Marianna Porfido,Marcus Waurick*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文证明，Murat 与 Tartar 在 1970 年代提出的乘法型算子 H-收敛（H-convergence）必然蕴含 2018 年引入的非局部 H-收敛（nonlocal H-convergence）。该结果不受空间维数、区域几何或特定散度-旋度引理（div-curl lemma）版本的限制，并将经典理论推广至更一般的高阶微分算子与不同边界条件，同时证实了文献中长期缺乏显式证明的 homogenization 公式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典 H-收敛理论在应用上受限于空间维数、区域几何以及 Hilbert 复形（Hilbert complex）对散度-旋度引理的依赖。本文旨在消除这些限制，并建立经典 H-收敛与非局部 H-收敛之间的蕴含关系，弥补文献中 homogenization 公式缺乏显式证明的空白。

Method: 通过分析乘法型算子的 H-收敛性质，在不依赖特定维数、几何结构或 Hilbert 复形的前提下，证明经典 H-收敛必然导出非局部 H-收敛。进一步将结果推广至具有不同边界条件与阶数的更一般微分算子。

Result: 经典 H-收敛总蕴含非局部 H-收敛，且该结果适用于任意空间维数与一般区域几何。经典理论被成功推广至更一般的微分算子与边界条件。文献中使用的 homogenization 公式被严格证明成立。作为推论，散度形式问题（divergence form problems）中乘法算子的 H-收敛自动意味着另一变分问题（variational problem）的 H-型收敛（H-type convergence）。

Conclusion: 本文统一了经典 H-收敛与非局部 H-收敛两种框架，显著拓宽了 H-收敛理论的适用范围。研究成果为均匀化（homogenization）理论提供了更坚实的数学基础，并揭示了不同变分问题之间收敛性的内在联系。

Abstract: We show that H-convergence for multiplication type operators as envisioned by Murat and Tartar in the 1970's always implies nonlocal H-convergence as introduced in 2018 in Calc.~Var.~PDE 57(6):159. In contrast to earlier findings, the results presented here work for arbitrary space dimensions, are not bound to a certain geometry of the underlying domain, and do not explicitly require an underlying Hilbert complex for the application of any particular version of the div-curl lemma. We extend classical theory and the main results to more general differential operators with different boundary conditions and orders. Furthermore, the present results confirm homogenisation formulas used in the literature of which we failed to find an explicit proof. As a consequence, H-convergence for multiplication operators in divergence form problems will always imply H-type convergence for a different variational problem for free.

</details>


### [43] [Exponential stability for the three-dimensional Navier-Stokes equations on negatively curved manifolds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04407)
*Zhi-Wei Wang,Samuel L. Braunstein*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文将在双曲空间$\HH^3$上建立的不可压缩Navier-Stokes方程指数稳定性定理，推广到具有负截面曲率夹挤和有界几何的完备单连通黎曼3-流形$(M^3, g)$上，证明了小初值下全局温和解的存在性与指数衰减，并解决了曲率非标量、Leray投影不交换及谱隙未知三个关键障碍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将三维不可压缩Navier-Stokes方程在双曲空间上的指数稳定性结果推广到更一般的、具有负曲率夹挤的完备单连通黎曼3-流形，以检验该稳定性结论是否依赖于双曲空间的特殊对称性，并理解几何曲率对流体动力学稳定性机制的影响。

Method: 采用形变拉普拉斯算子(Deformation Laplacian)$Δ_\Def = Δ_B + \Ric$作为黏性算子；针对双曲空间上成立的三个关键结构在一般流形上的失效，分别提出解决方案：(i)利用Ricci扰动$V = \Ric + 2a^2 g$的半负定性，结合Trotter乘积界(diamagnetic inequality)无条件处理半群分解失效；(ii)通过将换位子$[\PP, Δ_\Def]$代数约化为互补投影$(I-\PP)$作用于平移的Ricci自同态，得到与曲率夹挤$b^2 - a^2$成正比的零阶界；(iii)借助McKean定理、diamagnetic不等式和Weitzenböck恒等式确定谱隙。

Result: 在小$L^3$初值条件下，精确系统存在唯一全局温和解，且以Stokes算子谱隙决定的速率指数衰减；Fujita-Kato时间奇异性指数$1/2 - 3/(2p)$与双曲空间情形一致，表明紫外标度障碍是局部的、与几何无关的，根本上由不可消除的时间标度失配驱动。

Conclusion: 指数稳定性定理可以成功地从双曲空间推广到更一般的负曲率夹挤流形，其中曲率夹挤约束的唯一来源是Leray投影与形变拉普拉斯算子的非对易性；紫外标度障碍具有几何无关性，暗示该稳定性结果可能适用于更广泛的弯曲背景流形。

Abstract: We extend the exponential stability theorem for the three-dimensional incompressible Navier-Stokes equations from hyperbolic 3-space $\HH^3$ (established in a companion paper) to complete simply connected Riemannian 3-manifolds $(M^3, g)$ with pinched negative sectional curvature $-b^2 \leq K \leq -a^2 < 0$ and bounded geometry (including a strictly positive injectivity radius). The deformation Laplacian $Δ_\Def = Δ_B + \Ric$ remains the viscous operator, selected by Lagrangian kinematics. We prove that the {exact} system admits a unique global mild solution for small $L^3$ data, with exponential decay at a rate determined by the spectral gap of the Stokes operator. The extension overcomes three obstacles absent on $\HH^3$: (i) the semigroup factorisation $e^{tΔ_\Def} = e^{-2t}e^{tΔ_B}$ fails because $\Ric$ is not a scalar multiple of the metric; (ii) the Leray projector no longer commutes with $Δ_\Def$; (iii) the exact spectral gap is unknown. We resolve (i) unconditionally, without any curvature restriction, by observing that the Ricci perturbation $V = \Ric + 2a^2 g$ is negative semi-definite and applying a Trotter product bound with the diamagnetic inequality. We resolve (ii) by an algebraic reduction of the commutator $[\PP, Δ_\Def]$ to the complementary projector $(I-\PP)$ applied to the shifted Ricci endomorphism, giving a clean zeroth-order bound proportional to the curvature variation $b^2 - a^2$. This is the sole source of a curvature pinching constraint. We resolve (iii) via McKean's theorem, the diamagnetic inequality, and the Weitzenböck identity. The Fujita-Kato temporal singularity exponent $1/2 - 3/(2p)$ is unchanged from the $\HH^3$ case, confirming that the ultraviolet scaling obstruction is local and geometry-independent, driven fundamentally by an unresolvable temporal scaling mismatch.

</details>


### [44] [Phase transitions for the noisy transformer model in arbitrary dimension](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05140)
*Kyunghoo Mun,Matthew Rosenzweig*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文研究了噪声Transformer动力学中与未归一化自注意力（USA）模型相关联的McKean–Vlasov自由能在单位球面上的性质，证明了任意维度 d≥2 下存在尖锐的全局最小化子二分现象：存在唯一的 β_*^{(d)}，使得当 β≤β_*^{(d)} 时均匀密度保持唯一全局最小化子且相变连续，当 β>β_*^{(d)} 时均匀密度不再全局最小化且相变不连续。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在将作者近期在二维情形下的工作（arXiv:2604.16288）推广至任意维度 d≥2，系统研究噪声Transformer动力学中USA模型的McKean–Vlasov自由能在单位球面上的全局最小化子行为与相变性质。

Method: 采用单位球面上的尖锐Beckner–Onofri/对数Hardy-Littlewood-Sobolev（HLS）不等式，结合Funk–Hecke/Bessel系数计算以及二次四次 obstruction 方法进行证明。

Result: 证明了每个维度 d≥2 存在唯一的 β_*^{(d)}，由修正贝塞尔函数（modified Bessel function of the first kind）I_ν 的比值决定。当 0<β≤β_*^{(d)} 时，均匀密度在达到线性稳定阈值 K_#^{(d)}(β) 之前是唯一全局最小化子，相变连续；当 β>β_*^{(d)} 时，均匀密度在 K_#^{(d)}(β) 处不再全局最小化，临界耦合满足 K_c < K_#^{(d)}(β)，相变不连续。

Conclusion: 本文成功将USA模型自由能全局最小化子二分结果从二维推广至任意维度，揭示了连续相变与不连续相变的分界条件，深化了对噪声Transformer动力学中自注意力机制统计行为的理解。

Abstract: We study the McKean--Vlasov free energy on the unit sphere associated with the unnormalized self-attention (USA) model for noisy transformer dynamics. We prove a sharp global-minimizer dichotomy in every dimension $d\ge2$. There is a unique $β_*^{(d)}>0$ such that \begin{equation*}
  \frac{I_{d/2+1}(β_*^{(d)})}{I_{d/2}(β_*^{(d)})}=\frac1d, \end{equation*} where $I_ν$ is the modified Bessel function of the first kind. For $0<β\le β_*^{(d)}$, the uniform density remains the unique global minimizer up to the linear-stability threshold \begin{equation*}
  K_\#^{(d)}(β)=\frac{β^{d/2}}{2^{d/2}Γ(d/2)I_{d/2}(β)}, \end{equation*} and the phase transition is continuous. For $β>β_*^{(d)}$, the uniform density is not globally minimizing at $K_\#^{(d)}(β)$, so the critical coupling satisfies $K_c<K_\#^{(d)}(β)$ and the transition is discontinuous. This result generalizes the authors' recent $d=2$ work arXiv:2604.16288 to arbitrary dimension. The proof uses the sharp Beckner--Onofri/logarithmic Hardy-Littlewood-Sobolev (HLS) inequality on the sphere, together with a Funk--Hecke/Bessel coefficient computation and a degree-two quartic obstruction.

</details>

### [45] [Variational low-energy subspaces for chemically accurate excited states](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05148)
*Clemens Giuliani,Rocco Martinazzo,Giuseppe Carleo,Riccardo Rossi*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出EXIDOS方法，将变分激发态优化重新表述为电子哈密顿量低能子空间上的迭代基态问题，利用非正交斯莱特行列式实现多激发态同时优化，无需显式正交约束或对称性先验知识，并在多个分子体系上达到化学精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高精度电子激发态计算对光化学、光谱学和非绝热分子动力学至关重要，但传统高阶方法计算量随体系增大急剧增长，且需要预先知道目标态的特征或对称性信息，这限制了其自动化与可扩展性。

Method: 将变分激发态优化重新表述为电子哈密顿量（electronic Hamiltonian）低能子空间上的迭代基态问题；将该变分原理应用于非正交斯莱特行列式（non-orthogonal Slater determinants），得到EXIDOS方法；仅需控制状态数和每态的行列式数量，无需显式正交约束或自旋/点群对称性（spin and point-group symmetries）施加。

Result: 在N₂和CO的多个态上达到化学精度；成功处理HCl中的电荷转移态（charge-transfer states）、NH₃中的里德伯态（Rydberg states）、C₂中的双激发（double excitations）与扩展势能曲线（potential-energy curves），以及乙烯中的避免交叉（avoided crossings）和圆锥交叉（conical intersections）。

Conclusion: EXIDOS是一种低标度、全变分（fully variational）的化学精度激发态计算方法，为自动化激发态量子化学提供了新途径。

Abstract: Accurate electronic excited states are essential for photochemistry, spectroscopy and non-adiabatic molecular dynamics, but high-level calculations often scale steeply and require prior knowledge of the target state's character or symmetry. Here we show that variational excited-state optimization can be reformulated as an iterated ground-state-like problem for a low-energy subspace of the electronic Hamiltonian. Applying this variational principle to non-orthogonal Slater determinants leads to EXIDOS, an automatic method for excited state calculations controlled only by the number of states and determinants per state. EXIDOS optimizes multiple excited states simultaneously, without explicit orthogonality constraints or imposed spin and point-group symmetries. Benchmarks against FCI and state-of-the-art quantum chemistry methods show chemical accuracy for a multitude of states in N$_2$ and CO, charge-transfer states in HCl, Rydberg states in NH$_3$, double excitations and extended potential-energy curves in C$_2$, and avoided crossings and conical intersections in ethylene. These results establish EXIDOS as a low-scaling, fully variational route to chemically accurate excited states.

### [46] [Probing pairing symmetries through quasiparticle interference in chiral Bloch bands](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04097)
*Sayan Banerjee,Subrata Mandal,Peter P. Orth,Mathias S. Scheurer*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文为具有手性布洛赫能带（chiral Bloch bands）的超导体提供了准粒子干涉（QPI）理论，揭示了布洛赫态量子几何对干涉图案的关键影响，并展示了如何利用杂质周围的局域谱函数空间依赖性来区分不同的候选配对态（包括零质心动量和有限质心动量配对态），为手性能带材料中QPI图案的解读提供了理论指导。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期实验发现，在范德华（van der Waals）多层体系中，超导电性可以从对称性降低的手性（chiral）正常态中涌现出来。然而，目前缺乏针对具有手性能带的超导体中准粒子干涉（QPI）图案的理论理解，这使得实验上难以区分不同的候选配对态。

Method: 本文构建了一个适用于手性布洛赫能带（chiral Bloch bands）的超导体QPI理论框架，系统分析了布洛赫态的量子几何（quantum geometry）以及博戈留波夫准粒子（Bogoliubov quasiparticles）的量子几何与序参量动量依赖相位之间的相互作用如何影响干涉图案。

Result: 分析表明，即使在正常态中，布洛赫态的非平凡量子几何也会显著影响干涉图案，并诱导出明显的子格（sublattice）依赖性。在超导态中，由于博戈留波夫准粒子的量子几何与序参量的动量依赖相位之间的相互作用，行为变得更加复杂。杂质周围的局域谱函数空间依赖性可用于区分零质心动量（zero center-of-mass momentum）和有限质心动量（finite center-of-mass momentum）的不同候选配对态。

Conclusion: 该工作为解读手性能带材料中的QPI图案提供了理论指导，有助于探测此类系统中丰富的超导配对物理。

Abstract: Recent experiments in van der Waals multi-layer systems have demonstrated that superconductivity can emerge from symmetry-reduced, chiral normal states. We here provide a theory for quasiparticle interference (QPI) of superconductors with chiral Bloch bands. Our analysis reveals how the non-trivial quantum geometry of the Bloch states crucially affects the interference pattern even in the normal state, inducing significant sublattice dependence. In the superconducting state, the behavior becomes more complex due to the interplay of the quantum geometry of the Bogoliubov quasiparticles with the momentum-dependent phase of the order parameter. We reveal how the spatial dependence of the local spectral function around impurities can be used to distinguish between different candidate pairing states, both with zero and finite center-of-mass momentum. Our work thus provides guidance to interpreting QPI patterns in materials with chiral bands, which may be useful when probing the rich physics of pairing in such systems.

### [47] [Antiferromagnetic Quantum Criticality in Infinite-Layer Cuprates Sr1-xNdxCuO2](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04559)
*Bin-Jie Wu,Ze-Xian Deng,Guang-Ran Wei,Xi Zhou,Ji-Hai Zhang,Da-Zhuang Deng,Qun Zhu,Yong Zhong,Can-Li Song,Xu-Cun Ma,Qi-Kun Xue*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文通过臭氧辅助分子束外延法合成了高质量、氧化学计量比精确的无限层铜氧化物薄膜，霍尔输运测量揭示了在临界掺杂量 xc ~ 0.155 处发生的费米面重构，并证明该重构源于反铁磁量子临界性，为电子掺杂铜氧化物中的非常规超导理论提供了纯净的基准平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解量子临界性（quantum criticality）与费米面重构（Fermi surface reconstruction）之间的相互作用，是阐明高温铜氧化物超导体相图的核心问题。电子掺杂T'-结构铜氧化物的研究提示该重构可能源于反铁磁（antiferromagnetic）起源，但顶角氧不稳定性和不可控的氧空位阻碍了定量共识的达成。

Method: 利用臭氧辅助分子束外延（ozone-assisted molecular beam epitaxy）合成了高质量、氧化学计量比（oxygen-stoichiometric）的无限层铜酸盐 Sr1-xNdxCuO2 薄膜，覆盖整个超导穹顶区间；通过霍尔输运（Hall transport）测量追踪载流子类型转变，并采用自旋密度波紧束缚模型（spin-density-wave tight-binding model）对输运演化进行定量建模。

Result: 霍尔输运测量在临界掺杂量 xc ~ 0.155 处观测到尖锐的载流子类型转变，标志着费米面重构的发生。自旋密度波紧束缚模型能够定量重现输运演化，支持该量子相变（quantum phase transition）的反铁磁起源。此外，在强磁场抑制超导后，正常态电阻率在 xc 附近表现出纯净的奇异金属行为（strange metal behavior），该行为持续至 2 K。

Conclusion: 这些发现确立了电子掺杂铜氧化物中一种内在、普遍的反铁磁量子临界性，将结构最简单的无限层铜酸盐定位为非常规超导理论的一个清洁基准平台（clean benchmark platform）。

Abstract: The interplay between quantum criticality and Fermi surface reconstruction is central to elucidating the phase diagram of high-temperature cuprate superconductors. While studies on electron-doped T'-structure cuprates suggest an antiferromagnetic origin of this reconstruction, quantitative consensus has been hindered by apical oxygen instabilities and uncontrolled oxygen vacancies. Here, we overcome these limitations by utilizing ozone-assisted molecular beam epitaxy to synthesize high-quality, oxygen-stoichiometric thin films of infinite-layer cuprate Sr1-xNdxCuO2 across its entire superconducting dome. Hall transport measurements reveal a sharp carrier-type transition signaling a Fermi surface reconstruction at a critical doping xc ~ 0.155. We show that a spin-density-wave tight-binding model quantitatively reproduces the transport evolution, supporting an antiferromagnetic origin of this quantum phase transition. Furthermore, upon suppressing superconductivity with magnetic fields, the normal-state resistivity exhibits a pristine strange metal behavior that persists down to 2 K in the vicinity of xc. Our findings establish an intrinsic, universal antiferromagnetic quantum criticality in electron-doped cuprates, positioning the structurally simplest infinite-layer cuprates as a clean benchmark platform for theories of unconventional superconductivity.

</details>


### [48] [Nodal superconductivity with spin-triplet component in a noncentrosymmetric weakly-correlated metal](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04742)
*Marcel Strohmeier,Andriy Smolyanyuk,Karsten Held,Michael Smidman,Geetha Balakrishnan,Wolfgang Belzig,Elke Scheer,Angelo Di Bernardo*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文通过低温和取向分辨扫描隧道谱（scanning tunneling spectroscopy）实验，在弱关联非中心对称超导体 Nb₁₈Re₈₂ 中证实了反演不对称性（ASOC）本身足以产生可观测的自旋三重态（spin-triplet）分量，混合宇称（mixed-parity）序参量中的三重态振幅可达单重态的一半，为超自旋电子学（superspintronics）提供了一个易制备材料平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非中心对称超导体（noncentrosymmetric superconductors）中，反演对称性破缺导致反演不对称自旋-轨道耦合（ASOC），可能混合单重态（spin-singlet）与三重态（spin-triplet）配对。然而，ASOC 在无强电子关联条件下能否独立产生可测量的三重态分量，是一个核心未决问题。本文旨在通过 Nb₁₈Re₈₂ 这一弱关联体系解决该争议。

Method: 采用低温扫描隧道谱（low-temperature scanning tunneling spectroscopy, LT-STS）技术，测量具有四种不同晶体学取向的 Nb₁₈Re₈₂ 单晶的局域态密度（local density of states, LDOS），并结合对称性约束模型（symmetry-constrained model）对完整的隧道谱数据进行理论分析。

Result: 实验观察到与晶体取向高度相关的显著各向异性（orientation-dependent anisotropy）局域态密度。对称性约束模型表明，这些隧道谱只能由混合宇称序参量（mixed-parity order parameter）解释，其中三重态分量振幅最高可达单重态分量的一半。

Conclusion: ASOC 在无强电子关联时足以产生可观的自旋三重态分量，表明混合宇称超导态可能比此前预期的更为普遍。Nb₁₈Re₈₂ 易于制备成薄膜形式，可成为超自旋电子学器件的实用平台；同时，取向分辨隧道谱学（orientation-resolved tunneling spectroscopy）被确立为探测混合宇称序参量的一般性实验方案。

Abstract: In conventional superconductors, Cooper pairs form in an even-parity spin-singlet state. Noncentrosymmetric superconductors, which lack inversion symmetry, exhibit antisymmetric spin-orbit coupling (ASOC) that can combine even-parity spin-singlet and odd-parity spin-triplet pairs into a mixed-parity order parameter. Spin-triplet components are highly beneficial for superspintronic devices. Whether ASOC alone $-$ without strong electronic correlations $-$ is sufficient to generate a measurable triplet component remains a central open question. Here, we resolve this question in Nb$_{18}$Re$_{82}$ (Nb-Re), a weakly-correlated noncentrosymmetric metal whose superconducting pairing symmetry has been actively debated. Using low-temperature scanning tunneling spectroscopy on single crystals with four distinct crystallographic orientations, find a pronounced orientation-dependent anisotropy in the local density of states. Supported by a symmetry-constrained model, we show that the complete set of tunneling spectra requires a mixed-parity order parameter with the triplet amplitude reaching up to half of the singlet component. These results reconcile the conflicting reports in the literature on Nb-Re and demonstrate that ASOC is sufficient to foster a sizable spin-triplet component even without strong electronic correlations, suggesting that mixed-parity superconducting states may be more widespread than previously assumed. Since Nb-Re can be readily fabricated in thin-film form, these findings position it as an accessible platform for superspintronic devices and establish orientation-resolved tunneling spectroscopy as a general protocol for the detection of mixed-parity order parameters.

### [49] [A unified theory of thin film and bulk bilayer nickelates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04821)
*Jiangfan Wang,Yi-feng Yang*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文提出基于双组分（two-component）图像的统一理论框架，解释了双层镍酸盐（bilayer nickelate）在加压块材和薄膜中观察到的超导电性差异，预测了电子或空穴掺杂下的双超导穹顶（double superconducting domes）结构，并阐明了正常态从费米液体到非费米液体的转变及Kondo散射效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 双层镍酸盐超导体在加压块材和薄膜中展现出相似性与差异性，但目前缺乏统一的理论解释。本文旨在提供一个基于双组分机制的理论框架，以统一解释多个关键实验观测结果。

Method: 基于双组分（two-component）理论框架，考虑强层间超交换耦合（interlayer superexchange coupling）$J$ 的作用，分析 $d_{z^2}$ 和 $d_{x^2-y^2}$ 轨道电子的不同行为，并结合氧空位或化学取代对层间价键（interlayer valence bond）的破坏效应，对实验现象进行统一解释。

Result: 理论预测：强 $J$ 时，在 $d_{z^2}$ 半填充（half filling）附近存在价键态（valence bond state），分隔出电子或空穴掺杂下的两个超导穹顶；弱或中等 $J$ 时，呈现跨越半填充的单穹顶且 $T_c$ 较低。掺杂增加使正常态从费米液体（Fermi liquid）转变为非费米液体（non-Fermi liquid）或弱绝缘行为，在最优 $T_c$ 附近呈现准线性温度依赖散射率（quasi-linear-in-$T$ scattering rate）。破坏层间价键会抑制超导并导致局域Kondo散射（Kondo scattering）。

Conclusion: 该理论成功解释了块材与薄膜中不同的超导转变和正常态行为、$d_{z^2}$ 掺杂效应以及非超导样品中的Kondo效应。作者提出通过掺杂或减弱层间磁耦合可在常压下实现块材超导，并预测电子掺杂可获得更高 $T_c$。

Abstract: The discovery of bilayer nickelate superconductivity in both pressurized bulk and thin films has drawn enormous attention on their similarity and distinction. Here we provide a unified explanation based on the two-component scenario for a number of key experimental observations reported recently. Our theory predicts two superconducting domes upon electron or hole doping, separated by a valence bond state near $d_{z^2}$ half filling for strong interlayer superexchange coupling $J$, and a single dome across half filling with a lower $T_c$ for weak or moderate $J$. Increasing doping drives the normal state from a Fermi liquid to non-Fermi liquid or weak insulating behaviors, with quasi-linear-in-$T$ scattering rate near optimal $T_c$, while breaking the interlayer valence bonds by oxygen vacancies or chemical substitution simultaneously suppresses the superconductivity and causes local Kondo scattering of $d_{x^2-y^2}$ electrons. These explain the different superconducting transitions and normal states in bulk and thin films, the effect of $d_{z^2}$ hole or electron doping, and the Kondo effect in non-superconducting samples. We propose bulk superconductivity at ambient pressure by doping or reducing the interlayer magnetic coupling and predict even higher $T_c$ upon electron doping.

### [50] [Electron-Phonon Coupling and Charge Density Wave Instabilities in W2N and Halogen-Functionalized W2N Monolayers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04953)
*Jakkapat Seeyangnok,Udomsilp Pinsook*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文通过第一性原理计算，研究了单层W2N及其卤素功能化衍生物（W2NF2和W2NCl2）中电荷密度波（CDW）序与超导电性之间的竞争关系，揭示了二者均源于相同的、由软声子驱动的电子-声子耦合（EPC）机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 电荷密度波（charge-density-wave, CDW）序与超导电性之间的相互作用是凝聚态物理（condensed-matter physics）的核心问题之一，因为两者常源自相同的电子-声子耦合（electron-phonon coupling, EPC）机制。本文旨在通过第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations），系统揭示单层W2N家族材料中这一竞争关系的微观起源。

Method: 采用第一性原理计算，对原始单层W2N、卤素功能化W2N（W2NF2和W2NCl2）的结构、电子、振动及超导性质进行系统分析。通过对比不同条件下的声子软化（phonon softening）与声子线宽（phonon linewidth）行为，识别EPC驱动的晶格不稳定性；并通过施加压缩应变（compressive strain）或电子掺杂（electron doping）调控CDW行为。

Result: 原始W2N在M点和K点附近表现出由强EPC驱动的声子不稳定性，表明其具有CDW倾向；引入范德瓦耳斯（van der Waals）相互作用后，W2N成为强耦合超导体（λ = 1.00, Tc = 13.2 K）。氟化（fluorination）削弱了声子软化异常，得到中等耦合超导体（λ = 0.67, Tc = 5.3 K）。W2NCl2重新出现CDW相关声子软化，可通过压缩应变或电子掺杂连续抑制；在-3%压缩应变下，EPC常数从λ = 1.35降至λ = 0.71，产生Tc = 5.8 K的超导态。

Conclusion: 在整个W2N家族中，低能物理行为由M点附近的软化的ZA声子主导，建立了CDW序与超导电性作为同一软声子驱动的EPC机制的竞争表现形式的统一框架（unified framework）。

Abstract: The interplay between charge-density-wave (CDW) order and superconductivity is a central problem in condensed-matter physics because both phenomena often originate from the same electron-phonon coupling (EPC) mechanism. Here, we investigate the structural, electronic, vibrational, and superconducting properties of monolayer W2N and halogen-functionalized W2N (W2NF2 and W2NCl2) using first-principles calculations. Pristine W2N exhibits pronounced phonon instabilities near the M and K points driven by exceptionally strong EPC associated with softened low-frequency phonons. The coincidence between phonon softening and enhanced phonon linewidths identifies the instability as EPC-driven and indicative of a CDW tendency. Inclusion of van der Waals interactions stabilizes the lattice and yields strong-coupling superconductivity with λ = 1.00 and Tc = 13.2 K, while fluorination further weakens the soft-phonon anomaly, resulting in a moderate-coupling superconductor with λ = 0.67 and Tc = 5.3 K. In contrast, W2NCl2 exhibits a re-emergence of CDW-related phonon softening that can be continuously suppressed by compressive strain or electron doping. Under -3% compressive strain, the EPC constant decreases from λ = 1.35 to λ = 0.71, giving rise to superconductivity with Tc = 5.8 K. Across the entire W2N family, the low-energy physics is governed by softened ZA phonons near the M point, establishing a unified framework in which CDW order and superconductivity emerge as competing manifestations of the same soft-phonon-driven EPC mechanism.

### [51] [Triangular Charge-Density Waves (T-CDW) Stabilize Janus Group-VI Chalcogenide Hydrides](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04954)
*Jakkapat Seeyangnok,Udomsilp Pinsook,Graeme J. Ackland*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本研究通过第一性原理计算发现，Janus过渡金属硫族化合物氢化物1T-WSH和1T-WSeH中的三角电荷密度波（T-CDW）并非由费米面嵌套驱动，而是源于强动量依赖的电子-声子耦合（EPC）；T-CDW通过重整化EPC强度来稳定晶格，同时保留超导电性，揭示了1T-MCH家族中CDW与超导共存的普适机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 氢化是增强二维材料中电子-声子耦合（electron-phonon coupling, EPC）和超导电性的有效策略，但过强的EPC会诱发晶格不稳定性，导致电荷密度波（charge-density-wave, CDW）形成和结构相变。本研究旨在探究Janus过渡金属硫族化合物氢化物1T-WSH和1T-WSeH中CDW有序的起源及其对超导电性的影响。

Method: 采用第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）方法，分析了Janus结构1T-WSH和1T-WSeH的电子结构、磁化率（susceptibility）和声子谱（phonon spectrum），以研究CDW有序的性质及其与EPC的关联。

Result: 高对称相在M点出现显著声子软化，驱动体系转变为$2\times2$畸变结构并形成三角电荷密度波（triangular charge-density-wave, T-CDW）图案。该不稳定性源于强动量依赖的EPC而非常规费米面嵌套（Fermi-surface nesting）。T-CDW相中，1T-WSH的EPC常数从$λ=2.04$降至$1.50$，1T-WSeH从$λ=3.94$降至$1.06$；超导转变温度分别预测为$T_c=12.28$ K和$7.75$ K。

Conclusion: 在1T-$MCH$家族（$M=\mathrm{Mo},\mathrm{W}$；$C=\mathrm{S},\mathrm{Se}$）中，T-CDW相的首要作用并非消除超导电性，而是通过EPC重整化（renormalization）稳定晶格。T-CDW相作为一种内在的自稳响应机制，在缓解过强EPC的同时保留了声子介导的超导电性。

Abstract: Hydrogenation is an effective strategy for enhancing electron--phonon coupling (EPC) and superconductivity in two-dimensional materials. However, excessively strong EPC can also induce lattice instabilities, leading to charge-density-wave (CDW) formation and structural phase transitions. Here, using first-principles calculations, we investigate CDW order in the Janus transition-metal chalcogenide hydrides 1T-WSH and 1T-WSeH. We find that the high-symmetry phases exhibit pronounced phonon softening at the M point, driving a transition to a commensurate $2\times2$ distorted structure characterized by an emergent triangular charge-density-wave (T-CDW) pattern. Analysis of the electronic structure, susceptibility, and phonon spectrum reveals that the instability is not driven by conventional Fermi-surface nesting but originates from strong momentum-dependent EPC. The T-CDW transition reconstructs the electronic structure and reduces the density of states at the Fermi level, leading to a substantial renormalization of the EPC strength. Consequently, the electron--phonon coupling constants decrease from $λ=2.04$ to $1.50$ in 1T-WSH and from $λ=3.94$ to $1.06$ in 1T-WSeH, while superconductivity remains robust in CDW phase with predicted transition temperatures of $T_c=12.28$ K and $7.75$ K, respectively. Together with previous results for MoSH and MoSeH, our findings establish a universal mechanism in the 1T-$MCH$ family ($M=\mathrm{Mo},\mathrm{W}$ and $C=\mathrm{S},\mathrm{Se}$), where the primary role of the T-CDW phase is not to eliminate superconductivity but to stabilize the lattice through EPC renormalization. The T-CDW phase therefore acts as an intrinsic self-stabilizing response that relieves excessively strong EPC while preserving phonon-mediated superconductivity.

Abstract: The technology has been developed for synthesizing Nb$_{1-x}$Sc$_x$ films using magnetron co-sputtering from Nb and Sc targets. The material synthesis was accompanied by structural characterization using X-ray diffraction and X-ray reflectometry methods, which enabled the determination of thickness, phase composition and crystal structure. We also analyzed the superconducting properties. The critical temperature $T_c$ was measured for samples with different concentarions of Sc and Nb. The critical current density was as high as 2.5 $\text{ MA/cm}^{2}$. Magnetic measurements were performed with the field oriented perpendicular to the sample. The upper critical field $H_{c2}(0) = 3.2$ T, electron diffusion coefficient $D = 1.1$ $\text{cm}^{2}/s$, and coherence length $ξ_{GL} = 10.1$ nm. The synthesized Nb$_{1-x}$Sc$_x$ intermetallic compound shows promise for various functional cryogenic electronics devices. \keywords{NbSc; superconductor; microbridge}

### [53] [Theory of frozen flux in a narrow uniform superconducting strip after cooling in a small magnetic field](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04961)
*Alexei E. Koshelev*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文理论分析了超导（superconducting）窄长条在垂直小磁场中冷却时残留冻结磁通（residual frozen flux）的形成机制，推导并求解了动力学平衡方程，获得了冻结温度与冻结涡旋密度的定量结果，并揭示了冻结磁场与冷却速率等参数的依赖关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 残留冻结磁通对超导电子器件中的磁通捕获问题具有重要影响。本研究旨在揭示冷却过程中冻结涡旋（vortex）密度的形成机制及其对磁场、温度等参数的依赖规律。

Method: 在温度接近临界温度 $T_c$ 时，基于热激活（thermally-activated）涡旋越过几何能垒（geometrical energy barrier）的跃出与进入过程，建立了动力学平衡方程，并对其进行了推导与求解。

Result: 给出了冻结温度 $T_{\mathrm{fr}}$ 与冻结涡旋密度的定量结果。相对冻结温度 $1-T_{\mathrm{fr}}/T_c$ 超过转变涨落宽度一个大的对数因子，在磁场接近最小磁通排出场时迅速增大，并随冷却速率减小而对数增长。冻结磁通密度表现出极强的磁场依赖性，可用于定义有效磁通排出场（effective flux-expulsion magnetic field）。

Conclusion: 冷却过程中涡旋逃逸率呈指数下降，导致涡旋密度在磁场依赖的冻结温度处脱离平衡态。所得结果对理解并控制超导器件中的磁通冻结行为具有指导意义。

Abstract: We analyze residual frozen flux in a long narrow superconducting strip cooled through its transition temperature $T_{c}$ in a small perpendicular magnetic field. This problem is relevant for the issue of trapped magnetic flux in superconducting electronic devices. During cooling, the low-temperature vortex configuration is formed at temperatures very close to $T_{c}$, where the flux density is determined by dynamic balance between the thermally-activated exits and entries of vortices over the geometrical energy barrier formed by the interaction with the strip edges and the Meissner screening current. In the field range between the minimum flux-expulsion field and the penetration field, the equilibrium flux density is finite due to thermal activation and rapidly decreases with decreasing temperature. During cooling, however, the escape rate decreases exponentially, and the vortex density falls out of equilibrium at a field-dependent freezing temperature $T_{\mathrm{fr}}$. We derive and solve the dynamic-balance equation for this process, which yields definite quantitative results for $T_{\mathrm{fr}}$ and the frozen vortex density. The relative freezing temperature $1\!-\!T_{\mathrm{fr}}/T_{c}$ exceeds the fluctuation width of the transition by a large logarithmic factor, rapidly increases when the magnetic field approaches the minimum flux-expulsion field, and logarithmically increases with decreasing cooling rate. The resulting frozen flux density has a very strong magnetic-field dependence which can be used to define the effective flux-expulsion magnetic field.

</details>

### [54] [Floquet-Engineered Parity Anomaly Staircase in a Cold Atom Dirac Lattice](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05164)
*Binayyak Roy,Vito Scarola,Sumanta Tewari*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 通过Floquet工程在二维π-通量光晶格中冷原子系统实现了一个受宇称反常（parity anomaly）启发的异常霍尔阶梯（anomalous Hall staircase），其有效模型包含由时间反演对称性破缺的Floquet质量项和静态反演对称性破缺质量偏移共同产生的大质量狄拉克费米子（massive Dirac fermions），通过动量依赖的标量位移项选择性地占据各狄拉克扇区的贝里曲率（Berry curvature），从而获得接近0、e²/2h和e²/h的类平台霍尔响应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索在可控冷原子系统中实现受高能物理中宇称反常（parity anomaly）启发的拓扑现象，特别是通过Floquet工程在光晶格中构造具有量子化异常霍尔阶梯（anomalous Hall staircase）的平台响应。

Method: 采用Floquet工程在二维π-通量晶格中构建有效模型，结合时间反演对称性破缺的Floquet质量项与静态反演对称性破缺质量偏移产生大质量狄拉克费米子，并引入动量依赖的标量位移项（scalar displacement term）使不同狄拉克扇区在能量上发生相反方向偏移。通过评估完整晶格贝里曲率积分，系统分析低能狄拉克理论、能带拓扑、贝里曲率结构及双参数响应图。

Result: 通过调整化学势（chemical potential）或标量位移项，异常霍尔响应呈现阶梯式演化，平台值分别位于0、e²/2h和e²/h附近，对应零个、一个和两个有效大质量狄拉克扇区贡献的激活。论文还提出了在超冷原子光晶格中使用拉曼辅助隧穿（Raman-assisted tunneling）、非共振Floquet驱动以及交流斯塔克修饰（AC-Stark dressing）等技术的可能实现方案。

Conclusion: 该工作为在多组分冷原子系统中实现量子化异常霍尔阶梯提供了具体的理论方案和实验实现途径，连接了宇称反常概念与可观测输运现象。

Abstract: We propose a Floquet-engineered cold atom realization of a parity anomaly inspired anomalous Hall staircase in a two dimensional $π$-flux lattice. The effective model hosts massive Dirac fermions generated by the combined action of a time reversal symmetry breaking Floquet mass and a static inversion breaking mass offset. An additional momentum dependent scalar displacement term shifts different Dirac sectors in opposite energy directions without modifying their Bloch eigenvectors. As a result, the Berry curvature contribution associated with individual massive Dirac sectors can be selectively occupied, allowing the anomalous Hall response to evolve stepwise as a function of chemical potential or scalar displacement term. Evaluating the full lattice Berry curvature integral, we find plateau-like responses near $0$, $e^2/2h$, and $e^2/h$, corresponding respectively to the activation of zero, one, and two effective massive Dirac sector contributions. We analyze the associated low energy Dirac theory, band topology, Berry curvature structure, and two parameter response maps, and discuss a possible realization using Raman-assisted tunneling, off-resonant Floquet driving, and auxiliary AC-Stark dressing in ultracold atomic optical lattices.

</details>

### [56] [Cyclic source pairings for Penrose--Sparling non-Hausdorff twistor spaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04054)
*Ioannis P. Zois*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文引入非交换几何（noncommutative geometry）技术，通过构建一个étale黏合群胚（etale gluing groupoid）及其卷积代数（convolution algebra），重新诠释了反自对偶库仑场（anti-self-dual Coulomb field）的Penrose–Sparling非豪斯多夫扭量空间（non-Hausdorff twistor space）。计算表明，源适配循环配对（source-adapted cyclic pairing）能够恢复库仑荷（Coulomb charge），并进一步将结果推广到非阿贝尔主丛（principal bundle）情形。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有的Penrose–Sparling非豪斯多夫扭量空间缺乏一个代数的、可计算的描述框架。本文旨在利用非交换几何工具，为该扭量空间建立一个显式的代数模型，以便系统地处理其非分离的几何结构，并探索与之相关的拓扑不变量。

Method: 首先构造了一个显式的étale黏合群胚及其卷积代数，以代数方式编码非豪斯多夫扭量空间中已识别的开部分和两个非分离的源二次曲面（source quadric）拷贝。然后计算了两类Chern–Connes配对：一是严格的切模类比（tangent-module analogue），二是由Penrose–Sparling库仑线丛（Coulomb line bundle）定义的相对循环上循环（relative cyclic cocycle）配对。最后将构造推广到非阿贝尔情形，使用主丛语言处理连通复约化群（connected complex reductive group）及其最大环面（maximal torus）和余特征（cocharacter）。

Result: 严格的切模类比配对由于陈特征（Chern character）的对称性为零：ch₃(T¹,⁰ℂℙ³) + ch₃(T⁰,¹ℂℙ³) = 0。而基于Penrose–Sparling库仑线丛Cₙ的K₀(A_Q)-类，与支撑在两条非分离的母线（ruling line）L ⊂ Q上的相对循环上循环进行配对，得到配对值Q(Cₙ) = n，成功恢复了库仑荷。

Conclusion: 源适配的循环配对（source-adapted cyclic pairing）能够从非交换几何的角度精确提取库仑荷的整数值，表明该代数模型对非豪斯多夫扭量空间的物理内容具有良好编码能力。非阿贝尔版本的构造为主丛修正（principal G-bundle modification）提供了统一的框架。

Abstract: We introduce noncommutative geometry techniques in order to reinterpret the Penrose--Sparling non-Hausdorff twistor space of the anti-self-dual Coulomb field by means of an explicit etale gluing groupoid and its convolution algebra.
  This algebraic model keeps track of both the identified open part and the two non-separated copies of the source quadric.
  We compute two kinds of Chern--Connes pairings. The strict tangent-module analogue, obtained from \([T_{\mathbb R}\CP^3\otimes\C]\), vanishes because \[ \operatorname{ch}_3(T^{1,0}\CP^3)+ \operatorname{ch}_3(T^{0,1}\CP^3)=0. \] By contrast, the Penrose--Sparling Coulomb line bundle \(\calC_n\) defines a \(K_0(A_Q)\)-class, and the relative cyclic cocycle supported on the two non-separated copies of a ruling line \(L\subset Q\) gives \[ \mathcal Q(\calC_n)= \frac12\left\langle \varphi_L^+-\varphi_L^-,[\calC_n]\right\rangle=n. \] Thus the source-adapted cyclic pairing recovers the Coulomb charge.
  We also formulate the non-abelian version in principal-bundle language. For a connected complex reductive group \(G\), a maximal torus \(T\subset G\), and a cocharacter \(λ:\C^*\to T\), the source is a principal \(G\)-bundle modification of type \(λ\) along \(Q\).

Conclusion: 本文建立的新的变分刻画补充了标准变分公式，为在守恒型可逆相互作用粒子系统中推导扩散系数的下界提供了更直接的理论工具。通过具体实例验证了该方法的适用性。

This is a more natural framework when one is interested in obtaining lower bounds on the diffusion coefficient. ### [58] [SPLIT-PINN: Separable Probability Learning Technique via Physics-Informed Neural Networks for High-Dimensional Probabilistic Modeling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04000)
*Pouria Behnoudfar,Deekshith Naidu Ponnana,Noah J. Schmelzer,Janith Wanni,George T. Gray,Dan J. Thoma,Curt A. Bronkhorst,Nan Chen,Wenxiao Pan*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于概率建模的框架，通过李宇维尔方程（Liouville equation）和可分离概率学习技术（SPLIT-PINN），从数据中推断多晶金属材料微观状态的概率密度函数（PDF）演化规律，并实现了跨不同计算实现的泛化预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 宏观材料行为描述无法捕捉多晶金属材料中小尺度空间异质性（spatial heterogeneity）对微观结构演化的影响，现有的统计描述和推断方法在高维输运主导问题中缺乏准确性、稳定性和可解释性。

Method: 框架采用概率密度函数表示材料状态场，将微观结构演化建模为带未知漂移项（drift term）的Liouville方程；通过物理信息神经网络（Physics-Informed Neural Networks, PINNs）发展可分离概率学习技术（SPLIT-PINN），引入边际校正漂移分解（marginal-correction drift decomposition）、正交性约束（orthogonality constraints）和基于残差的自适应训练（residual-based adaptive training），实现漂移场的逆向推断。

Result: 在基准测试验证后，框架应用于多晶微观结构演化的计算数据集（含von Mises应力、位错密度和等效塑性应变率）。基于单个数据集训练得到的Liouville模型，成功预测了多个未见多晶实现的联合及边际PDF的时间演化，定量对比证明预测准确且鲁棒。

Conclusion: 该概率建模框架能够从数据中准确推断多晶材料微观状态演化的概率输运模型，并在不同计算实现间实现有效泛化，为连接小尺度异质性与宏观材料行为提供了可行的统计描述途径。

Abstract: We present a probabilistic modeling framework for incorporating small-scale spatial heterogeneity into macroscopic descriptions of material behavior for polycrystalline metallic materials. Spatially heterogeneous material state fields are represented using probability density functions (PDFs), providing a principled statistical description of microstructural variability and state evolution across different computational polycrystalline realizations. The framework is built on the inverse identification of a probabilistic transport model, formulated as a Liouville equation with an unknown drift term. To enable accurate, stable, and interpretable inference of this drift field in high-dimensional, transport-dominated settings, we develop a Separable Probability Learning Technique via Physics-Informed Neural Networks (SPLIT-PINN). This method incorporates a marginal-correction drift decomposition, orthogonality constraints, and residual-based adaptive training to enhance well-posedness, numerical stability, and physical consistency without imposing restrictive parametric assumptions. Using SPLIT-PINN, the drift field governing the temporal evolution of joint state PDFs is inferred directly from data. After benchmark validation, the framework is applied to physical computational datasets describing the evolution of polycrystalline microstructural states, including von Mises stress, dislocation density, and equivalent plastic strain rate. The learned Liouville model, trained on a single dataset, is subsequently used in forward predictions of the temporal evolution of joint and marginal PDFs for multiple unseen polycrystal realizations. Quantitative comparisons with reference PDFs demonstrate that the proposed framework yields accurate and robust probabilistic predictions and generalizes effectively across datasets.

</details>


### [59] [Uncertainty-Aware Symbolic Regression through Bayesian Support Selection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04042)
*Satadeep Bhattacharjee*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出一种概率化扩展的SISSO框架（确定性SIS/贝叶斯SO），在保持特征筛选可扩展性的同时，将稀疏化算子阶段转化为贝叶斯推断，从而提供描述符选择、回归系数和预测的不确定性量化。在Heusler合金磁矩数据集上，该方法在交叉验证RMSE和预测区间覆盖方面略有提升，更关键的是揭示了确定性分析中无法显现的竞争性描述符族。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准SISSO（Sure Independence Screening and Sparsifying Operator）是确定性的，仅返回单一描述符和点预测，无法量化描述符选择、回归系数及预测过程中的不确定性。因此，需要引入一种能够提供不确定性量化的扩展框架。

Method: 保持确定性的特征筛选（SIS）阶段以保障可扩展性，将稀疏化算子（SO）阶段重构为在SIS筛选后的支撑空间上的贝叶斯推断（Bayesian inference），形成确定性SIS/贝叶斯SO框架。在最大后验（maximum-a-posteriori, MAP）极限下可恢复标准SISSO的确定性SO描述符。

Result: 在$X_2YZ$ Heusler合金磁矩数据集上，该方法在五折交叉验证RMSE上取得适度改进，95%预测区间的经验覆盖接近标称水平。更重要的是，后验分布揭示了确定性分析中无法显现的、具有物理关联的竞争性符号描述符家族（symbolic descriptor families）。

Conclusion: 确定性SIS/贝叶斯SO可作为SISSO的一种不确定性感知诊断扩展，用于在小样本材料回归问题中评估描述符的置信度、稳定性和非唯一性（non-uniqueness）。

Abstract: The Sure Independence Screening and Sparsifying Operator (SISSO) framework is a powerful symbolic-regression method for extracting compact and interpretable descriptors from large nonlinear feature spaces. However, standard SISSO is deterministic: it returns a single descriptor and point prediction, without quantifying uncertainty in descriptor selection, regression coefficients, or predictions. Here we introduce a probabilistic extension in which the sure independence screening (SIS) stage is kept deterministic to preserve scalability, while the sparsifying operator (SO) stage is reformulated as Bayesian inference over the SIS-screened support space. The resulting deterministic-SIS/Bayesian-SO framework yields posterior probabilities for competing descriptor supports, feature-inclusion probabilities, Bayesian-model-averaged predictions, and predictive credible intervals, while recovering the deterministic SO descriptor of standard SISSO in the maximum-a-posteriori limit. Applied to an $X_2YZ$ Heusler-alloy magnetic-moment dataset, the approach gives modest improvements in five-fold cross-validation RMSE and near-nominal empirical coverage of the 95$\%$ predictive intervals. More importantly, the posterior exposes competing, physically related symbolic descriptor families that would appear artificially unique in a deterministic analysis. These results suggest that deterministic-SIS/Bayesian-SO can be used as an uncertainty-aware diagnostic extension of SISSO: a tool for assessing descriptor confidence, stability, and non-uniqueness in small-data materials regression problems.

</details>


### [60] [Emergence of Macroscopic Quantum Order via Translational Zero Modes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04187)
*Kenan Gundogdu*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出一种通过电子-晶格强耦合自生成可移动约束势（self-generated mobile confining potential）来实现宏观量子相干（macroscopic quantum coherence）的新机制，其平移零模（translational zero mode）可重构多体能谱、打开密度依赖的能隙，从而在高温下保护离域长程序（off-diagonal long-range order）。以铅卤钙钛矿中的高温超荧光（superfluorescence）作为具体实例。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统固体中的宏观量子相干（如超流、超导、凝聚体）仅限于低温，因为序形成于固定激发谱（fixed excitation spectrum）内，随温度升高竞争态会因热布居而破坏相干性。本文旨在探索一种不依赖固定谱内冷却或配对不稳定性（pairing instability）的替代路径。

Method: 通过电子激发与可变形晶格（deformable lattice）之间的强耦合，在超过临界密度时自生成约束势（confining potential），该势可俘获产生它的激发本身。该势与刚性外势不同，能在宿主晶格中平移而不改变内部结构，从而定义一个平移零模。耦合至该零模提供了一个共享的动力学坐标，降低并隔离单个集体多体构型（collective many-body configuration），打开一个密度依赖的能隙（density-dependent gap）。

Result: 该机制能抑制竞争态的热布居，支持在高温下保持离域长程序。具体实现方面，将铅卤钙钛矿中的高温超荧光识别为该零模“穿上”的激子有序态（zero mode dressed ordered excitonic state）的辐射不稳定性（radiative instability）。

Conclusion: 本文建立了一条通向宏观量子序（macroscopic quantum order）的一般性路径：既非在固定谱内冷却，也非依赖配对不稳定性，而是通过自生成的可移动约束结构，其平移零模重构多体能谱以保护相干性。

Abstract: Macroscopic quantum coherence in solids, such as in superfluids, superconductors, and condensates, is generally limited to low temperatures because order forms within a fixed excitation spectrum whose competing states become thermally populated as temperature rises. Here, we show that strong coupling between electronic excitations and a deformable lattice enables a different route. Above a critical density, this coupling nucleates self generated confining potentials that trap the very excitations generating them. Unlike rigid external traps, these potentials can translate through the host lattice without changing their internal structure, defining a translational zero mode. Coupling to this zero mode provides a shared dynamical coordinate that lowers and isolates a single collective many body configuration, opening a density dependent gap that suppresses thermal occupation of competing states and supports off diagonal long range order at elevated temperatures. As a concrete realization, we identify high-temperature superfluorescence in lead halide perovskites as the radiative instability of this zero mode dressed ordered excitonic state. More broadly, this establishes a general route to macroscopic quantum order: not cooling within a fixed spectrum, nor pairing instabilities, but a self generated mobile confining structure whose translational zero mode reconstructs the many-body spectrum to protect coherence.

</details>


### [61] [Physical properties of R$_2$Co$_6$Al$_{20-δ}$ (R = Gd-Tm, Y) single crystals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04241)
*Sushma Kumari,Fernando A. Garcia,Juan Schmidt,Tyler J. Slade,Aashish Sapkota,Ajay Kumar,Yaroslav Mudryk,Paul C. Canfield,Raquel A. Ribeiro*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本工作将单斜晶系 R₂Co₆Al₁₉ 系列扩展至重稀土元素，合成了正交晶系 R₂Co₆Al₂₀₋δ（R = Gd–Tm, Y）单晶。通过结构表征与物性测量，发现所有材料均呈现反铁磁（antiferromagnetic, AFM）有序，奈尔温度（TN）在 1.8 K（Ho）至 11.8 K（Tb）之间，其中 Gd 和 Tb 基材料表现出两个不同的 AFM 相变。研究揭示了该体系中 RKKY 交换与晶体电场（crystal electric field, CEF）相互作用的重要竞争关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 轻稀土 R₂Co₆Al₁₉ 系列已展现出从非费米液体行为到反铁磁有序等丰富的物理性质，且性质随稀土元素 R 变化。为进一步理解该体系的物理机制，本文将其拓展至重稀土元素，系统研究其晶体结构与物性演化。

Method: 通过单晶合成方法制备了重稀土化合物 R₂Co₆Al₂₀₋δ（R = Gd–Tm, Y），采用单晶 X 射线衍射（single crystal X-ray diffraction）确定晶体结构，并利用变温比热、电阻率和磁化率测量表征其物理性质。

Result: 所有化合物均采用正交晶系 Imma 型结构，δ 值在重稀土序列中非单调变化（0.73–0.91）。所有材料均表现出反铁磁有序，TN 范围为 1.8 K（Ho）至 11.8 K（Tb）；Gd 和 Tb 基材料存在两个分离约 2–3 K 的 AFM 相变。体系偏离 de Gennes 定标关系，并出现各向异性交叉。

Conclusion: 重稀土 R₂Co₆Al₂₀₋δ 系列被确认为具有强晶体电场效应和交换各向异性的各向异性反铁磁体。偏离 de Gennes 定标以及各向异性交叉现象突显了 RKKY 交换与晶体电场相互作用在该正交晶系中的关键竞争。

Abstract: Rare-earth (R) based intermetallic compounds can often exhibit diverse physical properties and distinct magnetic anisotropies. A Notable example are the light rare earth members of the mono-clinic, R$_2$Co$_6$Al$_{19}$ series that are known to display a range of physical properties, from non-Fermi liquid behavior to antiferromagnetic (AFM) ordering, with properties that vary depending on R. In this work, we have extended this series to the heavy rare earths and systematically investigate the synthesis, crystal structure, and physical properties of single crystals of  R$_2$Co$_6$Al$_{20-δ}$ for R = Gd - Tm and Y. Single crystal X-ray diffraction reveals that these materials adopt an orthorhombic Imma-type structure with delta varying non-monotonically across the heavy rare earths; ranging from 0.73 for Dy to 0.91 for Gd. Temperature-dependent specific heat, resistivity, and magnetization measurements demonstrate AFM ordering in all materials, with the Neel temperature (TN) ranging from 1.8 K for Ho to 11.8 K for Tb. Notably, Gd and Tb-based materials exhibit two distinct AFM transitions, separated by approximately 2 - 3 K. These findings establish the heavy rare-earth members of the R2Co6Al20-delta series as anisotropic antiferromagnets with strong crystal electric field effects and exchange anisotropy. The observed deviation from de Gennes scaling and the anisotropy crossover across the series highlight the important interplay between RKKY exchange and crystal electric field interactions in this orthorhombic system.

### [62] [High-density, high-mobility ultrathin spin-polarized two-dimensional electron gas at the polar/polar LaVO$_3$/KTaO$_3$ interface: Insights from first-principles calculations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04252)
*Arpan Das*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过第一性原理密度泛函理论（DFT）计算，揭示了在KTaO₃/LaVO₃界面处形成高迁移率、自旋极化二维电子气（2DEG）的微观机制，源于界面极性不连续性驱动的电子重构。该2DEG具有极小的有效质量和接近一量级更高的载流子密度，优于典型的LaAlO₃/SrTiO₃界面。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索氧化物界面处高迁移率二维电子气（2DEG）的微观起源，为新兴量子现象和下一代氧化物电子学提供理论依据。

Method: 采用第一性原理密度泛函理论（DFT）计算，对能带绝缘体KTaO₃（KTO）与Mott绝缘体LaVO₃（LVO）构成的异质结界面进行电子结构分析。

Result: 界面金属态源自极性不连续性驱动的电子重构：电子从外表面向界面转移，在表面VO₂层形成空穴积累、界面TaO₂层形成电子积累，从而稳定了高度局域且自旋极化的2DEG。该2DEG主要由界面Ta 5d_xy轨道贡献，其自旋向上抛物型能带的有效质量极低，且界面电子密度比LaAlO₃/SrTiO₃界面高出近一个量级。

Conclusion: LVO/KTO异质结是实现高密度、高迁移率、自旋极化2DEG的理想平台，为关联氧化物界面在量子电子学中的应用提供了新方向。

Abstract: The emergence of high-mobility two-dimensional electron gases (2DEGs) at oxide interfaces provides a fertile platform for exploring emergent quantum phenomena and next-generation oxide electronics. Here, using first-principles density functional theory (DFT) calculations, we investigate the microscopic origin of the 2DEG formed at the interface between the band insulator KTaO$_3$ (KTO) and the Mott insulator LaVO$_3$ (LVO). Although both constituents are insulating in bulk, the LVO/KTO heterostructure develops robust metallicity at the interface, consistent with experimental observations. Our calculations show that this metallic state originates from an electronic reconstruction driven by the polar discontinuity across the interface. To avoid the polar catastrophe on both the polar LVO film and the polar KTO substrate, electrons are transferred from the outer surfaces toward the interface, leading to hole accumulation in the surface VO$_2$ layer and electron accumulation in the interfacial TaO$_2$ layer. This charge redistribution stabilizes a highly confined and spin-polarized 2DEG localized at the interface. The electronic states forming the 2DEG are predominantly derived from interfacial Ta $5d_{xy}$ orbitals, confining carrier motion to the interfacial plane. Remarkably, the spin-up parabolic band hosting the 2DEG exhibits an exceptionally small effective mass, substantially lower than that of the prototypical LaAlO$_3$/SrTiO$_3$ interface, indicating the potential for enhanced carrier mobility. Furthermore, the calculated interfacial electron density is nearly an order of magnitude larger than that of LaAlO$_3$/SrTiO$_3$, consistent with experiment. These findings identify the LVO/KTO heterostructure as a promising platform for realizing high-density, high-mobility spin-polarized 2DEGs and for engineering correlated oxide interfaces for quantum electronic applications.

*Mingda Ding,Nanami Sakurai,Man Shen,Taiki Inoue,Takahisa Matsuzaki,Takuo Mizuno,Kento Suzuki,John Isaac Enriquez,Harry Handoko Halim,Yuji Hamamoto,Yuta Nishina,Hiroshi Y. Yoshikawa,Yoshitada Morikawa,Yoshihiro Kobayashi*

Method: 结合分子动力学（molecular dynamics, MD）模拟与纳米压痕（nanoindentation）实验。MD模拟了由两层石墨烯夹持CNTs的堆叠结构，识别了能量稳定构型及其控制参数（管间距、CNT直径和壁数）；实验方面制备了还原氧化石墨烯（reduced graphene oxide, rGO）-CNT杂化薄膜，并基于原子力显微镜进行纳米压痕测量。

Conclusion: 该研究为Gr-CNT杂化体系提供了重要的力学理解，并为设计具有增强性能的微观结构用于先进应用提供了指导。

Abstract: Hybrid systems composed of graphene (Gr) and carbon nanotubes (CNTs), such as films and aerogels, have attracted broad attention for applications in electronics, mechanics, energy, and environmental science. Since the microstructures of Gr-CNT hybrids strongly affect their properties, it is essential to establish mechanical principles that govern these structures. In this study, we investigated the structural stability and mechanical behavior of Gr-CNT hybrid systems by combining molecular dynamics (MD) simulations and nanoindentation experiments. MD simulations of stacked Gr-CNT structures, in which two Gr layers confine CNTs between them, identified the energetically stable configurations and their governing parameters, i.e., intertube spacing, CNT diameter, and wall number. Specifically, under certain conditions, the structures exhibit mechanical bistability with two stable configurations: adhesion and separation of the Gr layers, arising from the competition between interlayer van der Waals attraction and elastic deformation of Gr and CNTs. Simulated loading--unloading curves display hysteresis and energy dissipation related to the stable configurations. In addition, reduced graphene oxide (rGO)-CNT hybrid films were experimentally fabricated as macroscopic assemblies of the unit structures modeled in the simulations. Atomic force microscopy-based nanoindentation measurements on the rGO-CNT films exhibit clear hysteresis and higher dissipation energy compared with pure rGO, in good agreement with the simulation results. These results provide valuable insights into Gr-CNT hybrid systems and offer guidance for designing microstructures with enhanced properties for advanced applications.

This shows that the half-metallic character of the electron band structure translates into a fully spin polarized current flowing across the patterned films. ### [66] [Why Fe doping kills photoluminescence in CsPbCl$_3$ but not in CsPbBr$_3$: Role of midgap Fe 3$d$ states and electron-phonon coupling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04714)
*Arpan Das,Saptarshi Chakraborty*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过自旋极化密度泛函理论计算、实验测量和电子-声子耦合分析，揭示了Fe掺杂卤化物钙钛矿纳米晶中光致发光淬灭的微观机制，指出电子-声子耦合（electron-phonon coupling）是决定不同卤素组分下淬灭行为差异的关键因素。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解过渡金属掺杂对卤化物钙钛矿纳米晶（halide perovskite nanocrystals）光电性质的影响，是合理设计用于光子学应用（photonic applications）材料的基础。

Method: 采用自旋极化密度泛函理论（spin-polarized density functional theory, DFT）计算、实验光致发光（photoluminescence, PL）测量以及基于形变势方法（deformation potential approach）的电子-声子耦合计算。

Result: Fe掺杂引入的3d中间隙态（midgap states）形成高效电子捕获中心，驱动非辐射复合，抑制PL强度。CsPbCl3中PL完全淬灭而CsPbBr3保留饱和PL强度，电子结构计算和声子计算均无法解释该差异，但电子-声子耦合计算显示Fe掺杂CsPbCl3中存在显著更强的耦合，导致电子激发能高效耗散为晶格振动。

Conclusion: 电子-声子耦合是决定卤素依赖性PL淬灭的关键因素，为掺杂诱导的非辐射过程提供了统一的微观框架（unified microscopic framework）。

Abstract: Understanding the impact of transition-metal doping on the optoelectronic properties of halide perovskite nanocrystals is essential for their rational design in photonic applications. We establish the microscopic origin of photoluminescence (PL) quenching in Fe-doped CsPbCl$_3$ using spin-polarized density functional theory calculations. The emergence of Fe 3$d$ midgap states creates efficient electron-trapping centres that drive nonradiative recombination, accounting for the reduced PL intensity. Extending this analysis to Fe-doped CsPbX$_3$ (X = Cl, Br), we show experimentally that although PL intensity is suppressed in both systems relative to their pristine counterparts, their high-doping behaviour diverges: CsPbCl$_3$ becomes completely non-emissive, whereas CsPbBr$_3$ retains a finite, saturated PL intensity. Despite this contrast, electronic structure calculations reveal nearly identical midgap states in both materials, indicating that electronic effects alone cannot explain the distinct PL responses. Phonon calculations likewise fail to capture this difference. In contrast, electron-phonon coupling calculations based on the deformation potential approach reveal significantly stronger coupling in Fe-doped CsPbCl$_3$, enabling efficient dissipation of electronic excitation energy into lattice vibrations and leading to complete PL quenching. These results identify electron-phonon coupling as the key factor governing halide-dependent PL quenching and provide a unified microscopic framework for dopant-induced nonradiative processes in halide perovskites.

### [67] [Tunable Rashba Splitting in Janus InXPbP (X = S, Se, Te) Monolayers for Enhanced Photocatalytic Water Splitting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04720)

Method: 采用基于密度泛函理论（DFT）的第一性原理计算方法，对Janus InXPbP (X = S, Se, Te)单层的结构、力学、电子、光学和光催化性质进行了系统计算分析。

Abstract: Janus two-dimensional (2D) materials exhibiting Rashba spin splitting have recently attracted considerable attention owing to their potential applications in spintronic devices and photocatalytic water splitting. In this work, we investigate, using first-principles calculations, the structural, mechanical, electronic, optical, and photocatalytic properties of Janus InXPbP (X = S, Se, Te) monolayers that exhibit significant Rashba effects. Our results demonstrate that all three monolayers are energetically, dynamically, and mechanically stable, as evidenced by cohesive energy calculations, phonon dispersion analysis, and elastic constants. By varying the chalcogen atom (X = S, Se, Te), the Rashba effect in InXPbP can be effectively tuned. All three monolayers possess suitable band-edge alignments for overall water splitting, yielding solar-to-hydrogen (STH) conversion efficiencies of 21.67%, 26.03%, and 29.83% for InSPbP, InSePbP, and InTePbP, respectively. Our findings not only enrich the family of Janus materials but also suggest that the Janus InXPbP monolayers are promising candidates for spintronic devices and high-performance photocatalytic water-splitting applications.

### [68] [Curvature-driven revival of charge density waves in non-Euclidean space](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04728)
*Zhipeng Song,Zeyu Liu,Junde Liu,Yi Biao,Anning Yang,Qian Fang,Mojun Pan,Chen Liu,Jiaou Wang,Tian Qian,Chenmin shen,Hongliang Lu,Wei Ji,Hong-Jun Gao,Xiao Lin*

TL;DR: 通过在BLG/SiC衬底上首次构建单层TiSe₂-NbSe₂异质结构，该研究报道了非欧几何曲率驱动受抑电荷序（frustrated charge order）复活的现象。低温角分辨光电子能谱（ARPES）显示界面电荷转移破坏了全局费米面嵌套（Fermi surface nesting）并抑制了欧几里得平坦区域的长程电荷密度波（CDW）；然而，高分辨扫描隧道显微镜（STM）揭示了一种新型非线性CDW态奇迹般地存活在非欧几里得纳米级弯曲区域中。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 强关联量子态（如电荷密度波）对费米面拓扑和晶格对称性高度敏感，且通常被重载流子掺杂（heavy carrier doping）所抑制。在二维体系中，宏观几何曲率成为调控微观量子相干性的新型结构自由度，因此一个关键物理问题是：非欧几何变形能否与极端电子扰动竞争，从而重塑甚至复活已被抑制的宏观量子序。

Method: 在BLG/SiC衬底上构建单层TiSe₂-NbSe₂异质结构，结合低温角分辨光电子能谱（ARPES）和高分辨扫描隧道显微镜（STM）进行电子结构和实空间形貌表征，并辅以原子尺度模拟（atomistic simulations）揭示其结构起源。

Result: 界面电荷转移破坏了全局费米面嵌套，完全抑制了欧几里得平坦区域的长程CDW序；但在形态扭曲的非欧几里得纳米级弯曲区域中，一种新型非线性CDW态（non-linear CDW state）奇迹般地存活且严格局域化。原子模拟表明，界面扭转（interfacial twist）和晶格失配（lattice mismatch）自发产生了波纹状超晶格（corrugated superlattice）。

Conclusion: 非欧几何曲率作为二维体系中一种新颖的结构自由度，能够与极端电子掺杂效应相抗衡，在局域尺度上复活已被抑制的宏观量子序。这一发现为利用几何曲率调控强关联量子态提供了新的物理机制。

Abstract: Strongly correlated quantum states, such as charge density waves (CDWs), are exquisitely sensitive to Fermi surface topology and lattice symmetry, and are typically quenched by heavy carrier doping. In two-dimensional (2D) systems, however, macroscopic geometric curvature emerges as a novel structural degree of freedom to modulate microscopic quantum coherence. This raises a compelling physical question: can non-Euclidean geometric deformations compete with extreme electronic perturbations to reshape, or even revive, a quenched macroscopic quantum order? Here, by constructing monolayer TiSe$_2$-NbSe$_2$ heterostructure on a BLG/SiC substrate for the first time, we report the curvature-driven revival of a frustrated charge order in a non-Euclidean space. Low-temperature angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy (ARPES) reveals a massive interfacial charge transfer, which destroys the global Fermi surface nesting and completely suppresses the long-range CDW order in Euclidean flat regions. Strikingly, high-resolution scanning tunneling microscopy (STM) reveals that a novel, non-linear CDW state miraculously survives, remaining strictly localized within morphologically distorted, non-Euclidean nanoscale curved regions. Atomistic simulations unravel the structural origin of this phenomenon, demonstrating that interfacial twist and lattice mismatch spontaneously generate a corrugated superlattice.

</details>

While this mechanism induces sizeable electric polarization, it typically occurs at low temperatures and in complex materials. ### [70] [Strain-induced suppression of thermochromism in divalent cobalt molybdate thin films](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04745)

TL;DR: 该论文通过实验与理论结合，研究了热致变色氧化物 $CoMoO_4$ 薄膜的行为。结果表明，微应变（microstrain）抑制了块体粉末中观察到的 $\beta \rightarrow \alpha$ 结构相变，使薄膜在全部温度范围内保持高温 $\beta$ 相，并通过增强晶体场（crystal field）稳定该相，同时揭示了声子和电子反常的光学响应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 热致变色氧化物（thermochromic oxides）为耦合晶格、电子和磁自由度提供了平台，其中 $CoMoO_4$ 是典型材料。尽管粉末态研究充分，但薄膜行为——对器件应用至关重要——尚未被探索。因此，本文旨在填补 $CoMoO_4$ 薄膜在结构与光学性质上的认知空白。

Method: 采用实验与理论相结合的方法，包括首次在薄膜形式下获取 $β- CoMoO_4$ 的太赫兹-可见-紫外（THz-VIS-UV）光谱，并结合温度依赖性 X 射线衍射（X-ray diffraction）、结构精修（structural refinements）和理论计算进行表征。

Result: $CoMoO_4$ 薄膜在全部温度范围内保持高温 $\beta$ 相，而非如粉末在 230K 附近发生一级 $\beta \rightarrow \alpha$ 结构转变。光学光谱显示低声子软化（42 cm$^{-1}$，冷却时反常软化）及 Co$^{2+}$ 晶体场跃迁与电荷转移激发的蓝移。X 射线衍射确认 $\beta$ 相对称性持续存在，微应变随降温增大。

Conclusion: 微应变从根本上重塑了相图（phase landscape），抑制了热致变色效应并稳定了 $\beta$ 相。晶体场增强（crystal field strengthening）被识别为稳定 $\beta$ 相的关键机制。该工作确立了应变作为热致变色氧化物中调控相稳定性和功能性质的热力学杠杆（thermodynamic lever）。

Abstract: Thermochromic oxides provide a platform for coupling lattice, electronic, and magnetic degrees of freedom, with divalent cobalt molybdate $CoMoO_4$ as a prototypical example. Here, we present a combined experimental and theoretical investigation of $CoMoO_4$ thin films, including the first THz-VIS-UV spectra of $β- CoMoO_4$ in thin-film form. In contrast to bulk powders, which undergo a first order $β\rightarrow α$ structural transition near 230K, the thin films retain the high-temperature $β-$phase across the entire temperature range. We show that microstrain fundamentally reshapes the phase landscape, suppressing thermochromism and stabilizing the $β-$phase. The optical spectra reveal pronounced phonon and electronic anomalies, including a softening of a low-energy, cation-dominated phonon (42cm$^{-1}$) upon cooling, in contrast to conventional mode-hardening. This behaviour indicates incipient atomic displacements analogous to those driving the bulk $β\rightarrow α$ transition, despite the absence of a structural phase change, and saturates between 200 and 150K. Temperature-dependent X-ray diffraction confirms persistent β-phase symmetry with increasing microstrain, consistent with strain-induced frustration of the first-order transition. At higher energies (0.12-3.7eV), the optical response exhibits a blue-shift of Co$^{2+}$crystal-field transitions and charge-transfer excitations, indicating a strain-enhanced ligand field. Supported by structural refinements and theoretical calculations, we identify crystal field strengthening as the key mechanism stabilizing the $β$-phase. These results establish strain as a thermodynamic lever to control phase stability and functional properties in thermochromic oxides.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: A generalised version of the continuum theory of curved dislocations describing the spatial and temporal evolution of the fields: statistically stored dislocation density, geometrically necessary dislocation density, and curvature has recently been proposed. The dynamics of the system are derived from a scalar functional of the relevant fields that cannot increase during the evolution of the system. However, the framework was established only for small deformations.
  The aim of the present paper is to discuss the fundamentals of the elasticity theory of finite deformation in cases where individual dislocations are present in the system. The equilibrium equations are derived within a variational formalism. It is shown that introducing dislocations into the finite deformation framework is a nontrivial task. Moreover, if the deformation is large, the force acting on a dislocation segment is not the well-known Peach-Koehler force. In a forthcoming paper, the results obtained will be applied to the generalisation of the dislocation continuum theory of curved dislocations.

### [74] [SLUSCHI-UP: A Web Infrastructure for SLUSCHI Melting-Temperature Calculations Using Universal Machine-Learning Interatomic Potentials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04973)
*Qi-Jun Hong*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文介绍了SLUSCHI-UP，一个基于网页的原子尺度熔点估算服务。该服务将SLUSCHI小胞固液共存方法与可选的预训练通用机器学习原子间势（uMLIP）及异步GPU执行相结合。用户无需本地安装即可提交晶体结构、选择uMLIP后端进行排队计算。在MeltBench-10验证集上，三个生产后端的原始共存平均绝对误差约为178–327 K，PBC校正后的Allegro-OAM-L预测误差约为166 K。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高温材料设计中熔点（melting temperature）是关键性质，但基于有限温度分子动力学（finite-temperature molecular dynamics）的第一性原理熔点计算需要大量计算资源。SLUSCHI方法通过小胞固液共存模拟和大量短分子动力学轨迹的统计分析降低了这一成本，但仍需进一步降低使用门槛并提升计算效率。

Method: SLUSCHI-UP是一个部署在网页上的原子尺度熔点估算服务，它将SLUSCHI工作流与可选择的预训练通用机器学习原子间势（universal machine-learning interatomic potentials, uMLIPs）及异步GPU执行（asynchronous GPU execution）耦合在一起。用户通过Materials Project标识符或POSCAR输入提交晶体结构，选择uMLIP后端（当前支持mace-mpa-0-medium、Allegro-OAM-L和DPA-3.2-5M-OMat24），然后启动排队计算，无需本地安装仿真软件。

Result: 在包含10个样品的MeltBench-10验证集上，三个生产后端的原始共存平均绝对误差（mean absolute error, MAE）约为178–327 K。在MeltBench更广泛材料集上，当前已部署任务快照包含119条原始uMLIP条目，PBE校正后的Allegro-OAM-L预测MAE约为166 K。这些数值应视为筛选级基础设施验证结果，而非uMLIP的最终排名。

Conclusion: SLUSCHI-UP提供了一个实用且具有出处可追溯性（provenance-aware）的部署层，介于快速标量熔点预测器与更昂贵的第一性原理共存计算之间。该方法保留了uMLIP的可迁移性（transferability）、有限尺寸采样（finite-size sampling）和高温轨迹稳定性（high-temperature trajectory stability）等常见局限性。

Abstract: Melting temperature is a critical property for high-temperature materials design, but first-principles melting calculations based on finite-temperature molecular dynamics can require substantial computational resources. The SLUSCHI method reduces this cost by using small-cell solid--liquid coexistence simulations and statistical analysis of many short molecular-dynamics trajectories. Here I present SLUSCHI-UP, a deployed web service for atomistic melting-temperature estimation that couples the SLUSCHI workflow to selectable pretrained universal machine-learning interatomic potentials (uMLIPs) and asynchronous GPU execution. Users submit a crystal structure through a Materials Project identifier or POSCAR input, select a uMLIP backend, and launch a queued melting calculation without local installation of simulation software. The current production interface supports mace-mpa-0-medium, Allegro-OAM-L, and DPA-3.2-5M-OMat24, while beta deployments expose additional models. On the compact MeltBench-10 validation set, the three production backends produce raw coexistence mean absolute errors in the range of approximately 178--327 K. Across the broader set of materials tested so far in MeltBench, the current deployed-job snapshot contains 119 raw uMLIP entries, and PBE-corrected Allegro-OAM-L predictions reach a mean absolute error of approximately 166 K. These values should be interpreted as screening-level infrastructure validation rather than a definitive ranking of uMLIPs. The results demonstrate that SLUSCHI-UP provides a practical, provenance-aware deployment layer between fast scalar melting-temperature predictors and much more expensive first-principles coexistence calculations, while retaining the usual limitations of uMLIP transferability, finite-size sampling, and high-temperature trajectory stability.

### [75] [Berry-Curvature Activation by Orbital Flux in a Kagome Altermagnet](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04984)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索在无净磁化（net magnetization）的补偿磁系统中，如何实现动量依赖的自旋劈裂（momentum-dependent spin splitting）和贝里曲率工程（Berry-curvature engineering），并寻找一种不依赖相对论效应和标量自旋手性（scalar spin chirality）的全轨道机制来产生拓扑响应。

Method: 构建一个最小紧束缚模型（tight-binding model），包含最近邻跳迁、非共线交换耦合（noncollinear exchange coupling）、内禀自旋轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）和轨道手性通量，系统分析在kagome晶格上120°补偿共面磁织构（coplanar magnetic texture）下的电子结构、贝里曲率和异常霍尔电导（anomalous Hall conductivity）。

Result: 非共线交换场单独即可产生显著的交错磁自旋劈裂（altermagnetic spin splitting）和自旋极化费米面（spin-polarized Fermi surfaces）。严格共面磁态下隐藏反幺正对称性（hidden antiunitary symmetry） T C_{2z} 强制贝里曲率为零；引入轨道手性通量打破该对称性后，即使完全没有自旋轨道耦合和标量自旋手性，也能产生局域贝里曲率热点（Berry curvature hot spots）和强异常霍尔响应。

Conclusion: 受挫kagome交错磁体（frustrated kagome altermagnets）是工程化补偿磁系统中拓扑输运、贝里曲率和自旋选择性电子结构的多功能平台，揭示了从对称性保护的交错磁金属到拓扑交错磁相的层级相变机制。

Abstract: We investigate topological electronic responses in a kagome altermagnetic metal hosting a compensated coplanar $120^\circ$ magnetic texture. Using a minimal tight-binding model incorporating nearest-neighbor hopping, noncollinear exchange coupling, intrinsic spin--orbit coupling, and an emergent orbital chiral flux, we demonstrate that frustrated kagome altermagnets provide a natural platform for realizing momentum-dependent spin splitting and Berry-curvature engineering without net magnetization. The noncollinear exchange field alone generates pronounced altermagnetic spin splitting and spin-polarized Fermi surfaces despite the absence of relativistic effects. However, for a strictly coplanar magnetic state, the system preserves a hidden antiunitary symmetry $\mathcal{T}C_{2z}$, which enforces identically vanishing Berry curvature even in the presence of sizeable spin--orbit coupling. We show that finite Berry curvature emerges only after introducing an orbital chiral flux term that breaks the hidden symmetry and generates effective momentum-space gauge fields analogous to a Haldane-type orbital flux. Remarkably, this mechanism produces local Berry curvature hot spots even in the complete absence of spin--orbit coupling and scalar spin chirality, establishing a purely orbital route toward topological altermagnetism. By systematically analyzing the anomalous Hall conductivity as a function of exchange coupling, spin--orbit interaction, and chiral flux, we identify a hierarchy of competing energy scales governing the transition from a symmetry-protected altermagnetic metal to a topological altermagnetic phase with strong Hall response. Our results demonstrate that frustrated kagome altermagnets constitute a versatile platform for engineering topological transport, Berry curvature, and spin-selective electronic structure in compensated magnetic systems.

</details>


### [76] [Autonomous heterogeneous catalyst discovery with a self-evolving multi-agent digital twin](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05050)
*Zhilong Song,Zongmin Zhang,Lixue Cheng*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出CatDT（Catalysis Digital Twin），一个自进化多智能体系统，通过八个专业智能体和27个科学工具，在单GPU上5-30分钟内完成从晶体结构到反应动力学的催化模拟。其中创新点UniMech将路径搜索成本降低三个数量级以上，记忆增强强化循环将势垒计算成功率从41%提升至84%。在七类气固催化基准上，预测结果与实验值的偏差控制在0.5-2倍范围内。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理论多相催化（theoretical heterogeneous catalysis）的计算和机器学习预测常与实验偏离，且局限于窄的材料家族，缺乏忠实且考虑工况条件的催化模拟器。

Method: CatDT是一个自进化多智能体系统（self-evolving multi-agent system），集成八个专业智能体和27个科学工具，从初始体相晶体和自然语言反应描述出发，自动完成稳定晶面预测、工作表面重构、反应路径枚举与排序、过渡态定位及动力学计算。两大核心创新为：UniMech通过融合智能体引导提议与能量缓存图搜索（energy-cached graph search），实现主导路径的高效发现；记忆增强强化循环（memory-augmented reinforcement loop）提升势垒计算成功率。

Result: 在七类气固催化基准（包括阶梯金属、单原子催化剂、有序金属间化合物、富含空位的二维硫化物和碳化物、以及强金属-载体相互作用界面）上，所有CatDT预测值在四个数量级范围内与实验偏差在0.5-2倍之间。在丙烷脱氢（propane dehydrogenation）任务中，CatDT独立发现的非贵金属候选催化剂Ni@ZrO₂ SMSI覆盖层达到模拟TOF为1.63 s⁻¹，选择性约100%，与Pt基工业基准相当。

Conclusion: 实现忠实催化剂数字孪生（catalyst digital twin）的关键因素不在于原始大语言模型（large language model, LLM）能力，而在于围绕其构建的工程架构：确定性工具、持久记忆和经过验证的自我改进机制，这些要素在模型、工具和运行轮次之间形成复合增益。

Abstract: Theoretical heterogeneous catalysis promises rapid catalyst discovery, yet computational and machine-learning predictions often deviate from experiment and stay confined to narrow material families, for want of a faithful, condition-aware catalytic simulator. We present CatDT (Catalysis Digital Twin), a self-evolving multi-agent system that builds an autonomous digital twin of a working catalyst, unifying gas-solid and liquid-solid modeling. From only a bulk crystal and a natural-language reaction description, eight specialized agents and 27 scientific tools predict stable facets, reconstruct working surfaces, enumerate and rank reaction pathways, locate transition states, and compute kinetics in 5-30 min on a single GPU. Two innovations address the hardest steps: UniMech finds dominant pathways for novel materials at over $10^3\times$ lower cost than exhaustive enumeration by fusing agent-guided proposals with energy-cached graph search, and a memory-augmented reinforcement loop raises barrier-calculation success from 41\% to 84\% across 600 catalytic surfaces. Across seven gas-solid benchmarks -- stepped metals, single-atom catalysts, ordered intermetallics, vacancy-rich 2D sulfides and carbides, and a strong-metal--support-interaction (SMSI) interface -- every CatDT prediction lies within 0.5-2 times experiment over four orders of magnitude. For propane dehydrogenation, CatDT independently discovers non-precious candidates rivaling the Pt-based industrial benchmark, with a proposed Ni@ZrO$_2$ SMSI overlayer reaching a simulated TOF of $1.63~\text{s}^{-1}$ at $\sim$100\% selectivity. More broadly, the decisive factor for a faithful catalyst digital twin -- or any multi-stage scientific simulator -- is not raw LLM capability but the engineered harness around it: deterministic tools, persistent memory, and verified self-improvement that compound across models, tools, and runs.

### [77] [Mechanoluminescence in crystalline inorganic materials: local disorder and the elastic distortion hypothesis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05065)
*T. Rouxel,X. Rocquefelte,S. Tanabe*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过弹性常数运动学分析，研究了机械载荷对无机化合物中活性位点局部畸变与对称性破缺的影响，提出机械发光（ML）现象需要同时考虑静态结构畸变和动态载荷诱导畸变，并用简单多边形晶格变形模型解释了压力/剪切灵敏度差异、卸载时ML增强等实验现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解无机化合物机械发光（ML）现象的机制，重点关注机械载荷如何影响活性位点的局部畸变（local distortion）与对称性破缺（loss of symmetry）。

Method: 基于弹性常数（elastic constants）进行运动学分析（kinematic analysis），比较载荷诱导畸变与Baur描述符量化的本征结构畸变；采用简单多边形晶格（polygonal motifs）近似晶体变形。

Result: 载荷诱导畸变在量级上小于但可比拟于本征结构畸变；提出了静态结构畸变需由动态载荷畸变补充的框架，解释了静水压与剪切灵敏度差异、卸载时ML峰出现、以及有/无载荷下紫外预辐照的行为差异。

Conclusion: 结构畸变作为ML的结构指纹（structural fingerprint）本质上是静态参数，必须辅以机械载荷下发展的动态畸变贡献才能完整描述ML行为。

Abstract: In this exploratory work, we aim to understand the mechanoluminescence (ML) phenomenon manifested by various inorganic compounds by focusing on the influence of mechanical loading on local distortion and loss of symmetry at active sites. To this end, we have analyzed the elastic deformation of several relevant crystalline phases and shown, through a kinematic analysis based on elastic constants, that the loading-induced distortion is smaller than, but remains comparable in magnitude to, the intrinsic structural distortion as quantified by the Baur descriptor. Although the structural distortion has previously been proposed as a structural fingerprint of the ML potential of a compound, it is by nature a static parameter, and must be supplemented by a dynamic distortion contribution that develops under mechanical load. By approximating the crystal deformation by that of simple polygonal motifs, we have been able to propose a rationale for otherwise puzzling observations: in particular, the marked differences in sensitivity to hydrostatic pressure and to shear, the appearance of an intense ML peak upon unloading in certain compounds, and the contrast in behavior depending on whether the preliminary UV irradiation is performed under load or at rest.

Method: 采用基于密度泛函理论的第一性原理计算，量化间隙位（interstitials）、空位（vacancies）和非化学计量非晶结构（amorphous structures）对氢在 \b{eta}-SiC中行为的影响。

Abstract: An ab initio framework using density-functional theory has been developed to predict hydrogen solubility in both pristine and defective \b{eta}-SiC. This study is motivated by the critical need for accurate hydrogen permeation models in fusion reactor designs, where predicting hydrogen permeation through tritium permeation barrier (TPB) materials is essential. Although silicon carbide is one of the leading candidates for TPBs, experimental permeation values vary widely due to differences between ideal single crystals and real, defect-containing materials. First principles calculations are employed to quantify the effects of interstitials, vacancies, and nonstoichiometric (amorphous) structures on hydrogen behavior in \b{eta}-SiC. Our results show that hydrogen solubility is significantly enhanced in carbon-rich nonstoichiometric amorphous structures and silicon vacancies compared to hydrogen occupying interstitial sites in pure \b{eta}-SiC.
