### [79] [MicroCup: A Cryogenic Specimen Preparation Strategy for Atom Probe Tomography of Organic Molecular Liquids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05147)
*Kuan Meng,Florian Groll,Sebastian Eich,Guido Schmitz*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为MicroCup的策略，用于改善有机分子液体的原子探针断层扫描（APT）分析。该策略通过在聚焦离子束（FIB）制备的纳米级空腔中限制液体，提高了制样重现性、通量并减少了束流损伤。以液晶8CB和8OCB为模型体系，实现了稳定的场蒸发条件和70%以上的完整离子分子保存率，并揭示了氧原子对碎裂路径的影响以及固液界面的空间分辨证据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 有机分子液体的原子探针断层扫描（atom probe tomography, APT）受到低温聚焦离子束（cryo-FIB）制样过程中试样几何形状重现性差、减薄速率低以及束流敏感性的限制，亟需一种能够提高制样重复性和通量、减少束流损伤的改进方法。

Method: 引入MicroCup策略，在FIB制备的纳米级空腔中限制液体，在相分离（phase separation）之前进行封装，以减少沉积体积、提高制样通量、实现可重复的试样几何形状，并最小化目标区域的束流暴露。以液晶4'-辛基-4-氰基联苯（8CB）和4'-辛氧基-4-氰基联苯（8OCB）作为模型体系进行实验验证。

Result: 在近晶相（smectic-like phases）中实现了稳定且可重复的场蒸发（field evaporation）条件，完整离子分子保存率超过70%，碎裂行为具有可解释性。氧原子的存在促进了与高电场下键极化（bond polarization）相关的优先裂解路径。在MicroCup腔内诱导部分结晶后，8CB在晶区和非晶区表现出相似的蒸发行为，而8OCB则呈现更明显的区域对比：近晶相区域以完整分子或大碎片为主，晶区则产生小烷基碎片和醚类物种。

Conclusion: 该工作首次通过APT提供了冷冻制备有机液体中固液界面（solid-liquid interface）的空间分辨证据，并建立了一套可重复的工作流程，用于探测软材料（soft materials）中的局部相行为。

Abstract: Atom probe tomography (APT) of organic molecular liquids is limited by poorly reproducible specimen geometry, reduced milling rates, and beam sensitivity during cryo-FIB preparation. Here we introduce a MicroCup strategy that confines liquids in a FIB-prepared nanoscale cavity prior to phase separation, reduces deposited volume to increase preparation throughput, enables reproducible specimen geometry, and minimizes beam exposure in the region of interest. Using the liquid crystals 4'-octyl-4-cyanobiphenyl (8CB) and 4'-octyloxy-4-cyanobiphenyl (8OCB) as model systems, we establish stable and reproducible field evaporation conditions, enabling the detected intact ion molecular preservation above 70% in smectic-like phases with interpretable fragmentation behavior. Comparative analysis further shows that the oxygen atom in 8OCB promotes preferential cleavage pathways associated with bond polarization under high electric fields. By inducing partial crystallization within the MicroCup cavity, distinct regions could be resolved: 8CB shows broadly similar evaporation behavior across crystalline and amorphous regions, whereas 8OCB exhibits clearer regional contrast, with smectic-like regions dominated by intact molecular or large fragments and crystalline domains producing small alkyl fragments and ether-type species. These results provide spatially resolved evidence of a solid-liquid interface in a freeze-prepared organic liquid by APT and establish a reproducible workflow for probing local phase behavior in soft materials.

### [80] [Granular mass perturbations on the pulsar - supermassive black hole system](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04762)
*Zexin Hu,Lijing Shao*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 该研究通过数值模拟发现，银河系中心恒星质量黑洞的颗粒状尖峰结构会对绕人马座A*（Sagittarius A*）运行的射电脉冲星产生10–100秒的计时残差，这一数值远超传统预期，可能阻碍完整轨道相位连接计时解的构建。研究进一步指出，在仅利用近星点数据进行参数提取时，必须考虑光线传播中的参考系拖曳效应（frame-dragging effect），该效应能打破参数简并，将超大质量黑洞自旋的测量精度提升一个数量级。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用大规模数值模拟（numerical simulations），首次系统地研究了银心区域恒星质量黑洞构成的颗粒状尖峰（granular cusp）对脉冲星计时残差的扰动效应。

Result: 发现了10–100秒的拟合后计时残差，即使对于轨道周期Pb=0.5年的紧密轨道脉冲星，该残差也显著存在，与以往认知相反。如此大的计时残差可能导致显著的测量偏差，甚至阻碍构建全轨道的相位连接计时解（phase-connected timing solution）。

Conclusion: 在仅利用近星点数据提取超大质量黑洞参数的方案中，必须考虑光线传播中的参考系拖曳效应，该效应可以打破参数简并（parameter degeneracy），从而将黑洞自旋的测量精度提升一个数量级。

Abstract: Discovery and timing observations of a radio pulsar orbiting around Sagittarius A*, the supermassive black hole (SMBH) in our Galactic Centre (GC), will provide unprecedented opportunities of studying the SMBH spacetime, testing gravity theories, and probing the astrophysical environment in the GC. However, unknown mass distributions might cause timing residuals that are much larger than the timing precision. With extensive numerical simulations, for the first time we find that the perturbations caused by a granular cusp of stellar-mass black holes in the GC lead to post-fit timing residuals of 10-100 s, contrary to traditional wisdom, even for a pulsar in a tight orbit with an orbital period $P_b=0.5\,{\rm yr}$. Such a large timing residual can lead to significant measurement bias or even prevent construction of a phase-connected timing solution for the full orbit. We revisit the idea of extracting SMBH parameters only with data around periastron where the perturbation is small. Under the realistic phase-disconnected assumption, we point out that it is vital to consider the frame-dragging effect in the light propagation, which breaks parameter degeneracy and leads to an order of magnitude improvement for the measurement precision of the SMBH spin.

### [81] [Ulam Approximation for Nonautonomous Systems: Equivariant Measures and Linear Response](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02889)
*Stefano Galatolo,Valerio Lucarini,Isaia Nisoli*

Main category: math.DS

TL;DR: 本文研究非自治系统（nonautonomous systems）的统计性质近似问题：通过Ulam型有限维约化方法，证明了等变族（equivariant families）及其线性响应（linear response）可以经由粗粒化过程被严格逼近，并通过数值实验验证了时间依赖扩散模型中的收敛性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非自治系统在实际应用中普遍存在，但其统计性质的理解远不如自治系统（autonomous systems）深入，亟需发展严格的理论近似框架。

Method: 基于非自治系统的响应理论（response theory）最新成果，采用Ulam型有限维约化方法及更一般的有限元投影（finite-element projections）来逼近等变族及其线性响应；对转移算子具有正则化性质的系统，推导有限态Markov模型的线性响应收敛于原系统的投影线性响应。

Result: 证明了与经典Ulam方法及有限元投影相关的粗粒化过程能严格逼近具有记忆遗忘的序列系统（sequential systems）的等变族；对正则化系统，约化后的有限态Markov模型的线性响应收敛于原系统的投影线性响应；还通过时间依赖扩散模型进行了数值验证。

Conclusion: 该结果为在非自治复杂系统的统计性质研究中广泛使用的Markov近似方法提供了严格的理论基础，且相关近似结果在自治情形下也未曾在如此一般的形式下建立过。

Abstract: Despite the prevalence of nonautonomous systems in applications, their statistical properties are much less understood than in the autonomous setting. Building on recent results on response theory for nonautonomous systems, we study the approximation of equivariant families and of their linear response by Ulam-type finite-dimensional reductions. First, we show that coarse-graining procedures associated with the classical Ulam method, and more generally with suitable finite-element projections, provide rigorous approximation of equivariant families for sequential systems with memory loss. Second, for systems whose transfer operators are regularizing, we prove that the linear response of the reduced finite-state Markov model converges to the projected linear response of the original system. To the best of our knowledge, a general approximation result of this type has not previously been established in this form, even in the autonomous case. We complement the analysis with numerical experiments on simple but representative time-dependent diffusive models. These results provide a rigorous foundation for the use of Markov approximations in the study of statistical properties of nonautonomous complex systems which almost invariably relies on finite-scale and finite-precision descriptions of their states and dynamics.

### [82] [Exponential Time Differencing Schemes for a Phase-Field Model of Multicomponent Membranes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04347)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有工作中提出的多组分膜相场模型（phase-field model of multicomponent membranes）涉及膜变形与蛋白质分凝的耦合动力学，其数值求解面临高计算成本与稳定性挑战。本文旨在开发高效且稳定的数值格式来求解该模型。

Method: 针对固定相场膜，引入基于局域化函数（localization function）的几何自适应算子分裂方法（geometry-adapted operator splitting method），将表面Ohta-Kawasaki（OK）动力学重构为适合ETD积分的形式；结合有限差分离散化，构造一阶和二阶ETD格式。针对耦合系统，在基于FFT的谱框架（FFT-based spectral framework）下构建稳定化ETD格式，刚性线性项精确处理而非线性力化学耦合显式处理。采用窄带实现（narrow-band implementation）将表面计算限制在弥散膜区域以降低计算成本。

Result: 固定膜ETD格式被严格证明满足离散最大界原理（discrete maximum-bound principle）和无条件能量稳定性（unconditional energy stability）。数值实验验证了预测的时间精度、最大界保持与能量衰减行为，并实现了蛋白质驱动图案形成（pattern formation）与膜变形的三维稳定高效模拟。

Conclusion: 本文提出的ETD格式在理论上保证了最大界保持与能量稳定性，在计算上实现了高效的三维模拟，为多组分膜相场模型提供了可靠且可行的数值求解策略。

Abstract: In this paper, we develop and analyze exponential time differencing (ETD) schemes for a phase-field model of multicomponent membranes proposed in our previous work \cite{luo2025ohta}, in which membrane deformation is governed by a force-balance phase-field equation and protein segregation is described by a membrane-associated Ohta-Kawasaki (OK) dynamics. For a fixed phase-field membrane, we introduce a geometry-adapted operator splitting method based on the localization function, which reformulates the surface OK dynamics into a form suitable for ETD integration. The resulting first- and second-order ETD schemes, combined with finite-difference spatial discretization, are rigorously proved to satisfy a discrete maximum-bound principle and unconditional energy stability. For the coupled system, we construct stabilized ETD schemes in an FFT-based spectral framework, treating stiff linear terms exactly and nonlinear mechanochemical couplings explicitly. A narrow-band implementation further reduces the computational cost by restricting surface calculations to the diffuse membrane region. Numerical experiments confirm the predicted temporal accuracy, maximum-bound preservation, and energy decay for the fixed-membrane OK problem, and demonstrate stable and efficient three-dimensional simulations of protein-driven pattern formation and membrane deformation.

</details>

### [83] [Quantum String Interactions Revealed by Full Counting Statistics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04086)
*Chang-Yan Wang,Xue-Feng Zhang*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过全计数统计（FCS）推导出两条不可交叉量子弦之间的有效相互作用势，发现该势由纠缠熵控制，形式为 lnΔE(r) ~ -π²r²/(12S_ℓ)，并通过高精度数值计算验证了该理论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子弦作为多体量子物理中的扩展物体，其相互作用是一个基本问题，但即使在最简单的不可交叉硬核约束下，有效势的微观形式也难以确定，因为弦之间的相对距离本质上是非局域的。

Method: 利用全计数统计（full counting statistics, FCS）自然捕捉弦间距离的非局域性；对于两条硬核量子弦，通过识别两弦接触并跳回的虚过程，解析推导出FCS表达式，并利用FCS与纠缠熵（entanglement entropy）之间的关系得到有效势的渐近形式。

Result: 有效势具有由纠缠熵控制的渐近形式 lnΔE(r) ~ -π²r²/(12S_ℓ)，其中S_ℓ为量子弦两半之间的纠缠熵；通过高精度数值计算和有限尺寸FCS估计验证了该理论。

Conclusion: 全计数统计（FCS）为量子拓扑线缺陷之间的有效相互作用提供了直接途径，该框架可能进一步推广到高形式电荷（higher-form charge）系统。

Abstract: How quantum strings interact is a basic question for extended objects in quantum many-body physics. Even the simplest hard-core constraint (no crossing), can generate a nontrivial effective potential, whose microscopic form is difficult to determine because the relative distance between the strings is intrinsically nonlocal. Here we show that this nonlocality is naturally captured by full counting statistics (FCS). For two hard-core quantum strings, we derive an analytic FCS expression for the emergent interaction by identifying the virtual process in which the two strings touch and hop back. Using the FCS--entanglement relation, we find the effective potential has the entanglement-controlled asymptotic form $\lnΔE(r)\sim -π^2 r^2/(12 S_\ell)$ up to subleading terms, where $S_\ell$ is the entanglement entropy between the two halves of a quantum string. We confirm the theory using high-precision numerical calculations and finite-size FCS estimates. Our results reveal FCS as a direct route to effective interactions between quantum topological line-defects, which may also be extended to higher-form charge.

</details>


### [84] [Correlated States in Quantum Dot Clusters Coupled to a Common Superconductor](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04608)
*Martin Žonda,Jakub Rękas,Tobiáš Poláček,Jana Kodrlová,Vladislav Pokorný,Martin Friák*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过正则变换将常规量子点团簇-超导体耦合模型映射为粒子数守恒表示，利用神经网络量子态变分蒙特卡罗方法，结合精确对角化和密度矩阵重整化群，识别出三种相互作用区域：平凡超导单重态相、关联到有效海森堡模型的强关联区、以及在一维和二维中行为定性不同的临界中间区。在一维系统中，中间区出现单重态-双重态跃迁序列并在热力学极限下变得无带隙；二维团簇中则发现稳健的三重态基态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究耦合到公共超导体的规则量子点团簇（regular quantum dot clusters）的有效模型，探索超导能隙闭合机制及不同相互作用区域下的基态性质。

Method: 应用正则变换（canonical transformation）将系统映射到粒子数守恒（particle-number-conserving）表示；采用标准费米子神经网络量子态变分蒙特卡罗方法（fermionic neural-network quantum-state variational Monte Carlo methods）、精确对角化（exact methods）以及密度矩阵重整化群（density matrix renormalization group, DMRG）相结合。

Result: 超导能隙在一个高对称点处闭合；在有限非相互作用系统中该点对应不同性质单重态基态间的交叉。识别出三种相互作用区域：平凡超导单重态相、与有效海森堡模型（effective Heisenberg model）关联的强关联区、以及临界中间区。一维中间区呈现单重态-双重态跃迁（singlet-doublet transitions）序列且热力学极限下无带隙；二维团簇中存在稳健的三重态基态（triplet ground states）。

Conclusion: 标准的费米子神经量子态（fermionic neural quantum states）为关联超导纳米结构提供了一种高效计算途径。

Abstract: We study an effective model of regular quantum dot clusters coupled to a common superconductor. By applying a canonical transformation, we map the system onto a particle-number-conserving representation, making it directly accessible to standard fermionic neural-network quantum-state variational Monte Carlo methods. We show that the superconducting gap closes at a particular high-symmetry point, which, in finite non-interacting systems, corresponds to crossings between singlet ground states of different character. Combining exact methods, density matrix renormalization group, and neural quantum-state variational Monte Carlo calculations, we identify three distinct interacting regimes: a trivial superconducting singlet phase, a strongly correlated regime connected to an effective Heisenberg model, and a critical intermediate regime with qualitatively different behavior in one and two dimensions. In one-dimensional systems, the intermediate regime exhibits a sequence of singlet-doublet transitions and becomes gapless in the thermodynamic limit even for finite Coulomb interaction. In two-dimensional clusters, we find robust triplet ground states. Furthermore, our results demonstrate that relatively standard fermionic neural quantum states provide an efficient approach for correlated superconducting nanostructures.

</details>


### [85] [Magnetic structure of diamond EuTi2Al20](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04802)
*S. W. Lovesey,D. D. Khalyavin*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文基于实验证据，分析了EuTi₂Al₂₀中Eu离子在3.3 K以下有序化时出现的磁对称性（magnetic symmetries），证明其源于立方金刚石结构中的宇称混合（parity mixing），并通过d-f态混合形成的磁多极子（magnetic multipoles）区分两种正交候选对称性，提出共振X射线衍射（resonant x-ray diffraction）可作为鉴别手段。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有实验数据无法区分两种正交候选磁对称性（orthorhombic magnetic symmetries），其中一种为中心对称（centrosymmetric），另一种为极性（polar）。作者受首次提出金刚石EuTi₂Al₂₀低温磁对称性为正交晶系且包含时间反演（time reversal）的提议所驱动，旨在通过宇称奇异物态（parity-odd entities）的对称性分析解决这一区分难题。

Method: 通过分析Eu位置上d态与f态原子轨道混合所形成的磁宇称奇多极子（magnetic parity-odd multipoles），其分立对称性（discreet symmetries）与狄拉克磁单极子（Dirac monopole）匹配。利用共振X射线衍射图案中保留的母体立方金刚石结构宇称混合选择定则（selection rule），并结合晶体绕反射矢量的旋转（方位角扫描，azimuthal angle scan）以及X射线偏振（polarization）的完整描述，对两种候选对称性进行区分。

Result: 两种候选磁对称性在共振X射线衍射中对应的磁多极子不同，且允许出现的布拉格斑点（Bragg spots）位置存在差异。母体立方金刚石结构中的宇称混合选择定则得以保留，体心反平移（body-centre anti-translation）作为衍射图案的推论出现。

Conclusion: 基于对称性信息给出的衍射图案（包括方位角扫描和X射线偏振分析）能够区分两种候选正交磁对称性，为更深入的实验探测提供了理论指导。

Abstract: We study magnetic symmetries of EuTi2Al20 that appear in the ordering of Eu ions below a temperature at 3.3 K, according to an analysis of substantial experimental evidence [M. Kawamata et al., J. Phys. Soc. Japan. 95, 024701 (2026)]. They descend from the cubic diamond structure that depends explicitly on mixing of orbitals with different spatial parities, e.g., diamond s- and p-atomic states. The lattice (2, 2, 2) Bragg spot, for example, is lattice forbidden in the absence of parity mixing. Our work is motivated by a first proposal that low-temperature magnetic symmetries of diamond EuTi2Al20 are orthorhombic and belong to magnetic crystal classes that include time reversal. Body-centre anti-translation in diffraction patterns is a corollary. Current experimental data does not distinguish between two orthorhombic candidates, even though one is centrosymmetric and the other one is polar. We demonstrate that magnetic parity-odd entities (multipoles) formed by mixing d-and f-atomic states at europium positions, with discreet symmetries that match those of a Dirac monopole, are different for the two candidates. Moreover, the multipoles are visible in resonant x-ray diffraction patterns. The selection rule from parity mixing in the parent cubic diamond structure is preserved, and permitted Bragg spots are different for the two candidate magnetic symmetries. Our symmetry informed diffraction patterns include rotation of the crystal about the reflection vector (an azimuthal angle scan) and a full account of x-ray polarization to spur more revealing experiments.

</details>


### [86] [Stabilizing the parquet problem](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04936)
*Herbert Eßl,Stefan Rohshap,Marcel Gievers,Markus Wallerberger,Alessandro Toschi,Anna Kauch*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过分析雅可比矩阵（Jacobian）谱，系统研究了Parquet方程迭代解的稳定性，提出了判断物理不动点失稳的显式判据，揭示了虚假收敛问题并非由顶点发散引起，并引入了一种受控稳定化策略，成功在非微扰区域稳定了物理解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Parquet方程在中等至强相互作用区域的迭代求解常出现误导性的收敛问题，其根源尚不明确。本文旨在厘清这些收敛问题与顶点发散（vertex divergences）之间的关系，并提供稳定性判据及相应的稳定化方案。

Method: 采用阻尼不动点迭代（damped fixed-point iteration）方法求解Parquet方程，通过研究相应雅可比矩阵的谱来系统分析迭代解的稳定性；在此基础上引入受控稳定化策略（controlled stabilization strategy），并在零点模型和原子极限下的哈伯德模型（Hubbard model）中进行验证。

Result: 提出了Parquet迭代中物理不动点失稳的显式判据；证明误导性收敛问题在中间至强相互作用区域既可能出现在双粒子不可约顶点（two-particle irreducible vertex）发散时，也可能出现在其不发散的区域；揭示收敛问题并非直接由Luttinger-Ward泛函的多值解跨越引起；所提稳定化策略在非微扰区域甚至跨越多条发散线时仍能稳定地获得物理解。

Conclusion: Parquet算法中的虚假收敛问题并非顶点发散的直接后果；通过所提出的稳定化策略，可以在失稳区域有效恢复收敛至物理解，为强关联电子系统的Parquet计算提供了可靠的数值方法保障。

Abstract: We systematically analyze the stability of the iterative solution of the parquet equations by studying the spectrum of the Jacobian associated with the commonly used damped fixed-point iteration procedure. In this context, we provide an explicit criterion that determines when the physical fixed point of the parquet iteration becomes unstable. Importantly, we demonstrate that misleading convergence issues, observed in parquet calculation at intermediate-to-high interaction values, are not restricted to parameter regions where the two-particle irreducible vertex diverges, but can also arise in absence of vertex divergences. Hence, the misleading convergence issues of parquet-based algorithms are not directly caused by the crossings of two solutions of the (multivalued) Luttinger-Ward functional, that are associated with vertex divergences. Building on these insights, we introduce a controlled stabilization strategy that allows the convergence to the physical solution in the instability regimes. We apply this procedure to the zero-point model and the Hubbard model in the atomic limit, where we successfully stabilize the physical solution deep in the non-perturbative regime, even across multiple divergence lines.

</details>


### [87] [Coherent State Path Integral Monte Carlo](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05013)
*Riccardo Fantoni*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 提出一种基于Klauder相干态（coherent states）而非平面波展开高温密度矩阵（high temperature density matrix）的有限温度多体量子液体（many body quantum liquid）量子模拟新方法，该方法通过可调谐振子参数优化计算效率，并在刚性极限下恢复正确内能（internal energy）结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统路径积分方法（path integral methods）使用平面波（plane waves）展开高温密度矩阵，缺乏可调自由度；新方法旨在引入可调弹性常数（elastic constant）和质量参数，提升算法计算效率（computational efficiency）并允许更大的虚时间步长（imaginary timesteps）。

Method: 在John Rider Klauder提出的单粒子相干态（single particles coherent states）的超完备集（overcomplete set）上展开高温密度矩阵，替代传统路径积分中的平面波基；通过调节谐振子的弹性常数和质量来优化计算性能。

Result: 证明在极强谐振子（extremely stiff harmonic oscillator）极限下，内能趋于正确的期望值；并建议强谐振子可能允许使用更大的虚时间步长，这一额外自由度是传统路径积分方法不具备的。

Conclusion: 该算法通过谐振子参数提供了一个新的可调自由度，在保持正确热力学极限的同时有望提升计算效率，构成对传统路径积分模拟方法的有效补充。

Abstract: We propose a new quantum simulation method for a many body quantum liquid of identical particles at finite (non-zero) temperature. The new scheme expands the high temperature density matrix on the overcomplete set of single particles coherent states of John Rider Klauder instead of the usual plane waves as in conventional path integral methods. One is free to tune the elastic constant and/or the mass of the harmonic oscillator subtending the coherent states so as to maximize the computational efficiency of the algorithm. We prove that in the limit of an extremely stiff harmonic oscillator the results for the internal energy tends towards the correct expected values. Moreover we suggest that a stiff harmonic oscillator could allow the use of larger (imaginary) timesteps. This additional degree of freedom is the characteristic feature of our new algorithm and is not available in more conventional path integral methods.

</details>


### [88] [$η$-pairing in metallic and particle-hole asymmetric systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05092)
*Philipp Werner,Aaram J. Kim,Lei Geng*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过非平衡动力学平均场论（nonequilibrium dynamical mean field theory）结合强耦合杂质求解器，发现η-配对（η-pairing）在强关联大Mott能隙体系中，对填充变化和双占据-空穴密度不对称具有鲁棒性，但受有效温度不对称性显著抑制；在光掺杂金属态中，η-配对可在正有效温度和低能准粒子带粒子数反转条件下实现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 光诱导超导态已在若干关联材料中被观测到，而η-配对是实现非热超导的一种有前景的理论机制。然而，此前数值研究局限于大能隙Mott绝缘体中的粒子-空穴对称态，而实验却是在强关联金属体系中进行的，因此有必要探索η-配对在非粒子-空穴对称体系及光激发金属态中是否存在。

Method: 采用稳态非平衡动力学平均场论（nonequilibrium dynamical mean field theory, DMFT），结合最高至三阶的强耦合杂质求解器（strong-coupling impurity solver）进行数值研究。

Result: 在强关联大Mott能隙区域且有效双占据-空穴温度较低时，η-配对对总填充变化及双占据-空穴密度不对称具有鲁棒性；但有效双占据与空穴温度的不对称会强烈抑制序参量（order parameter）。在具有三峰局域态密度（local density of states）结构的光掺杂金属体系中，当双占据和空穴温度为正且低能准粒子带存在粒子数反转时，η-配对可以实现。

Conclusion: η-配对在非粒子-空穴对称的大能隙Mott体系中仍然稳定存在，但其对有效温度不对称性敏感；在光掺杂金属态中也能实现，前提是满足正温度条件和低能准粒子带粒子数反转。

Abstract: Light-induced superconducting-like states have been reported in several classes of correlated materials. From a theoretical point of view, the induction of $η$-pairing is a promising route to nonthermal superconductivity. Numerical studies of photo-doped Mott systems revealed $η$-pairing states with very high effective critical temperatures. These investigations were however restricted to particle-hole symmetric states in large-gap Mott insulators, while the experiments were performed on strongly correlated metallic systems. It is thus relevant to explore if $η$-pairing also exists in non-particle-hole symmetric setups and in photo-excited metallic states. Here we use steady-state nonequilibrium dynamical mean field theory combined with a strong-coupling impurity solver up to third order to investigate this issue. We find that in the strongly correlated regime with large Mott gap, and for low effective doublon and holon temperatures, $η$-pairing is robust against changes in the total filling and an imbalance in the doublon and holon density. An asymmetry in the effective doublon and holon temperatures can however strongly suppress the order parameter. In photo-doped metallic systems with a three-peak structure in the local density of states, $η$-pairing can be realized in set-ups with positive doublon and holon temperatures and a population inversion in the low-energy quasi-particle band.

</details>


### [89] [Soliton-antisoliton pairs in the supersymmetric gapped phase of an interacting Majorana chain](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05095)
*Alberto Nocera,Mobin Shakeri,Armin Rahmani,Ian Affleck*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文研究马约拉纳费米子（Majorana fermions）强相互作用链实现超对称三临界伊辛相（supersymmetric tricritical Ising phase）时，超对称性（SUSY）在能隙相中的表现，发现SUSY诊断量在伊辛侧发散后衰减至零，而最低激发态由束缚局域马约拉纳模式的孤子-反孤子对构成，形成非局域狄拉克费米子（Dirac fermion），并区分偶奇费米子宇称（fermion parity）的本征态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超对称性（supersymmetry, SUSY）在三临界点（tricritical point）的行为已清楚，但在进入对称破缺的有序能隙相（gapped phase）后其表现尚不明确。本文旨在回答两个关键问题：SUSY如何在能隙相中显现，以及该相中激发态的性质。

Method: 在热力学极限（thermodynamic limit）下，分析一个常规的SUSY诊断量（diagnostic）——该量在三临界点处保持有限——在伊辛（Ising）侧立即发散，并在深入能隙相后连续衰减至零。同时聚焦于超对称能隙区域的最低激发态，研究其组成与量子数特征。

Result: SUSY诊断量在进入伊辛侧后立即发散，随后向能隙相深处衰减至零，表明SUSY在该区域仍有残留。最低激发态由分隔不同有序区域的孤子-反孤子对（soliton-antisoliton pair）构成；每个孤子束缚一个局域马约拉纳模式（localized Majorana mode），两者共同形成一个非局域狄拉克费米子（nonlocal Dirac fermion）。该狄拉克模式的占据与否区分了具有偶费米子宇称（even fermion parity）和奇费米子宇称（odd fermion parity）的本征态。

Conclusion: 超对称性在能隙相中以诊断量发散后渐进衰减的方式持续存在；能隙相的最低激发态并非普通准粒子，而是由束缚马约拉纳模式的孤子-反孤子对组成的非局域狄拉克费米子，其费米子宇称标记了不同的本征态分支。

Abstract: A strongly interacting chain of Majorana fermions realizes the supersymmetric tricritical Ising phase, with supersymmetry (SUSY) extending into a symmetry-broken ordered phase adjacent to the tricritical point. Although the signatures of SUSY at the tricritical point are well understood, their behavior in the gapped phase remains less clear. Here, we address two key questions: how SUSY manifests in the gapped phase and what is the nature of the excitations in this phase. We show that, in the thermodynamic limit, a conventional SUSY diagnostic that remains finite at the tricritical point diverges immediately on the Ising side, yet decays continuously to zero deeper in the gapped phase, signaling the persistence of SUSY. Focusing on the lowest excited states in the supersymmetric gapped regime, we find that the excitations consist of soliton-antisoliton pairs separating distinct ordered regions. Each soliton binds an emergent localized Majorana mode, and together the pair forms a nonlocal Dirac fermion. The occupation of this Dirac mode distinguishes eigenstates with even and odd fermion parity.

</details>

### [90] [Contact interaction treatment of π and ρ elastic and transition tensor form factors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04255)
*Ke-Yu Guo,Ke-Xin Zeng,Xin-Yu Bai,Chen Chen,Craig D. Roberts*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文采用对称性保持的矢量×矢量接触相互作用（vector×vector contact interaction, SCI），在两种正则化方案下预言了π介子、ρ介子及其标量和轴矢量双夸克伙伴的张量荷（tensor charge）与形状因子（form factor）。结果显示两种方案差异微小；尽管形状因子较“硬”，但其红外行为在物理上可靠。关键结果包括：π介子张量荷约0.36，其张量形状因子半径与电荷半径几乎相同；ρ介子张量荷约为质子的80%；双夸克张量荷与形状因子在定性上与π、ρ伙伴相似。这些预测可作为未来更接近量子色动力学（QCD）研究的基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在无法直接从第一性原理QCD（量子色动力学）精确计算强子张量荷与形状因子时，需要一种对称性保持的有效模型方法提供可靠的理论预言，并检验其正则化方案的敏感性，以为未来更接近QCD的研究提供基线参考。

Method: 采用对称性保持的矢量×矢量接触相互作用（SCI）框架，利用两种不同的正则化（regularisation）方案处理红外发散，计算π介子、ρ介子及其标量和轴矢量双夸克伙伴的张量荷与弹性及跃迁形状因子。

Result: 两种正则化方案下结果差异很小；SCI框架下的形状因子虽然整体偏“硬”，但红外行为在物理上可靠。具体数值：π介子张量荷约为0.36，其张量形状因子半径与π介子电荷半径几乎相同；ρ介子张量荷约为质子的80%；双夸克张量荷与形状因子在定性上与其π、ρ伙伴相似。

Conclusion: SCI预言本身具有物理意义，同时可作为未来采用与QCD联系更紧密的方法进行研究的基准（baseline）。

Abstract: Predictions for tensor charges and form factors, elastic and transition, involving $π$- and $ρ$-mesons and their scalar and axialvector diquark partners, are delivered using a symmetry-preserving treatment of a vector*vector contact interaction (SCI). Two distinct SCI regularisation schemes are employed, with the results showing little sensitivity. Although, as typical in SCI analyses, the form factors are stiff; their infrared behaviour may be considered physically reliable. Notable amongst related quantities are the following: the pion tensor charge is approximately $0.36$ and the associated tensor form factor radius is practically the same as the pion charge radius; the $ρ$-meson tensor charge is roughly 80% of that for the proton; and diquark tensor charges and form factors are semiquantitatively alike with those of their $π$, $ρ$ partners. In addition to being interesting in themselves, the SCI predictions can serve as baselines for future studies with a closer connection to QCD.

### [91] [Thermodiffusive coupled-transport phenomena in dense quark matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04539)
*Kamaljeet Singh,Kangkan Goswami,Raghunath Sahoo*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文基于2+1味Nambu–Jona–Lasinio模型，在有限温度和夸克化学势下研究了热密夸克物质中的耦合输运系数（Soret效应与Dufour效应），通过求解相对论玻尔兹曼输运方程并结合弛豫时间近似，揭示了这些系数在手征对称性恢复区域附近的敏感行为，首次系统性地提供了致密夸克物质中交叉耦合输运性质的认识。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 耦合输运现象（coupled-transport phenomena）能揭示介质中热、电荷与粒子流之间的内在关联，相较于独立输运过程可提供更深入的微观动力学信息。本研究旨在理解手征对称性恢复（chiral symmetry restoration）区域附近耦合输运系数的复杂行为，填补致密夸克物质中交叉耦合输运性质的系统性研究空白。

Method: 采用2+1味Nambu–Jona–Lasinio（NJL）模型描述有限温度与夸克化学势下的夸克物质；通过求解相对论玻尔兹曼输运方程（relativistic Boltzmann transport equation），并利用弛豫时间近似（relaxation time approximation）结合温度依赖的截面来估计Soret系数和Dufour系数。

Result: 标度化的Soret系数与Dufour系数随温度和夸克化学势变化，在QCD相图（QCD phase diagram）上表现出对手征相变（chiral phase transition）的敏感性。研究结果首次提供了致密夸克物质中交叉耦合输运性质（cross-coupled-transport properties）的系统性洞察。

Conclusion: 耦合输运系数对手征相变高度敏感，为理解致密夸克物质中的交叉耦合输运行为提供了初步的系统性认识。

Abstract: Coupled-transport phenomena reveal that heat, charge, and particle flows are intrinsically interconnected, providing deeper insight into the microscopic dynamics of a medium than independent transport processes. We study the behavior of the coupled-transport coefficients in hot and dense quark matter within the framework of the 2+1 flavor Nambu--Jona--Lasinio model at finite temperature and quark chemical potential. These coefficients characterize coupled-transport phenomena, where particle diffusion is driven by temperature gradients (Soret effect) and heat flow is induced by gradients in chemical potential (Dufour effect). These coefficients are estimated by solving the relativistic Boltzmann transport equation using the relaxation time approximation with temperature-dependent cross sections. We study the scaled Soret and Dufour coefficients as functions of temperature and quark chemical potential across the QCD phase diagram. We aim to understand the intricate behavior of the coupled-transport coefficients near the chiral symmetry restoration region. Our results indicate that coupled-transport coefficients are sensitive to the chiral phase transition and provide the first systematic insight into the cross-coupled-transport properties in dense quark matter.

### [94] [Hydrodynamics of the Fermi-Pasta-Ulam-Tsingou chain](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04674)

TL;DR: 本文对FPUT链的流体动力学（hydrodynamics）进行了教学综述，推导了从欧拉（Euler）到纳维-斯托克斯-傅里叶（Navier-Stokes-Fourier）层次的流体动力学方程，并通过微观模拟检验了这些方程对非平衡初态（如畴壁和冲击波）时间演化的预测能力，发现某些情况下欧拉方程预测与模拟吻合良好，但在其他情形下存在显著偏差，表明耗散和噪声（noise）的作用普遍重要。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 从质量、动量和能量三个守恒律出发，推导FPUT链在欧拉层次的流体动力学方程，进而引入耗散和热传导效应得到纳维-斯托克斯-傅里叶方程；随后选取畴壁（domain walls）和冲击波（blasts）等非平衡初始条件，通过微观数值模拟与流体动力学预测进行对比验证。

Result: 部分非平衡初态（如某些畴壁情形）的微观模拟结果与欧拉方程预测吻合良好；但在另外多种情形下，微观模拟与欧拉预测存在显著偏差，表明耗散和噪声对系统的动力学行为具有重要影响。

Conclusion: FPUT链的流体动力学描述在部分情形下有效，但耗散和噪声的作用普遍不可忽略，因此需要超越欧拉层次（即考虑纳维-斯托克斯-傅里叶层次）的流体动力学理论来更准确地描述该系统的非平衡演化。

Abstract: We provide a pedagogical review of the hydrodynamics of the FPUT chain. There are three hydrodynamic fields corresponding to the conservation of mass, momentum and energy. We provide physically motivated derivations of the hydrodynamic equations at the levels of Euler and then Navier-Stokes-Fourier. Next we consider examples to test as to how successful the hydrodynamic description is in predicting the observed time evolution of nonequilibrium initial conditions such as domain walls and blasts. We find that in some cases there is good agreement of microscopic simulations with predictions from the Euler equations while, in several other cases, there is significant departure from the Euler predictions suggesting that the role of dissipation and noise is important in general.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Many-body localization(MBL) provides a mechanism by which isolated interacting quantum systems with disorder can avoid thermalization unlike ergodic systems satisfying the eigenstate thermalization hypothesis(ETH). Many-body localized systems retain signatures of their initial conditions at long times, whereas systems obeying ETH lose such information as they approach thermal equilibrium. Studying Non-equilibrium dynamics across ETH-MBL crossover is an important problem in condensed matter physics. Adiabatic control of parameters in interacting disordered systems provides a powerful framework to investigate MBL phases and their dynamical robustness. Using exact diagonalization and time-dependent numerical methods we study the effects of adiabatically ramped interactions in a disordered spin-1/2 XXZ chain, a paradigmatic model for exploring the many-body localization transition. By monitoring diagonal entropy density and entanglement entropy density growth across various ramp speeds, and system sizes. Our study incorporates Finite-size effects of spectral observables to probe the transition between ergodic and localized phases. The numerical results show that localized dynamical behavior remains largely intact under sufficiently slow ramp evolution, while increasing the driving rate promotes stronger excitation generation and larger entropy growth. This trend highlights the strong dependence of nonequilibrium adiabatic dynamics in disordered interacting quantum many-body systems.

### [96] [On singular solitons of the KP equation and the Go-diagrams](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04663)
*Shilong Huang*

Main category: nlin.SI

TL;DR: 本文证明KP方程（Kadomtsev-Petviashvili equation）的规则孤子解可由完全非负格拉斯曼流形（totally nonnegative Grassmannian）分类，并利用顶点算子（vertex operator）的乘积构造组合解；虽然组合后通常导致奇异解，但通过引入Go-图（Go-diagrams）——即Le-图（Le-diagrams）的推广，这些奇异解得以参数化，Go-图源于格拉斯曼流形的Deodhar分解（Deodhar decomposition）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有研究证明KP方程的规则孤子解与完全非负格拉斯曼流形之间存在分类关系，且顶点算子是构造孤子解的有效工具。本文旨在探索多个规则孤子解经顶点算子乘积组合后的行为特性。

Method: 通过顶点算子的乘积对多个规则孤子解进行组合，并分析组合后解的性质；利用Postnikov提出的Le-图参数化完全非负元素，进而引入Go-图来参数化组合后产生的奇异解。

Result: 规则孤子解的顶点算子乘积组合通常导致奇异解；这些奇异解可由Go-图参数化，Go-图是Le-图的推广，并出现在格拉斯曼流形的Deodhar分解中。

Conclusion: 本文建立了奇异孤子解与Go-图之间的参数化对应关系，将完全非负格拉斯曼流形中Le-图的分类框架扩展至Deodhar分解中的Go-图，从而深化了对KP方程解结构的理解。

Abstract: It has been proven that real and regular soliton solutions of the KP equation are classified in terms of the totally nonnegative Grassmannian. It is well known that vertex operators can be used to construct soliton solutions. In this paper, we consider several regular soliton solutions and study their combinations through products of vertex operators. In general, the resulting solutions become singular. Totally nonnegative elements are parametrized by the Le-diagrams introduced by Postnikov. We show that the resulting singular solutions can be parametrized by Go-diagrams, which extend Le-diagrams and arise in the Deodhar decomposition of the Grassmannian.

</details>


### [97] [Novel periodic solutions and rogue waves of the defocusing scalar and coupled Ablowitz-Ladik systems on a nonzero background](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05123)
*Francesco Coppini,Barbara Prinari*

Main category: nlin.SI

TL;DR: 本文应用Hirota双线性方法（Hirota's bilinear method）于散焦色散区（defocusing dispersion regime）的标量和耦合Ablowitz-Ladik系统（Ablowitz-Ladik systems），在背景振幅0<ρ<1假设下，发现了包括奇异解、规则呼吸子（regular breather）、暗孤子-呼吸子相互作用、新型Akhmediev型离散呼吸子以及怪波解（rogue wave solutions）在内的一系列新解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将Hirota双线性方法推广到Ablowitz-Ladik系统的散焦色散区，探索该方法能否揭示超出传统逆散射变换（inverse scattering transform）框架的新解，特别是非暗孤子类型的离散非线性波解。

Method: 采用Hirota双线性方法对标量和耦合Ablowitz-Ladik系统进行求解；在标量情形建立Hirota参数与逆散射变换谱参数之间的对应关系，并通过选择超出离散暗孤子（discrete dark soliton）范围的Hirota参数来构造新解；在耦合系统中引入背景离散反向传播平面波（counter-propagating plane waves）来推导Akhmediev型呼吸子。

Result: 标量情形下发现了一类时间周期解（time-periodic solutions）的规则呼吸子，可在晶格上始终保持正则（regular）；揭示了暗孤子与规则呼吸子之间、以及两个规则呼吸子之间的相互作用。耦合系统中导出了规则且空间周期性的Akhmediev型离散呼吸子（Akhmediev-type discrete breathers）；在该呼吸子周期趋于无穷（波数趋于零）的极限下，获得了耦合Ablowitz-Ladik系统的新型怪波解。

Conclusion: Hirota双线性方法能够有效揭示Ablowitz-Ladik系统在散焦色散区中超出传统暗孤子解的新奇非线性波结构，包括规则呼吸子和怪波解，为离散非线性系统的可积性和解的分类提供了新视角。

Abstract: In this paper we apply Hirota's bilinear method to the scalar and coupled Ablowitz-Ladik systems in the defocusing dispersion regime under the assumption of a background amplitude $0<ρ<1$. We first establish, in the scalar case, the correspondence between the Hirota's parameters and the spectral parameters of the inverse scattering transform. Then we show that when the Hirota parameter associated to the discrete eigenvalue is chosen outside the range corresponding to a discrete dark soliton, novel solutions of the Ablowitz-Ladik system emerge. In general, these solutions are singular, but there exists a class of time-periodic solutions for which it is possible to choose the soliton parameters so that the breathers remain regular on the lattice for all times. We also discuss the interactions between a dark soliton and a regular breather, and between two regular breathers. For the coupled Ablowitz-Ladik system, by including in the background discrete, counter-propagating plane waves, we use Hirota's method to derive novel Akhmediev-type (i.e., space-periodic) discrete breathers which are regular for all times. Finally, taking the limit of the discrete Akhmediev breathers as the period approaches infinity (i.e., as the wavenumber approaches zero) we obtain novel rogue wave solutions of the coupled Ablowitz-Ladik system.

</details>

### [98] [Discrete signaling mediates chaotic regularization in recurrent neural networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04426)
*Jan Bauer,Christian Keup,Jonathan Kadmon,Moritz Helias*

Main category: q-bio.NC

TL;DR: 本文发展了一个理论框架，将递归网络的微观混沌与神经表征的宏观几何联系起来，证明混沌动态在保持全局光滑性的同时引入局部粗糙度（local roughness），从而解释了混沌皮层回路如何维持稳定的群体编码（population codes）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 皮层回路（cortical circuits）本质上处于内在混沌（intrinsic chaos）状态，微小输入变化即可导致神经响应发散，然而群体编码却能随感官刺激（sensory stimuli）平滑变化并形成连贯的表征流形（representational manifolds）。本文旨在回答混沌网络如何维持稳定编码这一核心矛盾。

Method: 将核方法（kernel methods）与动态平均场理论（dynamical mean-field theory）相结合，建立连接微观混沌动态与宏观神经表征几何的理论框架。

Result: 混沌动态在局部尺度引入尖锐扭曲（sharp distortions），即局部粗糙度，同时在大尺度刺激变化上保持全局光滑性（global smoothness）；该结构特性作为内在正则化器（intrinsic regularizer），在增强泛化能力的同时保持表达力；混沌网络自然产生幂律谱特征（power-law spectral signatures），与皮层记录（cortical recordings）的实验观察高度吻合。

Conclusion: 研究结果解释了混沌脉冲网络（chaotic spiking networks）如何维持平滑且可微的群体编码，并建立了一个连接网络动态、计算结构与记录的神经活动的统一理论框架。

Abstract: Cortical circuits operate in a regime of intrinsic chaos, where even tiny changes in input can lead to divergent neural responses. Yet, remarkably, population codes in the brain vary smoothly with sensory stimuli, forming coherent representational manifolds. How can chaotic networks sustain such stable coding? Here, we develop a theoretical framework that links the microscopic chaos of recurrent networks to the macroscopic geometry of neural representations. Combining kernel methods with dynamical mean-field theory, we show that chaotic dynamics induce local roughness (introducing sharp distortions at small scales) while preserving global smoothness across larger stimulus variations. This structural property acts as an intrinsic regularizer, enhancing generalization while maintaining expressivity. Moreover, we show how chaotic networks naturally produce power-law spectral signatures, closely matching experimental observations in cortical recordings. These results explain how chaotic spiking networks can sustain smooth, differentiable population codes and establish a theoretical framework linking network dynamics, computational structure, and recorded neural activity.

</details>

### [99] [Spectral criteria for generalization in unsupervised Hebbian nets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04651)
*Elena Agliari,Paulo Duarte Mourão,Alberto Fachechi,Pierpaolo Vivo*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文研究了一种无监督赫布网络（unsupervised Hebbian network），该网络基于含噪隐空间真实向量构建神经元间的成对相互作用。通过随机矩阵理论（random matrix theory）与复制方法（replica methods）推导出相应相互作用矩阵的渐近谱（asymptotic spectrum），揭示泛化能力的出现由尖锐的谱相变（spectral transition）控制。当谱呈现分离双团块（two separated bulks）时，网络能够从含噪样本中重构隐真实向量；当合并为单团块（single-bulk phase）时，此区分能力丧失。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统Hopfield模型被设计为记忆设备，而本文旨在探索一类无监督赫布网络能否用于提取隐结构并在训练集之外实现泛化。核心动机是理解此类网络从含噪数据中学习潜在真实模式（ground-truth vectors）的机制与极限。

Method: 结合随机矩阵理论（random matrix theory）与复制方法（replica methods）推导相互作用矩阵的渐近谱（asymptotic spectrum）。通过分析谱结构随数据集质量和大小的变化，揭示泛化能力与谱相变（spectral transition）之间的定量关系。

Result: 谱结构呈现两种相：分离双团块（two separated bulks）编码信息方向与噪声方向，合并单团块（single-bulk phase）则失去此区分。谱分裂（spectral split）的出现由数据集质量与大小控制，并与正则化（regularization）耦合时预测网络的重构能力。

Conclusion: 谱分裂的出现预测了网络从含噪样本中重构隐真实向量（ground-truth vectors）的能力。该工作为理解无监督赫布网络（unsupervised Hebbian network）的泛化机制提供了理论框架，建立了谱分析与学习能力之间的直接联系。

Abstract: We consider an unsupervised Hebbian network where the pairwise interactions among neurons are built on noisy realizations of hidden ground-truth vectors. Unlike classical Hopfield models, designed as memory devices, this class of networks can be employed to extract latent structure and generalize beyond the "training" set. By combining random matrix theory and replica methods, we derive the asymptotic spectrum of the corresponding interaction matrix and show that the onset of generalization is controlled by a sharp spectral transition. Depending on the quality and the size of the accessible dataset, the spectrum displays either two separated bulks, encoding informative and noisy directions, or a merged single-bulk phase where such distinction is lost. We show that, when coupled with regularization, the emergence of such a spectral split predicts the network's capability to reconstruct the ground-truth vectors from corrupted samples.

</details>


### [100] [Finite-Basis Duality Estimate for the Surface-Code Threshold under Correlated Bit-Flip Errors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04723)
*Masayuki Ohzeki*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文基于有限基对偶性（finite-basis duality）和图形多项式（graph-polynomial）策略，通过使用环面基（toroidal bases）上的周期和扭曲周期扇区（periodic and twisted-periodic sectors），改进了Chubb-Flammia模型在空间相关比特翻转噪声下的表面码临界点估计，得到$p_c = 0.10348$。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Chubb和Flammia针对空间相关比特翻转噪声（spatially correlated bit-flip noise）下的表面码（surface code）引入了一个统计力学模型，并通过对偶性分析给出了临界点$p_c=0.1004(6)$，但该单一方程估计与蒙特卡洛（Monte Carlo）估计存在轻微偏差，因此需要更精确的临界点估计。

Method: 采用有限基对偶性（finite-basis duality）和图形多项式（graph-polynomial）策略，在环面基（toroidal bases）上使用周期扇区（periodic sectors）和扭曲周期扇区（twisted-periodic sectors）进行分析。

Result: 得到了改进的临界点估计值，$p_c = 0.10348$。

Conclusion: 相比Chubb-Flammia基于单一方程对偶性分析的估计，本文的方法提供了更精确的临界点结果。

Abstract: We apply finite-basis duality to a statistical-mechanical model introduced by Chubb and Flammia for the surface code under spatially correlated bit-flip noise. Their mapping gives a random-bond Ising model with both two-body edge interactions and four-body face interactions. The single-equation estimate based on the duality analysis is slightly deviated from their Monte Carlo estimate \(p_c=0.1004(6)\). Following the finite-basis and graph-polynomial strategy, we instead use periodic and twisted-periodic sectors on toroidal bases. We have obtained an improved estimate of the critical point, $p_c = 0.10348$.

</details>


### [101] [Percolation Criticality of Amorphous-Amorphous Transitions in Compressed Glasses](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04748)
*Julien Perradin,Simona Ispas,Ricardo V. Paredes,Anwar Hasmy,Bernard Hehlen*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文利用逾渗理论（percolation theory）研究压缩二氧化硅玻璃从低密度到高密度的转变，通过大规模分子动力学模拟揭示了不同配位多面体簇的临界逾渗行为，并发现其临界指数偏离随机逾渗标准值，暗示可能存在刚性逾渗（rigidity percolation）机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解压缩二氧化硅玻璃中低密度到高密度结构转变的机制，尤其是在系统尺度上的结构基元（structural motifs）涌现与生长过程。

Method: 采用大规模分子动力学模拟（molecular dynamics simulations），系统尺寸高达10^6个原子，压力范围为0–35 GPa；引入长程描述符（long-range descriptors）以补充传统的局域与中程结构度量；基于逾渗理论分析SiO_Z-SiO_Z簇（随配位数Z增加）和SiSi_z-SiSi_z簇（采用非键合方法）。

Result: 发现了SiO_Z-SiO_Z簇的临界逾渗转变（critical percolation transitions），临界指数略偏离标准随机逾渗关联，且高配位多面体的偏差比四面体更显著；键合与非键合两种分析路径互补，有助于揭示键合玻璃（如SiO_2）与非键合玻璃（如非晶冰）之间的共同机制。

Conclusion: 压缩二氧化硅玻璃的结构转变可由逾渗理论统一描述，其临界行为偏离随机逾渗，暗示受刚性逾渗机制调控；键合与非键合方法的结合为理解压力诱导结构转变提供了更完整的视角。

Abstract: The low-to-high-density transition in compressed silica glass is investigated using percolation theory. Large-scale molecular dynamics simulations of SiO$_2$ glasses, with system sizes of up to 10$^6$ atoms and pressures ranging from 0 to 35 GPa, were carried out to investigate the emergence of structural motifs and their growth to system-spanning length scales under compression. On this basis, we introduced long-range descriptors that complement conventional local and medium-range structural measures. The results reveal critical percolation transitions of SiO$_Z$-SiO$_Z$ clusters with increasing coordination number $Z$. The critical exponents slightly deviate from the standard (random) correlation, a behavior that seems to be more pronounced for higher coordinated polyhedra than for tetrahedra, suggesting a possible rigidity percolation mechanism. SiSi$_z$-SiSi$_z$ clusters were also analyzed using the non-bonded approach. Bonded and non-bonded approaches complement each other in a particularly illuminating way for describing pressure-induced structural transformations and common mechanisms shared by bonded glasses, such as SiO$_2$, and non-bonded glasses, such as amorphous ice.

</details>


### [102] [Experimental observation of three-dimensional Anderson localization of electromagnetic waves](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04897)
*Antton Goïcoechea,Alexey Yamilov,Clément Ferise,Sergey E. Skipetrov,Hui Cao,Matthieu Davy*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在凝聚态物理中，安德森局域化是一个重要现象，但此前所有尝试在三维系统中实现光（微波）的安德森局域化均受到实验假象（experimental artifacts）的干扰，因此迫切需要提供无歧义的实验证明。

Method: 研究使用无序金属聚集体样品，通过改变金属体积分数（volume fraction），对透射光束宽度（transmitted beam width）进行标度分析，以区分扩散行为（diffusive behavior）与局域化行为（localized behavior）。

Result: 实验清晰展示了扩散与局域化行为之间的差异，标度分析结果与理论和数值结果高度吻合，提供了三维安德森局域化的明确实验证据。

Conclusion: 该实验确证了三维安德森局域化的存在，为基础研究和实际应用开辟了新途径。

Abstract: A prominent phenomenon in contemporary condensed matter physics is Anderson localization -- suppression of wave propagation in disordered systems as a result of interference effects. Despite being observed with various types of waves over the years, all prior attempts to reach Anderson localization of light in three-dimensional systems have been hampered by experimental artifacts. Here, we report an unambiguous experimental proof of three-dimensional Anderson localization of microwaves in disordered metal aggregates. By studying samples with different metal volume fractions, we show a clear difference between diffusive and localized behaviors, and the latter is confirmed by a scaling analysis of transmitted beam width in excellent agreement with theoretical and numerical results. Our demonstration opens avenues for both fundamental studies and practical applications of this extraordinary phenomenon.

### [103] [Leggett-Garg test inequality with spin and flavour neutrino oscillations in a constant magnetic field](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04412)
*I. A. Monroy,S. D. Madrid*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本论文研究在恒稳横向磁场中，中微子味（ν_e^L↔ν_μ^L）和自旋（ν_e^L↔ν_e^R）振荡对Leggett-Garg不等式（LGI）的违反情况，发现强磁场下两种振荡均存在LGI被违反的长度区间ΔL，并由关联函数K_3和K_4定量表征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Leggett-Garg不等式（LGI）作为量子力学与经典预言之间的一项标志性检验，目前在其与中微子振荡（neutrino oscillation）特别是磁场背景下振荡行为的结合研究尚不充分。因此，本文旨在考察恒稳横向磁场中中微子味及自旋振荡是否违反LGI，以揭示其量子特性。

Method: 研究通过分析中微子味振荡（ν_e^L↔ν_μ^L）和自旋振荡（ν_e^L↔ν_e^R）在恒稳横向磁场（constant transverse magnetic field）中的动力学行为，计算关联函数（correlator functions）K_3和K_4来检验LGI是否被违反。

Result: 对于强磁场系统，两种振荡情形均存在某些长度区间ΔL，其中LGI被违反，违反程度通过关联函数K_3和K_4进行定量衡量。

Conclusion: 恒稳横向磁场中的中微子味和自旋振荡可以展现违反Leggett-Garg不等式的非经典行为，且该效应在强磁场条件下尤为显著，进一步支持了中微子振荡系统的量子本质。

Abstract: The Leggett-Garg inequality (LGI), an analogue of Bellś inequality involving correlations of measurements of one observable on a system at different times, stands as one of the hallmark tests of quantum mechanics against classical predictions. In this work, we investigate its implications in the context of neutrino flavour ($ν_{e}^{L}\leftrightarrowν_μ^{L}$) and spin ($ν_{e}^{L}\leftrightarrowν_{e}^{R}$) oscillations in the presence of a constant transverse magnetic field. For systems with strong magnetic fields, we show that, for both cases, there are length regions $ΔL$ where the LGI is violated, as quantified by the correlator functions $K_{3}$ and $K_{4}$.

### [104] [Spontaneous irreversibility and objective thermalization in stochastic modifications of quantum theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2504.16197)
*Aritro Mukherjee*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文提出量子理论是一种有效理论，需要引入随机扩展来修正，从而使宏观孤立量子系统能够客观地实现热化（thermalization），并构建了一个具有涨落-耗散关系（fluctuation-dissipation relation）保障一致性的随机量子理论模型，该模型统一描述了自发对称性破缺、量子态约化及客观量子热化等现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 孤立量子系统的确定性、时间反演对称动力学与热力学系统不可逆平衡之间存在根本矛盾。标准方法通过对可观测量或状态空间施加主观限制来调和这一矛盾，但未能解释单个宏观量子系统如何动态地达到平衡。

Method: 论文将量子理论视为一种有效理论（effective theory），认为在热力学极限（thermodynamic limit）下需要修正，并在此基础上构建了一个随机扩展（stochastic extension）的量子理论框架。

Result: 该随机量子理论与微观系统的量子力学几乎等同，但允许单个宏观孤立系统一般性地客观热化。模型满足涨落-耗散关系，保证了范数守恒、能量守恒、无超光速信号传递以及微正则平衡（microcanonical equilibrium）的出现。进一步纳入客观坍缩（objective collapse）后，可实现一个可证伪的自发普遍不可逆性理论。

Conclusion: 该模型描述了宏观量子系统的自发对称性破缺（spontaneous symmetry breaking）、量子态约化（quantum state reduction）和客观量子热化（objective quantum thermalization）的动力过程，并在系综层面实现了融合玻恩定则（Born's rule）与微正则平衡的混合统计行为。

Abstract: The deterministic and time-reversal symmetric dynamics of isolated quantum systems is at odds with irreversible equilibration observed in generic thermodynamic systems. Standard approaches at a reconciliation employ subjective restrictions on the space of observables or states and do not explain how a single macroscopic quantum system achieves equilibrium dynamically. We instead argue that quantum theory is an effective theory and requires corrections to accurately describe systems approaching the thermodynamic limit. We construct a stochastic extension of quantum theory which is practically identical to quantum mechanics for microscopic systems, yet allows individual macroscopic and isolated systems to objectively thermalize, generically. A fluctuation-dissipation relation guarantees physical consistency including norm preservation, energy conservation, no superluminal signalling and the emergence of microcanonical equilibrium. We further discuss the inclusion of objective collapse, thereby realizing a falsifiable theory of spontaneous universal irreversibility which describes the quantum-to-classical crossover dynamics of macroscopic quantum systems. The dynamics of the model describe spontaneous symmetry breaking, quantum state reduction and objective quantum thermalization for individual systems, while realizing emergent hybrid statistics for ensembles that integrate Born's rule and microcanonical equilibrium.

</details>


### [105] [Quantum error correction with the toric code](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04079)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 中性原子量子计算平台在高量子比特数、高操作保真度和任意量子比特连接性方面具有优势，可支持高效纠错方案。然而，目前尚缺乏可扩展至任意深度的重复纠错演示，该工作旨在填补这一空白。

Method: 采用环形量子纠错码，通过中间电路测量提取症候信息，并在丢失量子比特时进行替换，包括从量子比特库中重新加载原子以实现无限持续相干操作。

Result: 在多达90个纠错周期内表征了逻辑错误率，验证了逻辑信息可通过多轮量子比特重新加载得以保存；在最多8轮症候提取中比较了两种不同码距，发现更大码距对应的绝对逻辑错误率更低。

Conclusion: 该工作首次实验证明了中性原子量子计算平台上可扩展至任意深度的重复纠错能力，为未来基于逻辑量子比特的量子计算架构奠定了基础。

Abstract: Quantum computing platforms based on arrays of tweezer-confined neutral atoms have recently emerged as a competitive modality thanks to a direct path toward high qubit count, rapidly advancing operation fidelities, and their ability to execute circuits with arbitrary qubit connectivity. These features will enable the use of efficient error correction schemes with high encoding-rates, time-efficient decoding, and resource-efficient architectures based on transversal gates. With these goals in mind, recent state of the art neutral atom demonstrations focus on the transition from the use of physical qubits to error-corrected logical qubits, but to date there has been no demonstration of repeated error correction scalable to arbitrary depth. Here, we demonstrate many cycles of syndrome extraction in a toric quantum error correcting code, using mid-circuit measurement and replacement of lost qubits, including reloading of a qubit reservoir for indefinite coherent operation. We characterize the logical error rate after up to 90 cycles, showing that logical information can be preserved through multiple rounds of qubit reloading. Comparing two distances of the code up to 8 rounds of syndrome extraction shows a lower absolute logical error rate for the larger distance code.

</details>


### [106] [Arbitrary manipulation of nuclear spins in hexagonal boron nitride](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04497)

Method: 利用电子自旋作为辅助量子比特（auxiliary qubit），施加背景磁场和多音调连续驱动（multi-tone continuous drive），通过Hahn回波脉冲序列（Hahn echo pulse sequence）抑制非期望的电子-核相互作用，并采用适当的RF驱动实现目标量子门。

Conclusion: 该方案为hBN中V_B^-在量子计算中的实际应用奠定了基础。

Abstract: Due to its localized nature and controllability, the negatively charged boron vacancy centers (V$_\text{B}^-$) in hexagonal boron nitride (hBN) are a promising spin platform for accessing its neighboring nuclei with potential for performing quantum computational tasks. However, the methods of utilizing and manipulating the nuclear spins are still lacking. In this work, we propose a protocol for the preparation of single- and multi-qubit gates on the nuclear spins, utilizing the electron spin as an auxiliary qubit. By applying a background magnetic field and a multi-tone continuous drive, we show that the electron spin coupling to the nuclei can be efficiently engineered. This allows for suppressing the undesired electron-nuclear interactions through the Hahn echo pulse sequence. The target gates are then implemented by employing proper RF drives. Our numerical results for realistic parameters show gate fidelities as high as $99\%$ for single-qubit and $95\%$ for multi-qubit gates. With the gate execution durations being less than $300$ ns, our protocol evades electron spin decoherence effects. Therefore, our scheme sets the stage for the practical application of V$_\text{B}^-$ in hBN for quantum computation purposes.

### [107] [Extremely slow scaling of minimal Hamming distance in quantum sampling data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04558)
*P. S. Golubev,I. A. Iakovlev,V. V. Mazurenko*

TL;DR: 本文提出利用唯一比特串集合的平均最小汉明距离（average minimal Hamming distance）作为普适量子度量，通过其呈现的幂律行为（power-law behavior）参数，在稀疏测量数据下表征量子态复杂度并识别量子相变（quantum phase transitions），无需大量统计积累或显式计算物理可观测量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子数据来源多样（如噪声量子处理器、冷原子模拟器、变分神经网络态等），但受限于指数级增长的希尔伯特空间（Hilbert space），可获得的测量数据往往极为稀疏，导致系统表征能力存在根本性局限。

Method: 提出以唯一比特串集合的平均最小汉明距离作为鲁棒度量，该度量呈现出普适的幂律行为；通过真实实验与模拟的多个实例进行验证。

Result: 幂律参数能够可靠地捕捉量子态的复杂度，并在无需大量统计积累或显式计算物理观测量的条件下，从有限的量子信息中识别量子相变。

Conclusion: 该方法使得完全不同的量子实验能够在单一框架内进行分析，显著降低了对数据量和物理先验知识的要求。

Abstract: Quantum data can be obtained from a diverse range of sources, including direct measurements from noisy quantum processors, cold-atom simulators, and classical approximations such as variational neural-network states. However, our ability to characterize these systems is fundamentally limited, as the available measurement data is often sparse compared to the exponentially large Hilbert space of the system. To address this, we propose using the average minimal Hamming distance calculated for a set of unique bitstrings as a robust metric revealing a universal power-law behaviour. Through various examples of real experiments and simulations, we show that the power-law parameters reliably capture the complexity of quantum states and identify quantum phase transitions from limited quantum information, without the need for accumulating extensive statistics or explicitly calculating physical observables. This enables the analysis of completely different quantum experiments within a single framework.

</details>


### [108] [Pushing the Classical Frontier of 1D Fermi-Hubbard Quench Dynamics Beyond Current Quantum Simulations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04771)
*Roman Rausch,Sukhbinder Singh,Saeed S. Jahromi,Augustine Kshetrimayum,Roman Orus*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本研究通过利用 $\mathrm{U}(1)\times\mathrm{SU}(2)$ 对称性与 GPU 加速张量收缩，将时变变分原理（TDVP）模拟的键维度（bond dimension）推至 $\chi\approx62{,}000$，在费米-哈伯德模型（Fermi-Hubbard model）的整个模拟窗口内实现了完全收敛的结果，并将量子-经典性能差距从 Q-CTRL 声称的 $3000\times$ 缩小至约 $36\times$。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子优势（quantum advantage）的建立需与最优经典模拟进行对比。Q-CTRL 团队在一维费米-哈伯德模型的量子模拟中声称 $3000\times$ 加速，但其经典基准（baseline）在高纠缠区域 $t\in[5.2,6]$ 未能收敛，留下了最关键的验证窗口未被检验，因此需要更强大的经典模拟方法对该量子优势声明进行严格检验。

Method: 采用完整的 $\mathrm{U}(1)\times\mathrm{SU}(2)$ 对称性（symmetry）来约束费米-哈伯德哈密顿量的张量网络表示，并结合 GPU 加速的张量收缩（tensor contractions），在四块 NVIDIA H200 GPU 上运行时变变分原理（Time-Dependent Variational Principle, TDVP）模拟，将键维度提升至 $\chi\approx62{,}000$。

Result: 在整个模拟窗口（包括此前未解决的高纠缠区域 $t\in[5.2,6]$）实现了完全收敛的结果，并将经典模拟推进到 $t=7$，超越了量子硬件实验和此前任何已验证的全波函数经典演化。在与 Q-CTRL 最佳经典运行相当的键维度下，GPU 实现在约 100 分钟内完成，将 Q-CTRL 声称的 $3000\times$ 量子优势压缩至约 $36\times$。

Conclusion: 这些结果显著缩小了量子-经典性能差距，并为大规模量子模拟的张量网络基准测试（tensor-network benchmarking）建立了新标准，表明在严格的经典模拟下，此前宣称的量子优势可能被大幅高估。

Abstract: Establishing quantum advantage requires comparison against the best achievable classical simulation. The Q-CTRL team recently simulated quench dynamics of the one-dimensional Fermi-Hubbard model on an IBM processor, completing a $L=60$ evolution to time $t=6$ in under three minutes and claiming a $3000\times$ speedup over classical Time-Dependent Variational Principle (TDVP) simulation at bond dimension $χ=4096$. Their classical benchmark required over 160 hours on a CPU cluster, failed to converge in the high-entanglement regime $t\in[5.2,6]$, and left the most challenging window of the experiment unverified. Here, we push the boundaries of classical simulation by exploiting the full $\mathrm{U}(1)\times\mathrm{SU}(2)$ symmetry of the Fermi-Hubbard Hamiltonian combined with GPU-accelerated tensor contractions. Reaching bond dimensions up to $χ\approx62{,}000$ on four NVIDIA H200 GPUs -- among the largest ever achieved in TDVP simulations and fifteen times larger than Q-CTRL's classical baseline -- we achieve fully converged results across the entire simulation window, including rigorous certification of the previously unresolved high-entanglement regime $t\in[5.2,6]$. We further advance the classical frontier to $t=7$, which lies beyond the quantum hardware experiment and any previously verified classical evolution of the full wavefunction. At the bond dimension comparable to Q-CTRL's best classical run, our GPU implementation completes in $\sim\!100$ minutes, directly reducing the claimed $3000\times$ quantum advantage to $\sim\!36\times$. These results substantially narrow the quantum-classical performance gap and establish a new standard for tensor-network benchmarking of large-scale quantum simulations.

### [109] [Experimentally probing the Quantum Physics in the Inverted Harmonic Oscillator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05125)
*Si-Cong Ji,Philipp Schüttelkopf,Nataliia Bazhan,Federica Cataldini,Mohammadamin Tajik,Frederik S. Møller,Igor Mazets,Sebastian Erne,Jörg Schmiedmayer*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文利用玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体（Bose-Einstein condensate）在AtomChip上实现了反转谐振子（inverted harmonic oscillator, IHO）动力学，通过相空间层析成像（phase-space tomography）观测到亚真空压缩（sub-vacuum squeezing）达10.6 dB，并验证了量子相干性在远超出初始膨胀时间尺度上的可逆性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子系统通过不稳定不动点（unstable fixed point）时，局域动力学约化为反转谐振子（IHO），该过程会沿一个正交分量指数放大、另一个压缩，从而将微观零点涨落（zero-point fluctuations）放大为宏观量子态。本文旨在利用超冷原子平台，在受控条件下实验实现这一不稳定量子动力学，并检验其量子相干可逆性。

Method: 在AtomChip上制备玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体（BEC），利用射频缀饰（radio-frequency dressing）将横向简谐囚禁势翻转为反转谐振子势。通过相空间层析成像追踪演化量子态的完整Wigner函数（Wigner function），并通过时间反演IHO演化检验相干可逆性。

Result: 观察到亚真空压缩达10.6(1.3) dB；两个子云团之间的物质波干涉（matter-wave interference）证实了量子相干性在远超出初始膨胀时间尺度上仍然保持。

Conclusion: 该实验确立了超冷原子作为不稳定量子动力学的一个洁净、可控的多体平台，为基于时间反演相干性认证的力传感（force sensing）以及涨落放大（如暴胀场动力学中的量子涨落放大）的类比研究开辟了路径。

Abstract: When a quantum system passes through an unstable fixed point the local dynamics reduces to the inverted harmonic oscillator (IHO). It exponentially amplifies along one quadrature while squeezing the other, producing macroscopically extended quantum states from microscopic zero-point fluctuations. We realize this dynamics with a Bose-Einstein condensate on an AtomChip. Radio-frequency dressing flips the transverse harmonic confinement into an IHO. Through phase-space tomography we follow the full Wigner function of the evolving quantum state, observe sub-vacuum squeezing of 10.6(1.3) dB, and test coherent reversibility by time-reversing the IHO evolution. Matter-wave interference between the two daughter clouds confirms quantum coherence over timescales far beyond the initial expansion. Our experiment establishes ultra-cold atoms as a clean, controlled, many-body platform for unstable quantum dynamics opening a route to force sensing with time-reversal-based coherence certification and to analog studies of the amplification of quantum fluctuations in inflationary field dynamics.

### [110] [Modeling Rozansky-Witten Theory with Sheaves of Categories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04502)
*Enoch Yiu*

Main category: math.AG

TL;DR: 本文通过将 Rozansky-Witten 理论建模为 Perf(X×𝔸¹) 上模层的范畴层，推广了 Tamarkin 的奇异支撑方法，从而构造了 T^*X 上的混合拉格朗日子流形对应的对象，并验证了 Hom 空间由合适的矩阵分解给出。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的 Rozansky-Witten 理论主要处理 T^*X 中的锥形拉格朗日子流形（如余法丛），但缺乏适用于非锥形拉格朗日（hybrid Lagrangians）的系统构造方法。Tamarkin 利用层（sheaves）在 X×ℝ 上的奇异支撑（singular support）处理非锥形拉格朗日，但该方法与 Rozansky-Witten 理论之间的桥梁尚未建立。因此，本文旨在填补这一空白。

Method: 本文利用 Perf(X×𝔸¹) 上的模层（modules）作为工具，将 Rozansky-Witten 理论建模为 X×𝔸¹ 上的范畴层（sheaves of categories）。具体而言，构造了由混合拉格朗日（hybrid Lagrangians）所对应的 Rozansky-Witten 理论对象，其中图拉格朗日（graphs）和余法丛（conormals）是特例。

Result: 成功构造了 T^*X 上由混合拉格朗日给出的 Rozansky-Witten 理论对象，并证明这些对象之间的 Hom 空间由合适的矩阵分解（matrix factorizations）给出，作为理论一致性的验证。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了 Rozansky-Witten 理论与 Tamarkin 层论方法之间的平行关系，拓展了可处理的拉格朗日子流形的类型，并通过矩阵分解验证了构造的正确性。

Abstract: We model Rozansky-Witten theory of $T^*X$ using modules over $\operatorname{Perf}(X\times\mathbb{A}^1)$ viewed as sheaves of categories over $X\times\mathbb{A}^1$. This is in parallel to Tamarkin's approach to nonconic Lagrangians in $T^*X$ via the singular support of sheaves on $X\times\mathbb{R}$. More specifically, we construct the objects of Rozansky-Witten theory of $T^*X$ given by hybrid Lagrangians of which graphs and conormals are special cases. As a consistency check, we show that $\operatorname{Hom}$s between such objects are given by suitable matrix factorizations.

### [111] [Multiparametric Quantum Sensing of Liquids Using NV Centres and Tethered Magnetic Nanoparticles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04064)
*Johannes Fiedler,Martin Møller Greve,Justas Zalieckas*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 提出一种基于氮-空位（NV）中心磁测量、弛豫测量以及表面锚定磁性纳米颗粒的非侵入式多参数液体分析新概念；通过将不同DNA链修饰的磁性纳米颗粒固定于金刚石表面，利用其热运动对液体环境的敏感性，将单个液体的物理化学性质映射到高维量子响应向量上，实现并行、无标记的液体表征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统液体分析方法通常提供单一标量可观测量（scalar observable），难以同时获取液体的多种物理化学性质（如粘度、分子吸附、化学相互作用）。该研究旨在利用量子传感（quantum sensing）与表面异质性（surface heterogeneity）相结合，发展一种非侵入式、多参数（multiparametric）的液体分析新途径。

Method: 将磁性纳米颗粒（magnetic nanoparticles）通过DNA链（DNA strands）锚定到金刚石表面，形成纳米尺度机械振荡器（nanoscale mechanical oscillators）。这些颗粒的热驱动运动受周围液体环境影响，产生随时间变化的磁场，耦合到近表面的氮-空位（NV）中心。利用光探测磁共振（optically detected magnetic resonance, ODMR）或自旋相干时间（spin coherence time）的变化检测该磁场信号。通过对金刚石表面进行空间图案化，修饰不同长度、序列或化学修饰的DNA链，使单个液体映射到高维量子响应向量（high-dimensional quantum response vector）上。

Result: 液体的粘度变化、分子吸附或化学相互作用会以区域特异性（region-specific manner）方式影响磁性纳米颗粒的动力学行为，从而在金刚石表面不同功能化区域产生差异化的传感响应。论文给出了相关的物理换能机制（physical transduction mechanism）和标度关系（scaling relations），并基于现有宽场NV磁测量（wide-field NV magnetometry）与弛豫测量（relaxometry）方法评估了实验可行性。

Conclusion: 该平台将量子传感与表面异质性结合，为并行、无标记的液体表征提供了一种多功能新途径，有望实现单一液体的多参数、高维度特征提取。

Abstract: We propose a new concept for non-invasive, multiparametric liquid analysis based on nitrogen-vacancy (NV) centre magnetometry, relaxometry and surface-tethered magnetic nanoparticles. Magnetic nanoparticles are anchored to a diamond surface via DNA strands, forming nanoscale mechanical oscillators whose thermally driven motion is strongly influenced by the surrounding liquid environment. The resulting time-dependent magnetic fields couple to near-surface NV centres and are detected via optically detected magnetic resonance or changes in spin coherence time. By spatially patterning the diamond surface with regions functionalised by DNA tethers of different lengths, sequences, or chemical modifications, a single liquid is mapped onto a high-dimensional quantum response vector rather than a single scalar observable. Changes in viscosity, molecular adsorption, or chemical interactions modify the dynamics of magnetic nanoparticles in a region-specific manner, enabling differential sensing across the surface. We outline the physical transduction mechanism, discuss relevant scaling relations, and assess experimental feasibility using established wide-field NV magnetometry and relaxometry methods. The proposed platform combines quantum sensing with surface heterogeneity, offering a versatile route toward parallel, label-free liquid characterisation.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 本研究表明莫尔工程在延长自旋寿命方面具有显著效果，为未来的量子传感（quantum sensing）和信息处理（information processing）提供了新的可能性。

Abstract: The spin degree of freedom is a fundamental quantum mechanical attribute with implications spanning from magnetism to quantum computing. Consequently, the relaxation of spin states for extended, Bloch electrons in solids has been studied for decades as it defines many of their properties and applications. We show that moiré patterns in layered materials can extend spin relaxation times by two orders of magnitude to 1 millisecond and beyond. This is achieved by suppressing spin mixing for electrons in 2D semiconductor heterostructures, particularly in the MoSe2/WS2 system, as we elucidate both experimentally and theoretically. The extended longitudinal lifetime facilitates spin alignment over 50% using only nanowatt levels of optical power. Our findings highlight the potential of moiré engineering for future quantum sensing and information processing.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 实验对比了两种基于电子隧穿电流的原初温度计——库仑阻塞温度计（CBT）和散粒噪声温度计（SNT），二者仅依赖于玻尔兹曼常数 kB 和基本电荷 e，无需已知参考温度或外部校准参数，在20 mK至235 mK范围内进行互比较。

Conclusion: 两种基于基本物理常数且仅需电学测量的原初温度计在低温区间具有良好的一致性，但需注意测量频率对SNT精度的影响。

Abstract: Since the redefinition of the kelvin in 2019, new methods of primary thermometry have been considered to replace the currently agreed temperature scale in the very high and low temperature limits. These new methods should provide improved uncertainties and, most importantly, a more direct link to the definition of the kelvin. In the low temperature ranges it is possible to realize thermometers that do not require any known reference temperature or external calibration parameters. We present an experimental comparison of two such thermometers: the Coulomb Blockade Thermometer (CBT) and the Shot Noise Thermometer (SNT). Both thermometers measure temperature hinging only on the natural constants $k_\mathrm{B}$, and $e$. Furthermore both of them are based on electron tunneling current and, thereby, need only electrical measurements, enhancing the practicality. CBT and the SNT are inter-compared in a range of 20 mK to 235 mK. The results show that the agreement of SNT and CBT is approximately within 2.5 % in this range. Basic measurement uncertainty is analyzed and we show that uncertainty in the measurement frequency can cause significant error. to temperature measurement of the SNT at low temperatures where finite frequency plays a role.

### [114] [Breaking the width-scaling limit in high-performance atomically thin 2D nanoribbon transistors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04219)
*Sameer Kumar Mallik,Adrian Christiansen,Saroj P. Dash*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本研究通过使用超小尺寸二维半导体（2DSC）纳米带晶体管突破宽度缩放瓶颈，在15纳米沟道宽度下实现了导通电流密度提升（单层MoS₂达230%，双层达170%），并保持了高开关比、改进的迁移率和阈值电压稳定性，为晶体管的终极缩放提供了新路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用超小尺寸的二维半导体（two-dimensional semiconductor, 2DSC）纳米带（nanoribbon）晶体管，将沟道宽度缩小至15纳米，并基于原子级薄单层和双层二硫化钼（MoS₂）材料进行实验验证。

Result: 与传统宽度缩放导致电流密度下降的规律相反，单层和双层MoS₂纳米带晶体管的导通电流密度分别提升了230%和170%，并在最窄沟道（15纳米）下趋于饱和；同时保持了同类尺寸器件中最高的开关比（on/off ratio），迁移率和阈值电压稳定性也有所改善。

Conclusion: 二维半导体纳米带晶体管在更窄的沟道宽度下展现出增强的性能，打破了传统的宽度缩放规则，有望推动晶体管的终极缩放（ultimate scaling）。

Abstract: State-of-the-art transistors have been successfully scaled the gate lengths and channel thicknesses down to 5 nm for high-performance and energy-efficient information processing. However, reducing channel width below 40-50 nm remains a bottleneck, as dangling bonds, edge disorder, and lateral depletion suppress drive current and degrade device performance. Here, we break this width-scaling wall using ultra-scaled two-dimensional semiconductor (2DSC) nanoribbon transistors down to 15 nm. In contrast to the conventional scaling rule of degradation of current density upon width scaling, our atomically-thin monolayer and bilayer molybdenum disulfide nanoribbon transistors exhibit enhancement of on-current density of up to 230% and 170%,respectively, followed by a saturation for the narrowest channels down to 15 nm. The ultra-narrow nanoribbon transistors maintain the highest on/off ratios reported so far for similar device dimensions, with improved mobility and threshold-voltage stability, indicating reduced edge scattering and depletion with a stronger electrostatic control. These findings lead to a breakthrough in width scaling rules using 2DSC nanoribbons with enhanced performance at narrower channel widths, which is promising for the ultimate scaling of transistors.

### [115] [Perfect Nonreciprocal Axion-polaritons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04341)
*Abhinava Chatterjee,Chao-Xing Liu*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出动态轴子（dynamical axion）准粒子通过磁有序参量的涨落产生，并与电磁场耦合形成轴子-极化激元（axion-polaritons）。研究表明，在静态外电场和外磁场下，轴子-极化激元出现非互易色散（nonreciprocal dispersion），并存在完美非互易（perfect nonreciprocity）区域，即一个传播方向的光子完全退耦，而反向光子强烈杂化。该非互易色散可表现为光隔离器（optical isolator），为轴子准粒子的探测提供了实验可行的途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索动态轴子准粒子与电磁场的耦合行为，并揭示其是否能在特定条件下产生非互易传播特性，从而为轴子准粒子的实验探测提供新的物理机制和可行方案。

Method: 基于磁有序参量涨落产生的动态轴子与电磁场的耦合理论，分析在静态外电场和外磁场作用下轴子-极化激元的色散关系，并通过方向依赖的轴子-光子耦合（axion-photon coupling）推导非互易色散的存在条件。

Result: 发现轴子-极化激元在适当外场下呈现非互易色散 ω(k) ≠ ω(-k)；识别出完美非互易区域，其中正向传播光子与轴子完全退耦，反向传播光子则发生强烈杂化；该效应可实现光隔离器功能。

Conclusion: 非互易轴子-极化激元可作为探测轴子准粒子的有力工具，并为其实验检测提供了可行路径。

Abstract: Dynamical axion describes a massive axion quasiparticle that arises from fluctuations of the magnetic order parameter. These fluctuations couple to electromagnetic fields, forming axion-polaritons -- collective modes that are physically magnon-polaritons. We show that under appropriate static external electric and magnetic fields, axion-polaritons acquire a nonreciprocal dispersion, $ω(\textbf{k}) \neq ω(-\textbf{k})$, arising intrinsically from direction-dependent axion-photon coupling. Strikingly, we identify a regime of \textit{perfect nonreciprocity} in which the photon propagating in one direction is completely decoupled from the axion while the counter-propagating photon hybridizes strongly. Furthermore, the nonreciprocal dispersion manifests as an optical isolator -- a device transmitting light preferentially in one direction. Our results establish nonreciprocal axion-polaritons as a powerful probe of axion quasiparticles and suggest experimentally accessible routes for their detection.

</details>


### [116] [When Screening Current Controls Ferroelectric Switching: From Field-Limited to Current-Limited Regimes under an SPM Tip](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04481)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统观点将铁电体中的探针诱导切换视为由畴壁动力学控制的场驱动过程，但这种框架在解释纳米尺度压电滞后测量中观察到的畴壁定律偏离（breakdown of intrinsic domain-wall laws）时存在不足。作者旨在提出一个更通用的视角，揭示屏蔽电流动力学在极化反转中的核心约束作用。

Method: 结合局域切换实验（local switching experiments）与有限元模拟（finite-element simulations），通过分析电荷注入与空间电荷限制弛豫（space-charge-limited relaxation）过程，识别并验证屏蔽电流限制的切换机制。

Result: 发现极化反转的速率和畴生长（domain growth）的标度关系由电荷注入及其空间电荷限制的弛豫过程主导；该机制能自然解释不同体系间切换行为的表观变化（regime changes）以及纳米尺度压电滞后测量中本征畴壁定律的表观失效。

Conclusion: 屏蔽电流（screening current）应被视为铁电反转的隐藏控制参数（hidden control parameter），通过调控电流可实现确定性纳米尺度畴工程（deterministic nanoscale domain engineering）。该框架不仅重新诠释了探针诱导切换的物理图像，还为跨材料的铁电反转控制提供了新的实用手段。

Abstract: Tip-induced switching in ferroelectrics is commonly framed as a field-driven process controlled by domain-wall kinetics. Here we argue for a more universal viewpoint: under a scanning probe, polarization reversal is fundamentally constrained by how fast screening charge can be supplied and redistributed. By combining local switching experiments with finite-element simulations, we identify a screening-current-limited mechanism in which charge injection and its space-charge-limited relaxation set the pace of switching and the scaling of domain growth. This framework naturally explains regime changes and the apparent breakdown of intrinsic domain-wall laws often inferred in the nanoscale piezoelectric hysteresis measurements. Beyond a reinterpretation of tip switching, the results position screening currents as a hidden control parameter of ferroelectric reversal across materials, turning current regulation into a practical handle for deterministic nanoscale domain engineering.

### [119] [Curvature-Controlled Infrared Regularization of Crystalline Membranes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04614)
*Pablo A. Morales,Pavel Castro-Villarreal*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文发现负高斯曲率（negative Gaussian curvature）能够正则化晶体膜（crystalline membranes）的红外区域，通过面内声子与外在曲率之间的线性耦合，将反常粗糙化（anomalous roughening）替换为曲率控制的饱和，并推断不存在皱折相（crumpling phase）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 晶体膜在红外区域存在反常粗糙化等非平庸行为，标准平直或正曲率几何无法有效控制这些红外发散。本文旨在探索负高斯曲率几何是否能够正则化晶体膜的红外区域，并改变其弹性与声子行为。

Method: 采用嵌入弹性（embedded elasticity）的协变形式化（covariant formulation），在格林应变（Green strain）中引入法向声子（normal phonon）与外在曲率（extrinsic curvature）之间的对称性要求的线性耦合。通过对面内声子（in-plane phonons）进行积除（integrating out），将这一耦合转化为对逆弯曲响应（inverse flexural response）的有限二次贡献。

Result: 反常粗糙化被曲率控制的饱和（curvature-controlled saturation）所取代，该机制在最小双曲片（minimal hyperbolic patches）上仍然存活。双曲几何（hyperbolic geometry）在平坦红外区域达到之前便先发制人地阻止了反常弹性，暗示不存在皱折相。此外，相同的高斯阶耦合允许声音在红外区域传播。

Conclusion: 负高斯曲率通过几何机制有效正则化晶体膜的红外行为，消除反常粗糙化与皱折相，并维持红外声传播。该结果揭示了曲率几何在调控低维材料弹性响应中的关键作用。

Abstract: We show that negative Gaussian curvature regularizes the infrared sector of crystalline membranes. In a covariant formulation of embedded elasticity, the Green strain contains a symmetry-required linear coupling between the normal phonon and extrinsic curvature. Integrating out the in-plane phonons converts this coupling into a finite quadratic contribution to the inverse flexural response. Anomalous roughening is thereby replaced by curvature-controlled saturation, and the mechanism survives on minimal hyperbolic patches. Hyperbolic geometry preempts anomalous elasticity before the flat infrared regime is reached, implying the absence of a crumpling phase. The same Gaussian-order coupling admits sound propagation in the infrared.

Abstract: Interlayer excitons in transition metal dichalcogenide (TMD) heterobilayers possess a permanent electric dipole moment and long recombination lifetimes, making them a promising platform for exploring excitonic many-body physics. The emission exhibits a blueshift with increasing excitation power, indicating repulsive dipole-dipole interactions. ### [121] [Local-to-global heating crossover in chains of nanomagnets: A two-scale analytical framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04724)
*H. Kachkachi*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该论文建立了一个双尺度解析框架，用于研究一维纳米磁体系统在均匀交变磁场中的产热与热输运过程。通过纳米尺度的局域热源描述与粗粒化后的宏观方程，推导出从局域加热到全局加热的交叉条件，并应用于磁热疗系统，发现实际参数下系统处于集体加热 regime，局域温差仅为微开量级。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解纳米磁体在交变磁场中的产热与热扩散行为，特别是局域热效应与集体加热效应之间的转换机制，对于优化磁热疗（magnetic hyperthermia）等应用至关重要。现有模型缺乏在多尺度上统一描述热产生与输运的解析框架，且未能系统量化粗粒化过程的近似误差。

Method: 提出一种双尺度解析形式：在纳米尺度，每个纳米磁体被视为局域化的、与温度相关的热源，由磁响应、偶极相互作用（dipolar interaction）及与基质的界面耦合共同决定，用纳米尺度体积损耗系数 $L_m$ 表征；通过时空平均得到粗粒化的组装尺度方程，引入宏观损耗系数 $L_N$。利用模态分解（modal decomposition）在狄利克雷（Dirichlet）和诺伊曼（Neumann）边界条件下精确求解两个尺度的方程，并推导局域-全局加热交叉的显式条件。粗粒化过程被严格推导，近似误差被量化。通过克努森数（Knudsen number）分析验证连续傅里叶描述的适用性。

Result: 对于典型磁热疗系统（如水中的磁铁矿纳米磁体），实际参数使系统处于集体加热（collective heating） regime，局域温度变化约为微开（~μK）水平，目前实验上无法分辨。克努森数分析表明 $\mathrm{Kn} \ll 1$，证实连续傅里叶描述在无定形聚合物和水性基质中的有效性。建立了由产热、扩散、偶极耦合与层级损耗之间竞争所控制的局域-全局加热交叉条件，其通过空间相关长度（spatial correlation length）和温度方差进行量化。

Conclusion: 该双尺度形式为分析纳米磁体系统中的多尺度热传输提供了严格的解析工具，揭示了实际磁热疗系统中局域温差极小而系统表现为集体加热的本质，证明了宏观傅里叶热传导方程在纳米磁体系统中的适用性，并为优化加热效率提供了理论依据。

Abstract: We develop a two-scale analytical formalism to study heat generation and thermal transport in one-dimensional systems of nanomagnets subjected to a uniform alternating magnetic field. At the nanoscale, each nanomagnet acts as a localized, temperature-dependent heat source governed by its magnetic response, dipolar interactions, and interfacial coupling to the matrix, characterized by a nanoscale volumetric loss coefficient $L_m$. After spatial and temporal averaging, we obtain a coarse-grained assembly-scale equation with effective heating terms and a macroscopic loss coefficient $L_N$.
  Using modal decomposition, we solve both equations exactly under Dirichlet and Neumann boundary conditions and establish explicit conditions for a local-to-global heating crossover; this is governed by the competition between heat generation, diffusion, dipolar coupling, and hierarchical losses. The crossover is quantified through the spatial correlation length and temperature variance, with stability criteria incorporating both diffusion and nanoscale losses. The coarse-graining procedure is derived rigorously, and its systematic approximation errors are quantified.
  For prototypical magnetic hyperthermia systems, such as magnetite nanomagnets in water, our formalism reveals that realistic parameters place these systems firmly in the collective heating regime, with local temperature variations at the $\simμ$K level, which is currently unresolvable experimentally. The continuum Fourier description used here is validated by a Knudsen-number analysis ($\mathrm{Kn} \ll 1$ for amorphous polymer and aqueous matrices).

</details>


### [122] [Monitored chaotic scattering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04794)
*C. W. J. Beenakker,J. Sánchez Fernán,J. Tworzydło*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文将混沌散射的随机矩阵理论（random-matrix theory）扩展至受时间分辨测量监控的量子点（quantum dots）系统。通过从圆形系综（circular ensemble）中提取散射矩阵，构造了用于监控多体密度矩阵演化的Kraus算符系综，并在单粒子扇区中得出可代数求解的离散时间量子主方程，最后通过数值求解并与封闭形式的随机矩阵预言进行比较，验证了所提出的监控粒子均分规则（equipartition rule）猜想。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有随机矩阵理论主要用于描述混沌散射的静态或平均性质，尚未系统适用于受时间分辨测量实时监控的量子点动力学过程，因此需要拓展该理论框架以描述监控条件下的演化与电荷转移统计。

Method: 从圆形系综中采样散射矩阵，构造相应的Kraus算符（Kraus operators）系综以描述监控演化；在单粒子扇区中对测量结果进行代数求和，得到离散时间量子主方程（discrete-time quantum master equation）；并提出了一个基于均分规则（equipartition rule）的封闭形式随机矩阵预言。

Result: 通过数值求解离散时间量子主方程，获得了电荷转移统计特性，并将其与基于均分规则的封闭形式随机矩阵预言进行了定量比较。

Conclusion: 数值结果与随机矩阵预言的比对表明，所提出的监控粒子均分规则猜想是有效的，为受测量监控的量子点电荷统计提供了简洁的理论描述。

Abstract: We extend the random-matrix theory of chaotic scattering to quantum dots whose dynamics is monitored by time-resolved measurements. Starting from a scattering matrix drawn from a circular ensemble, we construct the corresponding ensemble of Kraus operators for the monitored evolution of the many-body density matrix. In the single-particle sector the sum over measurement outcomes can be carried out algebraically, giving a discrete-time quantum master equation for the transferred charge. We solve this equation numerically and compare the resulting charge-transfer statistics with closed-form random-matrix predictions. The latter rely on an equipartition rule for monitored particles, which we formulate as a conjecture and test against the master equation.

</details>

Abstract: We present a compact millikelvin scanning tunneling microscope (STM) operating at 270mK with topographic navigation to micron-scale targets. Two piezoelectric low-temperature nanopositioners extend the accessible sample area, while a multi-stage copper powder and capillary filter scheme preserves millikelvin energy resolution, verified by BCS spectroscopy on aluminium thin films. A lithographically fabricated binary-encoded gold pattern encodes unique 16-bit coordinates in 4x4 pixels of 200nm$\times$200nm each. Method: 考虑偶极相互作用（dipolar interactions）和量子交换相互作用（quantum exchange interactions），从微观角度评估CT激子之间的相互影响，并计算密度依赖的能量重整化（density-dependent energy renormalization）。
