Abstract: Lateral heterostructures of transition-metal dichalcogenides (TMDs) host spatially separated charge-transfer (CT) excitons. While analogous to interlayer excitons in vertical TMD heterostructures, these interfacial excitons possess much larger in-plane dipoles of several nanometers and an additional center-of-mass quantization. Here, we study the mutual interactions between these highly dipolar CT excitons on a microscopic footing. Accounting for the dipolar and quantum exchange interactions, we evaluate the experimentally accessible density-dependent energy renormalization and predict a net energy blueshift of a few meV for bound CT excitons. Abstract: The very strong light-matter coupling regime enables the non-perturbative modification of matter properties via light. Using a patterned GaAs/AlGaAs waveguide with twelve wide quantum wells, we demonstrate hybridization of heavy- and light-hole excitons within a single polariton state and show that, at finite magnetic field, the presence of the light-hole exciton suppresses coupling to the heavy-hole Rydberg excitons and unbound scattering states. We develop a fully microscopic theory that accounts for the combined effects of the magnetic field and light-matter coupling on the excitons, providing an accurate description of the experimental results beyond a perturbative coupled-oscillator framework. This identifies quantum well width as a key control parameter for engineering the light-induced hybridization of matter wave functions in polaritons, which, in turn, can play a crucial role in the optical non-linearities.

### [127] [Cooper quartets and fractional vortices in frustrated Josephson junction dice arrays](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04958)

Method: 采用弛豫动力学（relaxation dynamics）模拟研究该设备的临界电流，并分析体超流（bulk supercurrents）的傅里叶分解（Fourier decomposition）。通过蒙特卡洛方法（Monte Carlo techniques）和二维无限张量网络（two-dimensional infinite tensor networks）在有限温度下进一步表征系统。

Result: 在阻挫为1/3时观测到的临界电流与临界温度峰值对应一个与半涡旋（half-vortices）退禁闭（deconfinement）相容的超导-绝缘体相变（superconductor-insulator phase transition）。低温关联函数（correlation functions）证实了由Cooper四重态介导的4e超导相（4e superconducting phase）的出现。研究还考察了约瑟夫森能（Josephson energy）和通量无序（flux disorder）的影响，并评述了充电能（charging energies）在对应二维量子模型中的作用。

Conclusion: dice晶格约瑟夫森结阵列在1/3阻挫下可实现Cooper四重态介导的4e超导相，其特征可通过临界电流与关联函数的数值分析加以识别；相变由半涡旋退禁闭驱动。实验阵列中的约瑟夫森能和无序通量对物态有显著影响，充电能在二维量子模型中也扮演重要角色。

Abstract: Superconductivity mediated by Cooper quartets of charge 4e is a phenomenon of key importance for both the understanding of certain exotic superconductors and the engineering of quantum memories protected at the hardware level by topological order. Josephson junction arrays in the shape of the dice lattice constitute one of the main candidates for the realization of this phase of matter. Here, we analyze numerical signatures of the emergence of this exotic phase when superconducting dice arrays are frustrated by inserting one third of a flux quantum per rhombic plaquette. We adopt simulations of relaxation dynamics to study the critical current of such devices and analyse the Fourier decomposition of their bulk supercurrents. A further characterization of these systems at finite temperature is obtained through Monte Carlo techniques and two-dimensional infinite tensor networks. Our results indicate that the observed peaks of the critical current and temperature at frustration 1/3 correspond to a superconductor-insulator phase transition compatible with the deconfinement of half-vortices, while the low-temperature correlation functions of the model confirm the onset of a 4e superconducting phase mediated by Cooper quartets. We finally address the effects of Josephson energy and flux disorder typical of experimental arrays, and comment on the role of charging energies in the corresponding two-dimensional quantum model.

Abstract: Stimulated Raman transitions in Faraday geometry allow for simultaneous single-shot qubit readout and qubit control. Due to the simultaneous driving of both transitions with unequal detuning, the resulting time-dependent Stark shift gives rise to additional resonance conditions beyond the conventional picture. We identify a distinct regime in which repeated passages through avoided crossings lead to step-like population inversion arising from Landau-Zener-Stückelberg interference. By changing the detuning beatnote, we demonstrate a controlled continuous crossover from Rabi-like oscillations to adiabatic population switching. These findings establish the oscillating Stark shift as a mechanism for engineering and controlling spin dynamics in Faraday geometry.

Method: 研究了少层CrSBr在磁场中的光学吸收性质，测量了低场诱导铁磁序（ferromagnetic order）下共振的红移行为以及高场（至55 T）下的抗磁位移（diamagnetic shift）响应。

This behavior reportedly originates from the highly anisotropic nature of CrSBr -- particularly in its antiferromagnetic state -- where excitons are effectively confined within individual monolayers, such that excitons in the two surface layers "see" a different local dielectric environment and have a lower resonance energy. To explore this scenario, here we investigate optical absorption properties of few-layer CrSBr in magnetic fields. In addition to the fundamental exciton resonance at ~1.36eV, we observe an absorption resonance ~20 meV lower in energy. Compared to the fundamental transition, this resonance redshifts only half as much in small magnetic fields that induce ferromagnetic order, while in high fields to 55T it exhibits a smaller diamagnetic shift. Both behaviors point to distinguishable populations of bulk and surface excitons in CrSBr.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二维过渡金属硫族化合物（TMDs）中谷极化激子为量子应用提供了有前景的平台，但其可寻址性和退相干仍然是基础性挑战，亟需设计工程化的长寿命二能级系统。

Method: 发展第一性原理静电嵌入方法（first-principles electrostatic embedding approach），并结合大规模GW（Green's function and screened Coulomb interaction）加Bethe-Salpeter方程（BSE）计算，对TMD单层在铁电性扭曲双层hBN衬底上的激子行为进行从头算研究。

Result: 预言了两种相互竞争的低能激子：光学暗的电荷转移激子（charge-transfer excitons）和具有线性光学二色性（linear optical dichroism）的准一维Wannier激子（quasi-one-dimensional Wannier excitons）。Wannier激子的空间局域化结合单层TMD中的谷间交换相互作用（intervalley exchange interactions），可在无外磁场条件下使谷简并激子产生约3 meV的分裂。

Conclusion: 从头算结果阐明了界面扭曲角（interfacial twist angle）和边缘场空间局域化的作用，为在铁电衬底支撑的TMD单层中工程化设计长寿命二能级系统建立了设计规则。

Abstract: Valley-polarized excitons in two-dimensional transition metal dichalcogenides (TMDs) offer a promising platform for quantum applications, yet the addressability and decoherence of these states remain fundamental challenges. Here, by developing a first-principles electrostatic embedding approach and performing large-scale GW plus Bethe-Salpeter equation calculations, we reveal novel excitons that emerge in TMD monolayers when supported by a ferroelectric twisted bilayer hBN substrate. We predict two competing low-energy excitons whose ordering depends on the dielectric environment: optically dark, charge-transfer excitons, and quasi-one-dimensional Wannier excitons with linear optical dichroism. The spatial localization of Wannier excitons, together with intervalley exchange interactions in monolayer TMDs, splits valley-degenerate excitons by about 3~meV without external magnetic fields. Our ab initio calculations clarify the role of the interfacial twist angle and the spatial localization of fringe fields, establishing design rules for engineering long-lived two-level systems in TMD monolayers supported by ferroelectric substrates.

</details>


### [131] [Quantum Hall effect in vacancy-engineered $β$-Ag$_2$Te](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05128)
*Mizuki Ohno,Veronica Show,Reiley Dorrian,Joseph Falson*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过分子束外延（molecular beam epitaxy, MBE）生长中的原位空位工程（in-situ vacancy engineering），实现了高质量β-Ag₂Te薄膜的表面主导输运。在不借助外部栅极的情况下连续调控载流子密度穿越电荷中性点，观测到朗道能级（Landau levels）符合无质量狄拉克色散（massless Dirac dispersion）关系，并展现出ν=1的量子霍尔态（quantum Hall state）。该工作提供了一种无需光刻和栅极的通用方法，用于在拓扑绝缘体（topological insulators）薄膜中实现量子霍尔输运。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 拓扑绝缘体中的表面量子输运受限于晶格缺陷引起的体态电导（bulk conduction），亟需一种有效抑制体态载流子的材料制备方案。

Method: 在分子束外延生长过程中引入原位空位工程步骤，调控β-Ag₂Te薄膜的化学计量比，抑制施主型缺陷（donor-type defects），从而实现无外部栅极条件下跨越电荷中性点的载流子密度连续调控。

Result: 低载流子密度薄膜中观测到完全发展的ν=1量子霍尔态；跨样品的朗道能级能量符合E_N=v_F√(2eℏNB)关系，证实表面态具有无质量狄拉克费米子（massless Dirac fermion）色散特征。

Conclusion: 化学计量比驱动的空位工程是一种灵活且无需光刻与栅极的通用方法，可在外延拓扑绝缘体薄膜中实现量子霍尔输运。

Abstract: Accessing surface quantum transport in topological insulators is hampered by residual bulk conduction arising from lattice defects. Here, we demonstrate a novel synthesis pathway for realizing high mobility $β$-Ag$_2$Te thin films where surface transport is dominant. An \textit{in-situ} vacancy engineering step as part of the molecular beam epitaxy growth process acts to modify the stoichiometry and suppress donor-type defects, enabling continuous tuning of the sheet carrier density over more than an order of magnitude through the charge-neutrality point without an external gate electrode. In the lower-carrier-density films, a fully developed $ν=1$ quantum Hall state is observed, and Landau-level energies extracted across samples collapse onto the $E_N=v_\mathrm{F}\sqrt{2e\hbar NB}$ relation, providing evidence for the massless Dirac dispersion of the top and bottom surface states. These results establish stoichiometry-driven vacancy engineering as a versatile lithography- and gate-free approach to accessing quantum Hall transport in epitaxial topological-insulator thin films.

Donor-side matter accretes onto the common five-dimensional horizon, increases the horizon radius, and consequently enlarges its intersection with our brane. As a result, the gravitational mass inferred by an observer living on our brane grows. We slice the five-dimensional geometry onto each brane and show that the induced exterior on our brane has the usual Schwarzschild/Vaidya monopole form at leading order, with subleading Weyl/Kaluza-Klein corrections in the localized-feeding branch. ### [134] [Neutrino mass constraints in interacting dark energy models after DESI DR2](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05005)
*Hui Li,Guo-Hong Du,Tian-Nuo Li,Hai-Li Li,Lu Feng,Jing-Fei Zhang,Xin Zhang*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 该研究基于DESI等最新观测数据，在四种相互作用暗能量（IDE）模型下分析中微子总质量上限，发现不同模型对质量上限的约束差异显著，且某些IDE模型与地面中微子振荡实验确定的正常层级下界（~0.06 eV）之间存在加剧的统计张力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用四种不同的相互作用暗能量（interacting dark energy, IDE）模型，结合最新的DESI重子声学振荡（baryon acoustic oscillation, BAO）、宇宙微波背景（cosmic microwave background, CMB）和Ia型超新星数据集，对总中微子质量进行宇宙学上限分析。模型拟合优度评估使用Deviance Information Criterion (DIC)和Δχ²_MAP指标。

Result: 总中微子质量上限对相互作用项的具体现象学形式高度敏感：IΛCDM2模型（Q ∝ H ρ_c）显著放宽上限至∑m_ν < 0.129 eV（95%置信水平），而IΛCDM3模型（Q ∝ H_0 ρ_de）则压缩参数空间，给出高度严格的约束∑m_ν < 0.051 eV。

Conclusion: 当前观测数据在统计上更偏好这些压制中微子质量的IDE模型，这加剧了观测偏好的IDE情景与地面中微子振荡实验确定的正常层级下界（~0.06 eV）之间的统计张力。

Abstract: Recent DESI observations indicate a deviation from the $Λ$CDM model, showing a preference for dynamical dark energy and thereby relaxing the upper limit on the neutrino mass within this framework. This deviation can also be explained by the presence of an interaction between dark energy and dark matter. In this work, we investigate the cosmological upper bounds on the total neutrino mass ($\sum m_ν$) across four different interacting dark energy (IDE) models. The present analysis employs the latest DESI baryon acoustic oscillation, cosmic microwave background, and type Ia supernova datasets. These results demonstrate that the upper bounds on $\sum m_ν$ exhibit profound sensitivity to the specific phenomenological formulation of the interaction term. While the I$Λ$CDM2 model ($Q \propto H ρ_{\mathrm{c}}$) substantially relaxes the stringent upper limit ($\sum m_ν < 0.129$ eV at 95% confidence level), notably the I$Λ$CDM3 model ($Q \propto H_0 ρ_{\mathrm{de}}$), severely compresses the allowed parameter space, yielding a highly restrictive bound of $\sum m_ν < 0.051$ eV. Furthermore, rigorous goodness-of-fit evaluations utilizing the Deviance Information Criterion and $Δχ^2_{\mathrm{MAP}}$ indicate that the current observational data statistically favor these mass-suppressing IDE models. This establishes an exacerbated statistical tension between the observationally preferred IDE scenarios and the normal hierarchy lower bound ($\sim 0.06$ eV) determined by terrestrial neutrino oscillation experiments.

### [135] [First Constraints on the Ellipticities of Self-Interacting Fermionic Dark Matter Admixed Neutron Stars from Continuous Gravitational-Wave Searches](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05082)
*Premachand Mahapatra,Andrew L. Miller,Prasanta Kumar Das*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文研究了自相互作用费米子暗物质（dark matter）与快速旋转、非轴对称孤立中子星混合后产生的连续引力波（continuous gravitational wave, CW）辐射，建立了描述暗物质累积如何改变星体结构、产生“暗山”（dark mountains）以及增强引力波振幅的形式化框架，并利用LIGO O3数据首次对暗物质混合中子星的暗物质诱导椭圆率（ellipticity）施加了观测约束，同时排除了部分暗物质质量-自相互作用耦合强度参数空间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索暗物质（dark matter）与中子星混合后能否通过产生非轴对称的“暗山”（dark mountains）增强连续引力波（continuous gravitational wave, CW）辐射，并利用现有引力波观测数据对暗物质性质施加独立于传统天体物理方法的约束。

Method: 发展了一个形式化框架（formalism），描述中子星内部暗物质（dark matter）累积如何改变星体结构、暗物质各向异性分布如何产生赤道变形（暗山），以及如何增大转动惯量（moment of inertia）从而提升引力波振幅；利用LIGO O3全天空搜索数据，对暗物质混合中子星的暗物质诱导椭圆率（ellipticity）施加约束，并排除特定暗物质质量与自相互作用耦合强度（self-interaction coupling strength）参数空间区域。

Result: 基于LIGO O3数据，对于距离d=1 kpc（d=10 kpc）处、椭圆率ε=10⁻⁷（ε=10⁻⁹）的暗物质混合中子星，在暗物质质量m_χ∈[0.1,10] GeV范围内，最佳（最差）情况下排除耦合强度g≳10⁻⁵·⁵（g≳10⁻⁴）；下一代探测器（如爱因斯坦望远镜Einstein Telescope和宇宙探索者Cosmic Explorer）可将排除范围拓展至g≳10⁻⁶（对于d=10 kpc、ε=10⁻⁷的中子星）。

Conclusion: 连续引力波（continuous gravitational wave, CW）搜索为直接探测由暗物质混合中子星维持的“暗山”（dark mountains）提供了天然途径，暗物质的存在可显著增强中子星的引力波信号，从而将引力波观测转化为暗物质性质的有效探针。

Abstract: We investigate continuous gravitational-wave (CW) emission from rapidly rotating, non-axisymmetric, isolated neutron stars admixed with self-interacting fermionic dark matter (DM) and hosting DM-induced equatorial deformations (``dark mountains''). In particular, we develop a formalism that describes how DM accumulation inside the star changes its structure, how dark mountains arise from an anisotropic distribution of DM inside it, and how the star's moment of inertia and thus the amplitude of its GW emission is increased compared to that of an ordinary neutron star. Moreover, using results from all-sky searches for CWs from non-axisymmetric neutron stars performed with LIGO O3 data, we place the first constraints on the DM-induced ellipticities $\varepsilon$ of DM-admixed neutron stars across the full GW frequency range analyzed by LIGO and for a range of self-interaction strengths. With the same data, we also exclude portions of the DM-mass/self-interaction coupling strength parameter space that would have produced detectable GW signals in LIGO O3 data. We rule out at best (at worst) couplings $g\gtrsim10^{-5.5}$ ($g\gtrsim 10^{-4}$) for DM-admixed neutron stars with ellipticities $\varepsilon=10^{-7}$ ($\varepsilon=10^{-9}$) at distances $d=1$ ($d=10$) kpc away for DM masses of $m_χ\in[0.1,10]$ GeV. Furthermore, we show that even larger regions of this parameter space will become accessible to next-generation detectors, such as Einstein Telescope and Cosmic Explorer, with exclusions as strong as $g\gtrsim10^{-6}$ for neutron stars located $d=10$ kpc away for $\varepsilon=10^{-7}$. Our results demonstrate that searches for CWs naturally provide a direct probe of dark mountains sustained by DM-admixed neutron stars.

### [136] [Influence of anisotropy on the expansion performance of auxetic skin meshing geometries: a finite element study](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04893)
*Masoumeh Razaghi Pey Ghaleh,Denis O'Mahoney,Kevin Moerman*

Main category: physics.med-ph

TL;DR: 本研究通过有限元建模分析了各向异性（anisotropy）与拉胀网格（auxetic mesh）几何结构对皮肤移植扩张性能的联合影响，发现各向异性显著且复杂地调控扩张行为，且各向同性模型会高估应力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有皮肤移植扩张研究多采用各向同性假设，忽略了皮肤自身各向异性（如兰格线（Langer's lines））与拉胀网格几何结构的交互作用，因此需要系统评估该联合效应对扩张性能的影响。

Method: 基于狭缝型拉胀几何（auxetic slit-based geometries）建立有限元模型，施加25%拉伸应变；皮肤采用各向异性本构方程（anisotropic constitutive formulation）建模，并改变兰格线相对于载荷方向的角度。

Result: 各向异性显著影响扩张行为，且该效应复杂、高度依赖于网格类型；各向异性既可增强也可抑制拉胀扩张行为。在所有网格类型中，兰格线与横向对齐时扩张性能最低，接近载荷方向时扩张最大。各向同性模型相较于各向异性模型会高估应力。

Conclusion: 拉胀结构可用于皮肤网格扩张应用，且各向异性是变形与应力预测中的重要因素。

Abstract: This study investigates the combined effects of anisotropy and auxetic mesh geometry on the performance of skin graft expansion. Finite element models of auxetic slit-based geometries were developed and subjected to 25 percent tensile strain. Skin was modelled using an anisotropic constitutive formulation. Langer's line orientations were varied relative to the load direction. Results showed anisotropy strongly influenced expansion behaviour. The effect was observed to be complex and highly dependent on mesh type. Anisotropy was observed to enhance or inhibit the auxetic expansion behaviour. In all mesh types studied, the expansion performance is lowest when Langer's lines align with the transverse direction. Greatest expansion was typically observed when Langer's lines were close to the loading direction. Isotropic models overpredicted stress relative to the anisotropic models. These findings support the use of auxetic structures for skin mesh expansion applications and show that anisotropy is an important factor in both deformation and stress prediction.

### [137] [CaloTrilogy: Toward a Breakthrough in One-Step, End-to-End, Physics-Guided Shower Generation for Modern Calorimeters](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04165)
*Cheng Jiang,Sitian Qian,Kevin Pedro,Oz Amram,Huilin Qu,Maggie Voetberg*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种统一的快速模拟框架，通过平均速度场积分器、数据驱动的生成先验和物理引导的损失项，在仅需一到几步推理的情况下实现与最先进流匹配和扩散模型相当的量热器簇射模拟质量，同时保持端到端推理的高效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高精度量热器模拟（calorimeter simulation）在现有和未来对撞机实验中计算需求快速增长，促使开发机器学习替代方法以加速传统的蒙特卡洛工具（如Geant4）。现有流匹配（flow matching）和扩散模型虽然样本质量高，但推理时需要约上百次函数评估，且常依赖辅助网络约束全局可观测量，难以实现精简的端到端生成。

Method: 方法包含三个核心组件：(i) 平均速度场积分器（average velocity field integrator），支持单步或少数几步采样；(ii) 从数据而非随机噪声构建的簇射空间生成先验（learned generative prior）；(iii) 物理引导的损失项（physics-guided loss terms），在训练时对关键可观测量施加归纳偏置（inductive biases）。这些元素作为训练时正则化器，不增加推理额外成本。

Result: 在多个公开的高粒度量热器数据集上测试，仅需一步或少量评估步骤，模型即可达到与最先进流匹配和扩散方法相当的簇射质量（shower quality）。结果展示了与底层物理一致的层间簇射结构（inter-layer shower structure）。

Conclusion: 该方法为未来快速模拟工作流程提供了有力候选方案，在速度、簇射质量和物理保真度之间实现了更好的平衡。

Abstract: High-precision calorimeter simulation at current and future colliders imposes rapidly growing computational demands, motivating the development of machine-learning surrogates for traditional Monte Carlo tools such as Geant4. Flow matching and diffusion-based generative models have become leading approaches for high-dimensional fast simulation because of their sample quality, but typically require ${\cal O}(100)$ function evaluations at inference and often rely on auxiliary networks to constrain global observables, compromising streamlined end-to-end generation. We introduce a unified framework that improves the balance between speed, shower quality, and physics fidelity. The method combines: (i) an average velocity field integrator that enables sampling in one or a few evaluations; (ii) a learned generative prior in shower space, constructed from data rather than random noise; and (iii) physics-guided loss terms that impose inductive biases on key observables during training. These elements are training time regularizers, preserving end-to-end inference with no additional cost. With only one or a few evaluation steps, the model achieves shower quality competitive with state-of-the-art flow and diffusion approaches, tested on several public high granularity calorimeter datasets. The results demonstrate inter-layer shower structure consistent with the underlying physics, providing a strong candidate for future fast simulation workflows.

</details>

Zani,F. Zeng,M. Zeyrek,B. Zhang,X. Zhao,V. Zhilich,Q. D. Zhou,X. Y. Zhou,L. Zhu,R. Žlebčík*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文基于Belle和Belle II实验采集的约772×10⁶和521×10⁶个Υ(4S)衰变事例，测量了B⁰→K_S⁰π⁰γ衰变中的时间依赖CP破坏参数。在K*⁰(892)主导区域联合数据集的测量结果为S=0.09±0.16±0.02、C=-0.09±0.08±0.04；非K*⁰(892)区域结果为S=-0.32±0.33±0.09、C=-0.07±0.17±0.08。结果与标准模型预言一致，且精度优于以往测量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: B⁰→K_S⁰π⁰γ衰变是研究时间依赖CP破坏（time-dependent CP violation）的理想过程，可为检验标准模型（Standard Model）的CKM（Cabibbo-Kobayashi-Maskawa）机制提供精确约束。此前对该衰变道的CP破坏参数测量精度有限，需利用更大统计量的实验数据以提高测量精度。

Method: 利用Belle（约772×10⁶个Υ(4S)衰变）和Belle II（约521×10⁶个Υ(4S)衰变）实验的联合数据样本，对B⁰→K_S⁰π⁰γ衰变进行时间依赖CP破坏参数测量。根据K_S⁰π⁰不变质量将数据分为K*⁰(892)主导区域（M∈[0.8,1.0]GeV/c²）和非K*⁰(892)区域（M∈[1.0,1.8]GeV/c²）分别进行分析。

Result: 在K*⁰(892)主导区域，联合数据集的CP破坏参数为S=0.09±0.16(stat)±0.02(syst)、C=-0.09±0.08(stat)±0.04(syst)；在非K*⁰(892)区域，结果为S=-0.32±0.33(stat)±0.09(syst)、C=-0.07±0.17(stat)±0.08(syst)。

Conclusion: 所有测量结果与标准模型预言在误差范围内一致，且精度优于此前对该衰变道的测量结果，为检验CP破坏机制提供了更严格的实验约束。

Abstract: We perform a measurement of time-dependent $CP$ violation parameters in $B^{0} \to K_{S}^{0} π^{0} γ$ decays using a dataset of approximately $772 \times 10^6$ and $521 \times 10^6$ $Υ(4S)$ decays collected by the Belle and Belle II experiments, respectively. The measured parameters for the combined dataset in the $K^{*0}(892)$ dominated region ($M_{K_{S}^{0} π^{0}} \in [0.8,1.0] \mathrm{GeV}/c^2$) are $S = 0.09 \pm 0.16 \pm 0.02$ and $C = -0.09 \pm 0.08 \pm 0.04$. For the non-$K^{*0}(892)$ region ($M_{K_{S}^{0} π^{0}} \in [1.0,1.8] \mathrm{GeV}/c^2$), the corresponding values are $S = -0.32 \pm 0.33 \pm 0.09$ and $C = -0.07 \pm 0.17 \pm 0.08$. The first quoted uncertainties are statistical, while the second ones are systematic. These results are consistent with Standard Model predictions and more precise than previous measurements.

</details>


### [139] [Archi: Agentic Operations at the CMS Experiment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04755)
*Pietro Lugato,Luca Lavezzo,Jason Mohoney,Hasan Ozturk,Muhammad Hassan Ahmed,Juan Pablo Salas,Viphava Ohm,Krittin Phornsiricharoenphant,Gabriele Benelli,Mariarosaria D'Alfonso,Manasvita Joshi,Warren Nam,Aron Soha,Samantha Sunnarborg,Austin Swinney,Jack Tucker,Dmytro Kovalskyi,Tim Kraska,Christoph Paus*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文提出Archi，一个面向科学合作的开源端到端框架，集成了异构数据源的系统化摄取与组织，以及可配置、私有、可扩展的智能体（agent）部署。该系统已部署于CERN LHC的CMS实验计算运维团队，通过结合文档、历史数据和实时监控系统提供检索与分析能力。评估表明，系统在真实运维问题中表现有效，且本地托管的开源权重模型（open-weight model）具有竞争力，能够实现对敏感数据的完全私有化管理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 科学合作中涉及大量异构数据源，现有工具难以在保护数据隐私的同时实现高效检索与推理。Archi旨在提供一个端到端、开源且可私有化部署的框架，解决数据组织与智能体部署之间的整合问题。

Method: Archi框架包含两大核心组件：一是对异构数据源进行系统性摄取与组织的模块；二是部署可配置、私有且可扩展的智能体（agent），用于对数据进行检索与推理。系统以CMS实验计算运维团队为应用场景，整合文档、历史数据与实时监控系统。

Result: 系统基于运维人员反馈和来自生产环境的问题集进行评估，由人工和自动化评审组共同评分。结果表明Archi能有效解决CMS运维人员提出的真实问题。此外，本地托管的开源权重模型（open-weight model）表现与专有模型相当，支持敏感数据的完全私有化管理。

Conclusion: Archi在科学合作的数据管理与智能问答场景中展现了有效性，并验证了开源权重模型（open-weight model）在敏感数据处理场景中的竞争力，为未来科学计算运维的私有化智能系统提供了可行方案。

Abstract: We present Archi, an open-source, end-to-end framework for scientific collaborations that combines the systematic ingestion and organization of heterogeneous data sources with the deployment of configurable, private, and extensible agents that retrieve and reason over them. An instance of Archi has been deployed for the Computing Operations team of the CMS experiment at CERN's LHC since February 2026 as a support agent for technical operators, offering retrieval and analysis capabilities by combining documentation, historical data, and live monitoring systems. We evaluate the system on operator feedback and a question set collected from production usage, graded by human and automated panels. The system proves effective at operational tasks, resolving real-world queries posed by CMS operators. We also observe that locally-hosted, open-weight models perform competitively, enabling fully private management of sensitive data.

</details>


### [140] [Probing Nucleon Spin Structure with a Polarized Gamma Beam from Compton Backscattering at FCC-ee](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04805)
*A. C. Canbay,S. Sultansoy,F. Zimmermann*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于康普顿背散射（Compton backscattering, CBS）的高能极化伽马射线设施设计方案，利用FCC-ee电子束寄生运行，可产生能量高达148 GeV的极化光子，并通过对NH₃极化靶的开粲光生过程，将极化胶子分布Δg(x)的测量精度提升至现有最佳世界测量值（HERMES）不确定度的1/4至1/7。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有极化胶子分布Δg(x)的测量精度受限于统计量和蒙特卡洛模型不确定性，尤其是在中等x区域（0.07≤x≤0.19）缺乏高精度约束。本文旨在通过高能量、高极化的伽马射线束，为Δg(x)提供显著优于现有测量的约束。

Method: 该设施基于激光与FCC-ee电子束（运行在Z、WW、ZH和t\bar{t}模式）的康普顿背散射，转换点位于FCC-ee全能量增强环（booster）中，无需专用对撞点光学系统，实现寄生运行。每个模式中运动学参数κ固定为安全值4.35，以此确定激光波长。极化光子通过配对谱仪（pair spectrometer）逐事件选取，在高能康普顿边缘重建光子能量E_γ，实现圆偏振度|\langle S_{2}\rangle|>0.99。灵敏度分析基于开粲光生过程γp→c\bar{c}X作用于NH₃动态核极化（dynamic-nuclear-polarization）靶，引入次领头阶（next-to-leading-order, NLO）QCD修正的K因子，并通过NNPDFpol2.0的100个蒙特卡洛副本传播极化部分子分布函数（polarized-PDF）不确定性。

Result: 在Compton分数f_{CBS}=10^{-8}（每束团交叉）的寄生模式下，运行激光脉冲能量处于毫焦耳量级，不损失FCC-ee标称亮度。在中等x区域四个不同⟨x⟩值上，Δg(x)/g(x)的总投影精度δ(Δg/g)_{tot}约为1.8–3.0×10^{-2}，比HERMES（目前最精确的直接世界测量）的总不确定度小约4–7倍。

Conclusion: 该设施将在中等x区域为极化胶子分布提供主导性约束，与电子-离子对撞机（Electron–Ion Collider, EIC）在低x区域的覆盖形成互补。

Abstract: We present a kinematic and optical design of a high-energy polarized gamma-ray facility based on Compton backscattering of lasers against the FCC-ee electron beams in its $Z$, $WW$, $ZH$ and $t\bar{t}$ modes. The conversion point is located in the FCC-ee full-energy booster, allowing parasitic CBS operation without dedicated interaction-point optics. Saturating the safe value of the kinematic parameter $κ= 4.35$ in each mode fixes the laser wavelength and yields backscattered photons up to $ω_{\max} = 148$~GeV. The facility operates in a parasitic mode with Compton fraction $f_{\rm CBS} = 10^{-8}$ per bunch crossing, preserving the nominal FCC-ee collider luminosity; the corresponding operational laser pulse energies are in the millijoule range. Polarized photon selection is performed event-by-event via a pair spectrometer that reconstructs $E_γ$ on the high-energy Compton edge, delivering circular polarization $|\langle S_{2}\rangle| > 0.99$. We project the resulting sensitivity to the polarized gluon distribution $Δg(x)$ through open-charm photoproduction $γp \to c\bar{c}X$ on an NH$_{3}$ dynamic-nuclear-polarization target, including next-to-leading-order QCD corrections via $K$-factors and propagating polarized-PDF uncertainties through the $100$ Monte Carlo replicas of NNPDFpol2.0. The projected total precision on $Δg(x)/g(x)$ is $δ(Δg/g)_{\rm tot}\simeq 1.8$--$3.0\times 10^{-2}$, a factor of $\sim 4$--$7$ smaller than the total uncertainty of the most precise existing direct world measurement (HERMES, dominated by Monte-Carlo model uncertainties), with four distinct values of $\langle x\rangle$ in the medium-$x$ region $0.07\leq x\leq 0.19$. The proposed facility would set the dominant constraint on the polarized gluon distribution in the medium-$x$ region, complementary to the low-$x$ reach of the Electron--Ion Collider.

</details>


### [141] [Software compensation of hadronic showers in the longitudinally segmented CRILIN Cherenkov crystal calorimeter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05111)
*V. Ciccarella,E. Di Meco,R. Gargiulo,L. Sestini,I. Sarra*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文研究针对CRILIN（一种基于PbF₂晶体的纵向分段式切伦科夫晶体电磁量能器）的软件补偿技术，通过Geant4模拟π介子簇射，利用基于簇射形状的修正和ParticleNet图神经网络（Graph Neural Network, GNN）充分重建三维簇射拓扑，显著提升了强子能量重建性能，使得晶體量能器在非补偿响应条件下仍能实现优异的电磁-强子联合能量分辨率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 未来正负电子希格斯工厂（Higgs factory）需要优异的喷注能量分辨率（jet energy resolution）来精确测量希格斯玻色子与夸克及胶子的耦合强度。然而，均匀晶体量能器虽具有出色的电磁能量分辨率，但其强烈的非补偿响应（non-compensating response）使得强子能量重建极具挑战性。

Method: 基于Geant4模拟π介子簇射，首先分析簇射形状观测量（shower-shape observables）与CRILIN模块中沉积能量重建分数的相关性，提出基于簇射横向均方根（transverse RMS）和纵向重心（longitudinal center-of-gravity）的逐事例修正；进一步采用ParticleNet图神经网络（ParticleNet Graph Neural Network）充分利用完整的三维簇射拓扑信息进行重建。

Result: 简单基于簇射形状的逐事例修正已能显著改善强子能量重建；GNN方法在性能上明显优于简单能量求和重建。在考虑下游强子量能器（hadronic calorimeter, HCAL）的实际假设下，基于GNN的重建将CRILIN对联合量能器分辨率的有效贡献降低至约$(1 ~\mathrm{GeV}/E \, \oplus \, 12\%/\sqrt{E[\mathrm{GeV}]}\,\oplus\,2.5\%)$，保持了优异的ECAL+HCAL联合性能。该结果对假设的HCAL分辨率的依赖在考察范围内有限。

Conclusion: 高颗粒度晶体量能器能够通过基于软件的补偿技术（software compensation techniques）在很大程度上恢复因非补偿响应而损失的信息，在联合电磁-强子量能器系统中实现对强子的优异能量分辨率，使其成为未来对撞机实验的有前景的选择。

Abstract: Future electron-positron Higgs factories require excellent jet energy resolution to perform precision measurements of Higgs boson couplings to quarks and gluons. Although homogeneous crystal calorimeters provide remarkable electromagnetic energy resolution, their strongly non-compensating response makes hadronic energy reconstruction particularly challenging. In this work, software compensation techniques are investigated for CRILIN, a longitudinally segmented Cherenkov crystal electromagnetic calorimeter based on PbF$_2$ crystals.
  Using Geant4 simulations of pion showers, it is shown that shower-shape observables are strongly correlated with the fraction of deposited energy reconstructed in a CRILIN module. Simple event-by-event corrections based on the shower transverse RMS and longitudinal center-of-gravity already yield a substantial improvement in hadronic energy reconstruction. A ParticleNet Graph Neural Network exploiting the full three-dimensional shower topology achieves significantly improved performance with respect to simple energy sum reconstruction. Under realistic assumptions for the downstream hadronic calorimeter, the GNN-based reconstruction reduces the effective CRILIN contribution to the combined calorimetric resolution to approximately $(1 ~\mathrm{GeV}/E \, \oplus \, 12\%/\sqrt{E[\mathrm{GeV}]}\,\oplus\,2.5\%)$, therefore preserving an excellent combined ECAL+HCAL performance. The dependence of the result on the assumed HCAL resolution is also studied and found to be limited within the range considered. These results show that highly granular crystal calorimeters can recover a large fraction of the information lost because of their non-compensating response through software-based compensation techniques, achieving an excellent energy resolution on hadrons in a combined ECAL+HCAL system, making them promising options for future collider experiments.

</details>

# cs.LG [[Back]](#toc)

### [142] [Shortcomings and capacities of real-constrained neural networks in complex spaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04390)
*Andrew Gracyk*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了在复杂假设类（complex hypothesis class）中，施加实数预激活（real pre-activations）与复数预激活（complex pre-activations）时，存储容量（storage capacity）之间的渐近比率（asymptotic ratio）。证明依赖于Harish-Chandra-Itzykson-Zuber (HCIZ)公式，并结合Weyl积分公式（Weyl integration formula）与Haar测度（Haar measure）在紧致流形（compact manifolds）上的积分，获得了更鲁棒的渐近比率近似。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为理解在复假设类中施加实值约束对存储容量的影响，作者希望确定实预激活与复预激活条件下存储容量之间的渐近比率，从而在临界容量（critical capacity）下比较两种假设类。

Method: 采用Gardner容量比较方法，在临界容量下进行体积比较；应用Harish-Chandra-Itzykson-Zuber (HCIZ)公式，并通过Weyl积分公式与Haar测度在酉群（unitary group）和正交群（orthogonal group）对应的紧致流形上进行积分，从而获得更鲁棒的渐近比率近似。

Result: 获得了在复假设类中，施加实数预激活与复数预激活时存储容量之间的渐近比率。

Conclusion: HCIZ公式在紧致流形上的积分处理为存储比率提供了更鲁棒的渐近近似，该策略对同类问题具有适用性。

Abstract: We find the asymptotic ratio between the storage capacities when enforcing real pre-activations in a complex hypothesis class as opposed to complex ones in the same class. Our methods depend on Gardner volume comparisons at critical capacity. Our proof relies on an application of the Harish-Chandra-Itzykson-Zuber (HCIZ) formula, nonstandard in literature. With the HCIZ formula, we may obtain a more robust approximation for the final asymptotic ratio. This strategy is applicable to our work specifically since we integrate over the unitary and orthogonal compact manifolds, facilitated via the Weyl integration formula and the Haar measure.

</details>
